# 機械安裝施工手冊 Mechanical erection manual

Heat Recovery Steam Generator with horizontal gas flow, 3 pressure with HP benson once through section 
熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 採水平煙氣流向，三壓含高壓 Benson 直流式區段  

Non-pressure parts and pressure parts 
非受壓件與受壓件

# 2. 通則 GENERAL

This erection manual covers the field installation of the two Heat Recovery Steam Generator (HRSG) for the Sun Ba Phase II CCPP project in Taiwan. 
本安裝施工手冊涵蓋台灣森霸電力二期複循環電廠專案中，兩部熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的現場施工作業。 

The Heat Recovery Steam Generator is located downstream a Siemens SGEN6-9000HL natural gas fired turbine and consists of a natural circulation, triple pressure with reheat unit, of which the high pressure section is a once through Benson system. 
本熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 位於西門子 SGEN6-9000HL 天然氣氣渦輪機的下游，由自然循環、三壓再熱單元組成，其中高壓區段採用 Benson 直流式系統。 

The HRSG shall be constructed in accordance with ASME 1, ASME B31.1. 
本熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的建造應符合 ASME Section I 及 ASME B31.1 之規範要求。 

Construction per these standards shall be defined to include, but not limited to, material selection, design, fabrication, examination, inspection testing, certification and pressure relief. 
依據上述標準進行之建造，其定義應包括但不限於：材料選用、設計、製造、檢驗、檢測測試、認證及壓力釋放裝置。 

Boilers are to be ASME stamped. 
鍋爐均須取得 ASME 鋼印認證。 

This manual describes the mechanical site installation of the HRSG, covering non-pressure and pressure parts. 
本手冊說明熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的現場機械安裝施工，內容涵蓋非受壓件與受壓件。 

The document describes the lay-out and set-up of the HRSG and provides description and guidance on how the HRSG components can be installed at the construction site. The reader must note that the document cannot be used for commercial purposes or scope description. 
本文件說明熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的配置與組裝，並針對如何在施工現場安裝各項 HRSG 組件提供說明與指引。讀者須注意，本文件不得用於商業用途或工作範圍之說明。 

Alternative erection and/or sequences are possible; however, the erection contractor shall consult with, and obtain written approval from the manufacturer prior to commencing with the chosen alternative installation and/or sequence. 
亦可採用其他替代的吊裝架設方案及/或安裝順序；然而，安裝施工承攬商在開始執行所選的替代安裝及/或順序之前，應先諮詢原廠並取得其書面同意。 

This erection manual shall in no way relieve the erection contractor from its responsibility to comply with local law and requirements, as well as construction code and project specific requirements. 
本安裝施工手冊絕不免除安裝施工承攬商遵守當地法律與法規要求、建造規範以及專案特定要求的責任。

# 4. 熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 說明 HRSG DESCRIPTION

Flue gas entrance for the HRSG scope is at the inlet duct. Gas turbine flue gasses enter the HRSG transition-duct and inlet-duct in horizontal direction. The boiler-duct contains the vertically positioned harps with inlet and outlet headers and interconnecting piping. The HRSG is divided into six boxes with an A.I.G. / SCR section in between box two and three. Each box is divided in three gas paths: left harp module, center harp module and a right harp module. Flue gasses exit the boiler through the outlet-duct and stack. 
熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 範圍的煙氣入口位於入口煙道。氣渦輪機的煙氣以水平方向進入 HRSG 的過渡煙道與入口煙道。鍋爐煙道內含有垂直配置的管排 (Harps)，並配有進出口集管箱 (Header) 及連接管路。HRSG 共分為六個箱體 (Boxes)，在第二與第三箱體之間設有氨氣注入網格系統 (AIG) / 選擇性觸媒還原脫硝系統 (SCR) 區段。每個箱體分為三個煙氣通道：左側管排模組、中間管排模組與右側管排模組。煙氣經由出口煙道與排煙煙囪排出鍋爐。 

From hot to cold side of the HRSG, the location of the bundle harps are as follows: 
自 HRSG 的高溫側至低溫側，管束管排的配置位置如下： 

- Box 1 - Harps HP / RH Super heater 
- Box 1 - 高壓 / 再熱過熱器管排 

- Box 2 - Harps HP Evaporator / Separator vessel 
- Box 2 - 高壓蒸發器管排 / 汽水分離器 

- A.I.G. / SCR box 
- A.I.G. / SCR 箱體 

- Box 3 - Harps HP Economizer / IP Super heater 
- Box 3 - 高壓省煤器 / 中壓過熱器管排 

- Box 4 - Harps HP Economizer / IRAC Econ / IP Evaporator 
- Box 4 - 高壓省煤器 / 汽機抽汽冷卻省煤器 (IRAC Econ) / 中壓蒸發器管排 

- Box 5 - Harps LP Super heater / IP Economizer / HP Economizer / LP Evaporator 
- Box 5 - 低壓過熱器 / 中壓省煤器 / 高壓省煤器 / 低壓蒸發器管排 

- Box 6 - Harps Condensate Preheater Economizer 
- Box 6 - 凝結水預熱省煤器管排 

The HRSG consists of the following main components; 
HRSG 由以下主要組件組成： 

## 4.1. 非受壓件 Non – pressure parts

Transition duct and Inlet duct Boiler Main steel Boiler casing Internal insulation including liner sheeting Boiler bumpers and sealing plates Boiler baffles 
過渡煙道與入口煙道、鍋爐主鋼結構、爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing)、含不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 的內部保溫、鍋爐防震擋塊與密封板、鍋爐煙氣導流板 

Outlet duct 
出口煙道 

Stack including stack damper Flue gas silencers stack Secondary steel Pipe supports Expansion bellows External insulation (piping only) AIG and SCR system 
排煙煙囪（含煙囪擋風門）、煙囪煙氣消音器、二次鋼結構（扶手平台樓梯）、管路支撐架、波紋伸縮接頭、外部保溫（僅限管路）、AIG 與 SCR 系統 

Equipment Noise cancelling Shroud 
設備隔音罩 

## 4.2. 受壓件 Pressure parts

Drums and Tank Separator vessel Bundles 
汽鼓 (Steam Drum) 與槽體、汽水分離器、管束 

Piping Piping appendages Equipment 
蒸汽管路、管路附件、設備 

# 5. 專案規範、技術規格書及當地法律與法規之要求 REQUIREMENTS BY PROJECT CODE(S), SPECIFICATIONS and LOCAL LAW AND REGULATIONS

## 5.1. 職責 Responsibilities

The erection works are not in the scope of supply of Manufacturer (delivery only contract). Manufacturer is not the party responsible for the erection works (quality, progress, etc.) 
安裝施工工程不屬於原廠的供應範圍（本合約僅限設備交貨）。原廠並非安裝施工工程（品質、進度等）的負責方。 

If applicable, a Technical Field Advisor (TFA) can be provided by Manufacturer to assist the erection works. As required this TFA can give advice on the best and most expeditious method of erection of the components. If required, documents can be explained. 
若適用，原廠可提供技術現場顧問 (TFA) 以協助安裝施工。該 TFA 可根據需要，針對組件的最佳且最快速的吊裝架設方法提供建議。如有需要，亦可對文件進行說明。 

This erection manual shall in no way relieve the Erection Contractor from its responsibility to comply with local law and requirements, as well as construction code and project specific requirements. It is mandatory that the erection works shall be done by skilled and qualified personnel, who shall be capable of following and assessing the instructions as described in this manual. 
本安裝施工手冊絕不免除安裝施工承攬商遵守當地法律與法規要求、建造規範以及專案特定要求的責任。安裝施工工程必須由具備技術且合格的人員執行，且該等人員應有能力遵循並評估本手冊中所述之說明。 

## 5.2. 受壓件 Pressure Parts

The design and manufacturing of the pressure parts of the HRSG is in accordance with the requirements of ASME section I edition 2019, ASME BPVC Section I edition 2019, ASME B31.1 edition 2018 and ASME VIII – div. 1 edition 2019 and also complies with the project specific requirements. 
HRSG 受壓件之設計與製造符合 ASME Section I（2019年版）、ASME BPVC Section I（2019年版）、ASME B31.1（2018年版）及 ASME VIII - Div. 1（2019年版）之要求，且亦符合專案之特定要求。 

## 5.3. 非受壓件 Non-Pressure Parts

The design and manufacturing of the Non pressure parts of the HRSG is in accordance with the requirements of AWS D1.1 Ed. 2020 and project specific requirements. 
HRSG 非受壓件之設計與製造符合 AWS D1.1（2020年版）之要求及專案特定要求。 

## 5.4. 安裝施工承攬商 Erection Contractor

The erection contractor shall make itself familiar with the situation on site and with all requirements by project code, project specifications and standards, local law and regulations and the content of this manual and Manufacturer erection documentation. 
安裝施工承攬商應熟悉現場狀況，以及專案規範、專案技術規格書與標準、當地法律與法規之所有要求，並熟悉本手冊及原廠安裝施工文件的內容。 

The erection contractor shall comply with and execute the works in accordance with the applicable requirements resulting from the aforementioned documents. 
安裝施工承攬商應遵守上述文件所產生的適用要求，並據以執行工程。 

The erection contractor shall provide sufficient and adequately skilled labour as well as suitable machinery, equipment, tools, materials and consumables to execute the installation works. 
安裝施工承攬商應提供充足且具備適當技術的勞工，以及合適的機械、設備、工具、材料與耗材，以執行施工作業。 

### 5.4.1. 職業安全衛生與環境 (環安衛) 計畫 Health, Safety and Environmental Plan

The erection contractor shall use a Health Safety and Environmental Plan, which includes Work Method Statements (WMS), in accordance with the project requirements before start of the installation work. 
安裝施工承攬商在開始施工作業前，應依據專案要求採用一份包含施工計畫書 (WMS) 的職業安全衛生與環境 (環安衛) 計畫。 

The plan shall at least cover the following items : 
該計畫應至少涵蓋以下項目： 

- Erection contractor organogram 
- 安裝施工承攬商組織圖 

- Description of the responsibilities and duties of the erection contractor personnel on site 
- 安裝施工承攬商現場人員的職責與義務說明 

- Emergency procedures and standards 
- 緊急應變程序與標準 

- Inspections, meetings and toolbox event schedule 
- 檢驗、會議及工具箱會議 (Toolbox) 時程表 

- Work Method Statements (including lifting plans) 
- 施工計畫書（包括吊裝計畫） 

The following measures shall be taken : 
應採取以下措施： 

- A team of Safety officers present on site matching the contract size. 
- 現場配置與合約規模相符的安全官 (工安人員) 團隊。 

- Proper use and availability of the necessary personnel protection equipment and first aid provisions. 
- 正確使用並提供必要的個人防護裝備 (PPE) 與急救設施。 

- Frequent Toolbox meetings (minimum once every week) covering actual work e.g. scaffolding, lifting, personnel protection, etc. 
- 頻繁召開工具箱會議（每週至少一次），內容涵蓋實際工作，例如鷹架搭設、吊裝作業、個人防護等。 

- Create overall awareness and knowledge of the HSE plan content, amongst the workforce. 
- 在全體施工人員中建立對環安衛計畫內容的整體意識與認知。 

- Proper House keeping 
- 做好現場環境整理整頓 (Housekeeping) 

### 5.4.2. 施工品質計畫 FQPs

The erection contractor shall follow the FQP’s as prepared by Manufacturer for all site installation works. 
安裝施工承攬商在進行所有現場施工作業時，應遵循原廠所編製的施工品質計畫。 

These shall as a minimum be divided into, but not limited to: 
這些計畫至少應劃分為（但不限於）以下各項： 

#### 非受壓件 Non – Pressure Parts

The following inspections shall be part (minimum) of above mentioned document: 
以下檢驗應（至少）作為上述文件的一部分： 

- Foundation height and position of the centerline, anchor positions and base plate elevation. 
- 爐座基礎高度與中心線位置、錨栓位置及基板 (Base plate) 高程。 

- Alignment of the main steel. 
- 主鋼結構之對心調整。 

- Inspection on all main steel welds (if applicable). 
- 所有主鋼結構銲縫之檢驗（若適用）。 

- Inspection on all the boiler casing external welds. 
- 所有爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 外部銲縫之檢驗。 

- Inspection of all the inlet duct internal / external welds. 
- 所有入口煙道內部/外部銲縫之檢驗。 

- Torque after tensioning of bolting main steel and secondary steel. 
- 主鋼結構與二次鋼結構（扶手平台樓梯）螺栓張拉後之扭力檢查。 

- Torque after tensioning of the anchor bolts. 
- 錨栓張拉後之扭力檢查。 

- Inspection of the internal insulation and liner sheeting. 
- 內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 之檢驗。 

- Inspection of sealing plate and baffle tolerances. 
- 密封板與煙氣導流板公差之檢驗。 

- Position and verticality of the stack. 
- 排煙煙囪的位置與垂直度。 

- Alignment flange connection GT duct with Boiler inlet duct. 
- 氣渦輪機 (GT) 煙道與鍋爐入口煙道法蘭連接處之對心調整。 

#### 受壓件 Pressure Parts

- Pressure parts installation by the requirements as per contract 
- 依據合約要求進行受壓件安裝 

- Pressure parts documentation by the requirements as per contract 
- 依據合約要求提供受壓件文件 

- Drums setting, elevation and horizontality. 
- 汽鼓 (Steam Drum) 的定位、高程與水平度。 

- Hydrostatic testing 
- 水壓試驗 

It is the erection contractor’s responsibility to carry out sufficient inspections in order to guarantee that the installation of the HRSG is performed in accordance with the requirements. 
安裝施工承攬商有責任進行充分的檢驗，以確保熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的安裝符合各項要求。 

### 5.4.3. 施工計畫書 / 工法說明書 (WMS) WMS (work method statements)

The erection contractor shall prepare WMSs for all site erection works. 
安裝施工承攬商應針對所有現場安裝施工工程編製施工計畫書 (WMS)。 

It is the erection contractor’s responsibility to carry out sufficient inspections in order to guarantee that the erection of the HRSG is performed in accordance with the requirements. 
安裝施工承攬商有責任進行充分的檢驗，以確保熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的吊裝架設符合各項要求。 

### 5.4.4. 圖面 Drawings

The erection contractor shall keep a record of all the drawing mark-ups and deviations and indicate the "as built" status on each drawing upon completion of the installation work. 
安裝施工承攬商應記錄所有圖面的紅線標註與偏差，並在施工作業完成後，於每張圖面上標示「竣工 (As-built)」狀態。 

### 5.4.5. 銲接作業 Welding

Quality (control) is the responsibility of the erection contractor. All work executed by the erection contractor shall be of first class, good workmanship and in accordance with the requirements. 
品質管制（QC）為安裝施工承攬商之職責。承攬商所執行之所有工作皆應具備一流且優良之施工技術，並完全符合各項規範要求。

Welding typicals shall be prepared to facilitate the review of welding documents. The welding typical will address all joint configurations applicable to the project with cross reference to the selected WPS. 
應準備銲接典型示意圖（Welding Typicals），以利銲接文件之審查。銲接典型示意圖應涵蓋本專案適用之所有接頭配置，並註明其對應之銲接程序書（WPS）。

The erection contractor shall prepare and qualify its Welding Procedure Specifications. These Welding Procedure Specifications and Procedure Qualification Records shall be maintained at the jobsite and be in accordance with the applicable project requirements. 
安裝施工承攬商應負責編製並取得其銲接程序書（WPS）之資格檢定。此類銲接程序書（WPS）與程序資格檢定紀錄（PQR）皆應妥善保存於施工現場，並符合適用的專案規範要求。

Preparation of WPS/PQR: 
銲接程序書（WPS）與程序資格檢定紀錄（PQR）之準備：

#### 每一種銲接配置與每種材質皆必須提交對應之銲接程序書（WPS） A WPS must be submitted for every weld configuration and each material type

- Each WPS shall be supported by a PQR 
- 每份銲接程序書（WPS）皆應有程序資格檢定紀錄（PQR）作為佐證支持。

- WPS shall identify actual brand and type of filler metal 
- 銲接程序書（WPS）中應明確標示所使用銲材之實際品牌與型號。

The erection contractor shall ensure that each welder has a qualification in accordance with the requirements. 
安裝施工承攬商應確保每位銲工皆具備符合規範要求之合格資格檢定。

The erection contractor shall provide all welding materials, equipment and consumables as per the requirements. All welding equipment, where applicable, will have a valid calibration/test certificate. 
安裝施工承攬商應依規範要求提供所有銲接材料、設備及耗材。所有適用之銲接設備皆應具備有效之校正或檢驗合格證明書。

### 5.4.6. Non-destructive testing and (Post) Weld Heat Treatment
NDE and (Post) Weld Heat Treatment shall be in accordance with the applicable code and project requirements. All personnel involved shall be qualified accordingly.
### 5.4.6. 非破壞檢測與銲後熱處理（PWHT）
非破壞檢測（NDE）與銲後熱處理（PWHT）應符合適用之法規與專案規範要求。所有參與之人員皆應取得相應之資格檢定。

All Non-Destructive testing equipment, where applicable, will have a valid calibration/test certificate. 
所有適用之非破壞檢測設備皆應具備有效之校正或檢驗合格證明書。

### 5.4.7. 設備、工具與材料 Equipment, Tools and Materials

All equipment, instruments and materials, where applicable, will have a valid calibration / test certificate. 
所有適用之設備、儀器與材料皆應具備有效之校正或檢驗合格證明書。

Examples of such are: 
範例如下：

- Lifting Equipment 
- 起重吊裝設備

- Measurement devices 
- 量測儀器與設備

- Scaffolding materials 
- 施工鷹架材料

- HSE related materials and equipment 
- 工安衛（HSE）相關材料與設備

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- The weight for large parts is mentioned on the manufacturer’s drawings. 
- 大型組件之重量皆已標示於原廠製造圖面上。

- All temporary lifting constructions, provisions or facilities are considered to be included in the scope of the Erection contractor unless otherwise mentioned. 
- 除非另有註明，否則所有臨時性吊裝結構、防護措施或設施皆視為包含於安裝施工承攬商之工作範圍內。

- Lifting lugs already foreseen in the shop are for handling and transportation purposes only unless, otherwise noted. These are not designed and shall not be used for installation activities unless, otherwise noted. Some parts and components may require special lifting equipment and/or temporary lifting constructions or facilities. 
- 除非另有說明，否則出廠前已預焊之吊耳僅供搬運與運輸之用。此類吊耳並非針對安裝作業設計，且除非另有註明，否則不得用於安裝施工。部分零件與組件可能需要專用的吊裝設備及／或臨時性吊裝結構或設施。

- Assembly, use and disassembly of the special lifting equipment delivered by the manufacturer (like strong back frames, lifting frames, spreader beams, etc.) are to be considered in the scope of the installation contractor. 
- 由原廠提供之專用吊裝設備（如加強背架、吊裝框架、平衡樑等）之組裝、使用與拆卸，皆應納入安裝施工承攬商之工作範圍。

### 5.4.8. 材料標記、儲存與搬運 Material Marking, Storage and Handling

#### 收料驗收 Receipt

- Delivered goods are clearly marked with their unique piece mark number and/or item tag no. 
- 運抵現場之貨品皆應清晰標示其專屬之件號（Piece Mark Number）及／或設備位號（Tag No.）。

- Erection contractor shall check all delivered goods on quantity, dimension, damage, documents and heat number according to the MRR. In case of any deviation like overage, damaged or shortage, a report shall be submitted to the manufacturer in writing as mentioned in the “Storage and Handling Procedure – Site” 
- 安裝施工承攬商應依據材料接收報告（MRR），針對所有運抵現場之貨品進行數量、尺寸、外觀受損、隨附文件及爐號（Heat Number）之核對。若發現任何異常（如超量、損壞或短缺），應依據「現場儲存與搬運程序書」之規定，向原廠提交書面報告。

#### 儲存與搬運 Storage and Handling

- For storage and handling, see document 60031-730-01-005 “Storage and Handling Procedure” for all specific requirements. 
- 關於儲存與搬運之所有具體要求，請參閱文件編號 60031-730-01-005 之「儲存與搬運程序書」。

### 5.4.9. 現場組裝準備工作 Preparation for Site Assembly

Activities to be performed by the erection contractor in advance and to be ready before the installation works commence: 
安裝施工承攬商應提前執行，並於安裝工程開工前準備就緒之作業項目：

- Site mobilisation (manpower, office facilities and tools/equipment) ready 
- 工地動員（人力、辦公設施及工具／設備）準備就緒

- Lay-down plan ready (HRSG parts storage) 
- 堆置場規劃圖準備就緒（用於 HRSG 組件儲存）

- Lay-down plan ready (HRSG pre-assembly) 
- 預組裝場地規劃圖準備就緒（用於 HRSG 預組裝）

- Material receive and  handling procedure ready (how to receive, store and control HRSG parts on site) 
- 材料接收與搬運程序書準備就緒（規範現場如何接收、儲存及管制 HRSG 組件）

- Approved documents for : 
- 以下項目之核准文件：

   - HSE Plan 
   - 工安衛（HSE）計畫書

   - Welding documentation (WPS, PQR, Welder qualifications) 
   - 銲接相關文件（WPS、PQR、銲工資格檢定）

   - FQPs 
   - 現場品質計畫書（FQP）

   - Work Method  Statements 
   - 施工說明書／工法說明書（Work Method Statements）

- Drawings for construction according to the Erection Drawing List 60031-730-01-002 available on site. 
- 現場已備妥符合安裝施工圖樣清單（Erection Drawing List）編號 60031-730-01-002 之施工圖面。

### 5.4.10. 施工調整 Construction adjustments

Adjustments required for compensating fabrication and/or erection tolerances are part of the Erection contractor’s scope. 
用於補償製造及／或安裝公差所需之調整工作，皆屬於安裝施工承攬商之工作範圍。

Examples of such typical construction adjustments are: 
典型施工調整之範例如下：

- Clashes between small bore piping (field run) and steel work or other objects. 
- 小口徑管路（現場配置管）與鋼結構或其他物件之間之碰撞干涉。

- Clashes between small bore piping (field run) and large bore piping. 
- 小口徑管路（現場配置管）與大口徑管路之間之碰撞干涉。

- Fit-up of piping. 
- 管路對口組對（Fit-up）。

- Adjustments of small bore piping, relative to the isometric, which are required based on the final dimension check at site. 
- 根據現場最終尺寸量測結果，針對小口徑管路對照等角圖（Isometric）進行之必要調整。

- Correction of deviations in wall thickness and/or roundness of piping. 
- 管路壁厚及／或圓度偏差之修正。

- Threading of small bore piping, where indicated on the isometrics. 
- 依等角圖所示，進行小口徑管路之車牙（絞螺紋）作業。

- Adjustment of construction steel, ducting or casing panels, requiring cutting or use of filler plates. 
- 施工鋼結構、煙道或爐牆氣密鋼板（Casing）面板之調整（包含切割或使用墊板）。

- Adjustment or re-drilling of bolt holes in construction steel 
- 施工鋼結構螺栓孔之調整或重新鑽孔。

- Adjustments on internal insulation and liner sheeting. 
- 內部保溫材與不銹鋼內護板（Liner Sheet）之調整。

- Grating cut-outs and reinstatement with reference to E&I, tubing, conduit etc. 
- 配合儀電（E&I）、儀控管線、電線管等進行之格柵板（Grating）開孔與復原。

- Adjustments on internal baffle and sealing plates. 
- 內部煙氣導流板（Baffle）與密封板之調整。

- Adjustments on platform, grating, handrailing, kick plates, e.g. with reference to clashes with piping, valves, actuators, insulation e.g. 
- 平台、格柵板、扶手欄杆、踢腳板等之調整（例如解決與管路、閥門、驅動器、保溫層等之碰撞干涉）。

# 6. 預組裝作業 PRE-ASSEMBLY

## 6.1. 通則 GENERAL

Pre-assembly of HRSG components is not a must, but a recommendation from the manufacturer. 
HRSG 組件之預組裝並非強制性要求，但為原廠強烈建議之工法。

Specific requirements as part of the pre-assembly and / or installation are mentioned in the relevant chapter or paragraph for the preassembly or installation (if any). 
作為預組裝及／或安裝作業之一部分，其具體要求皆已於預組裝或安裝之相關章節中說明（若有）。

Manufacturer advices to coordinate which and at what time specific parts are best pre-assembled with all relevant parties involved. Pre-assembly of parts mostly starts at the beginning of the project. 
原廠建議與所有相關單位共同協調，確認哪些特定組件在何時進行預組裝最為合適。組件之預組裝作業通常於專案初期即開始進行。

## 6.2. 主鋼結構架／門型排架 Main steel structure portals

This paragraph describes the pre-assembly of the Main steel structure portals of the boiler. 
本節說明鍋爐主鋼結構架／門型排架（Goalposts）之預組裝作業。

### 6.2.1. 通則 GENERAL

A main steel structure portal is built-up from two (2) vertical columns and a top and bottom girder. 
每組主鋼結構架／門型排架係由兩（2）支立柱（Columns）以及頂部與底部橫樑（Girders）組裝而成。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
安裝施工承攬商應編製包含吊裝計畫在內之施工說明書與風險評估報告。

### 6.2.2. 主鋼結構架／門型排架預組裝之文件與程序書 Documents and procedures for pre-assembly of main steel structure portals rows

Documents and procedures required for pre-assembly of main steel structure portals 
主鋼結構架／門型排架預組裝所需之文件與程序書：

-  業主／客戶 Client
- Approved and reviewed from erection contractor: 
- 已審查並核准安裝施工承攬商之以下文件：

   - Work method statement :  Erection main steel structure boiler. 
   - 施工說明書：鍋爐主鋼結構吊裝架設。

   - Work method statement :  Preparation lay-down area and site area. - FQP :  HRSG Main steel - Bolt torque procedure :  Non pressure parts. - WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts. 
   - 施工說明書：堆置場與現場區域準備。 - 現場品質計畫書（FQP）：HRSG 主鋼結構。 - 螺栓扭力鎖緊程序書：非受壓件。 - 銲接程序書／程序資格檢定紀錄／銲工資格檢定（WPS / PQR / WPQ）：非受壓件。

   - Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts. 
   - 銲接典型示意圖／紀錄：非受壓件。

   - Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts. 
   - 銲材管制與搬運程序書：非受壓件。

   - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts. 
   - 非破壞檢測（NDE）程序書／人員資格檢定：非受壓件。

### 6.2.3. 主鋼結構架／門型排架 Main steel structure portals

Preferably, the pre-assembly area for the non-panelized main steel structure portals is near or on the HRSG foundation. It is preferable to erect the main steel structure portals directly after pre-assembly. 
未預先組裝成板片狀之主鋼結構架／門型排架，其預組裝場地建議優先選擇在 HRSG 爐座基礎旁或基礎上方。建議於預組裝完成後，立即進行主鋼結構架／門型排架之吊裝架設。

Before the pre-assembly of the steel structures can start, some preparations need to be made in advance. 
在鋼結構預組裝作業開始之前，必須提前完成相關準備工作。

#### 準備工作與先決條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述章節中所提及之文件與程序書皆應準備就緒，並經由權責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 以下準備工作／作業項目必須完成，且若適用，應於現場品質計畫書（FQP）中簽認同意。

   - Pre-assembly area ready. 
   - 預組裝場地準備就緒。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report). 
   - 材料已接收，且其數量與品質已檢驗完成（包含溢短裝與損壞報告 OSD Report）。

#### 準備工作 Preparation

- Assembly area shall be prepared taking into account the project and client requirements. _Note:_ 
- 組裝場地之準備應考量專案與業主之規範要求。_注意事項：_

   - Pre-assembly area shall be accessible without obstacles. 
   - 預組裝場地應保持暢通，無任何障礙物。

   - Adequately support the columns and girders on the pre-assembly area. 
   - 預組裝場地上之立柱與橫樑應提供足夠且妥善之支撐。

   - Supporting needs to be exactly levelled. 
   - 支撐結構必須精確抓平（水平度調整）。

   - Sufficient supports shall be in place to prevent sagging of columns and girders. 
   - 應設置足夠之支撐，以防止立柱與橫樑發生下垂或撓曲變形。

   - If the HRSG foundation is used as the pre-assembly area, take care of proper protection and avoid damaging of the foundation. 
   - 若使用 HRSG 爐座基礎作為預組裝場地，必須做好妥善之防護措施，避免損壞基礎。

#### 預組裝作業 Pre-assembly

- Erect, fit, align and bolt the columns, top and bottom girder per row. _Note:_ - Install the temporary profile angles to support the columns and the girders for the correct fit-up and installing bolts. - Use the correct bolt material and bolt length, in accordance with the bolt list. - Tightening of the bolted connections for the goalpost rows in accordance with the work method statement. - Adjustment of holes with cutting torches is prohibited. - When misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 依序將每排之立柱、頂部與底部橫樑進行立起、對口、對齊並以螺栓鎖緊。_注意事項：_ - 安裝臨時型鋼角鐵以支撐立柱與橫樑，確保正確對口並便於安裝螺栓。 - 應依據螺栓清單，使用正確之螺栓材質與長度。 - 依據施工說明書之規定，鎖緊門型排架（Goalposts）各排之螺栓連接處。 - 嚴禁使用割炬（乙炔切割）進行螺栓孔之擴孔或調整。 - 若發現螺栓孔錯位，必須在與原廠協商後方可進行調整。

- - Splices in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing. - Erection of transverse bumper supports while the main steel portal is still in horizontal position. 
- - 除非圖面另有標示，否則螺栓連接處不允許進行拼接。 - 當主鋼結構架仍處於水平狀態時，即應安裝橫向防撞支撐（Transverse Bumper Supports）。

- Bolting • Bolting of girders to the columns. _Note:_ 
- 螺栓鎖緊作業 • 將橫樑以螺栓鎖緊至立柱上。_注意事項：_

#### 螺栓鎖緊作業 Bolting

- Follow the details and or typical for bolting on the drawings. 
- 請遵循圖面上之螺栓鎖緊細部圖或典型示意圖進行作業。

- Quality control • Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). _Note:_ 
- 品質管制（QC） • 依據適用之現場品質計畫書（FQP）及／或程序書執行品質管制活動。_注意事項：_

- During pre-assembly frequently check the assembly and / or fit-up. 
- 於預組裝過程中，應頻繁檢查組裝及／或對口狀況。

- Final inspection of pre-assembled goalposts to take place prior to erection. 
- 預組裝完成之門型排架（Goalposts）在吊裝架設前，應進行最終檢驗。

- Release for erection of pre-assembled main steel structure portals with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 釋放預組裝完成之主鋼結構架／門型排架以進行吊裝，並隨附未完工項目清單（Outstanding Items，若有）。

- In case of lifting a complete portal use slings for lifting. 
- 若要吊裝整組結構架，應使用吊帶進行吊掛。

#### 後續作業釋放 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 順利完成本節所述之作業後，即可釋放並進行以下後續作業：

   - Erection pre-assembled main steel structure portals. 
   - 吊裝架設預組裝完成之主鋼結構架／門型排架。

## 6.3. 平台、樓梯、管架分段，以及煙囪與出口煙道之支撐鋼結構 Platforms, Stair cases, Pipe rack sections and  Bracing steel structures stack and outlet duct.

For pre-assembly of the platforms, stairs, ladders, hand railing and grating, follow the steps and requirements stipulated in the chapter “Secondary steel”. 
關於平台、樓梯、爬梯、扶手欄杆及格柵板（Grating）之預組裝，請遵循「二次鋼結構」章節中所規定之步驟與要求。

## 6.4. 煙囪分段 Stack sections

This paragraph describes the pre-assembly of the stack . 
本節說明排煙煙囪的預組裝作業。 

### 6.4.1. 通則 General

In order to minimize work at height it is required to pre-assemble the complete stack, including platforms ladders at ground level. The stack is built-up from several sections. The lower sections (part 1,2,3 and 4) of the stack unto the stack damper can be erected at the stack location. 
為儘可能減少高處作業，必須在地面層進行整座煙囪的預組裝，包含平台與爬梯。煙囪是由數個分段組合而成。煙囪下半部（第 1、2、3 及 4 部分）至煙囪擋風門（Damper）之區段，可直接在煙囪安裝基礎位置進行吊裝架設。 

The upper three sections (part 5, 6 and 7) of the stack can be pre-assembled. These stack sections are built-up from 120 degrees segments (shell parts). The segments can differ in weight and height. 
煙囪上半部的三個分段（第 5、6 及 7 部分）可進行預組裝。這些煙囪分段是由 120 度的弧形分段（殼體部件）拼裝而成。各分段的重量與高度可能有所不同。 

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
安裝施工承攬商應準備施工計畫書／風險評估報告以及吊裝計畫。 

### 6.4.2. 文件與程序書 Documents and procedures

Documents and procedures required for pre-assembly of stack 
排煙煙囪預組裝所需之文件與程序書： 

- Work method statement :  Installation stack. 
- 施工計畫書：煙囪安裝作業。 

- - Work method statement :  Scaffolding stack pre-assembly. - Work method statement :  Preparation lay-down area and site area - FQP :  HRSG Stack 
- - 施工計畫書：煙囪預組裝施工架架設。 - 施工計畫書：堆置場與現場區域準備。 - 施工品質計畫：HRSG 煙囪。 

- WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲接程序書 (WPS) / 銲接程序資格檢定記錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格檢定記錄 (WPQ)：非受壓元件。 

- Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 典型銲接細部圖／銲接紀錄：非受壓元件。 

- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲材管制程序書：非受壓元件。 

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序書／檢測人員資格證明：非受壓元件。 

### 6.4.3. 煙囪分段預組裝 Pre-assembly of stack sections

Preferably the pre-assembly area is near the final stack location. 
預組裝區域以鄰近煙囪最終安裝位置為佳。 

Before stack section pre-assembly can start, some preparations need to be made in advance. 
在開始進行煙囪分段預組裝之前，必須提前做好相關準備工作。 

#### 準備工作與先決條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落中提及的文件與程序書必須準備就緒，並經由負責單位審查完成。 

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 以下準備工作／活動必須完成，且若適用，須在施工品質計畫 中簽認同意： 

   - Pre-assembly area ready 
   - 預組裝區域準備就緒 

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已點收，且其數量與品質已檢驗完成（運輸損壞與短缺報告，即 OSD 報告） 

- Prepare a suitable stable table (platform) for pre-assembly of the stack segments. 
- 準備一個合適且穩固的平台（工作台），用於煙囪弧形分段的預組裝。 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

   - The table for pre-assembly needs to be levelled for correct pre-assembly of the stack section. 
   - 預組裝平台必須進行水平校正，以確保煙囪分段預組裝的精準度。 

   - Create sufficient height between table and ground for easy access to the inside of the stack part during pre-assembly. 
   - 平台與地面之間應保持足夠的高度，以便在預組裝期間人員能輕易進入煙囪內部作業。 

   - Before pre-assembly of the segments, mark the 0, 120 and 240 degrees as a reference for longitudinal seam location. 
   - 在進行弧形分段預組裝之前，請標記出 0 度、120 度及 240 度位置，作為縱向銲道位置的基準參考。 

- Prepare the scaffolding for the stack segments on the outside and inside for the section. 
- 準備該分段內側與外側所需的煙囪分段施工架（鷹架）。 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Install the scaffolding in such way that the segments can be pre-assembled easily and without interference. 
- 施工架的搭設方式應便於弧形分段的預組裝，且不得產生干涉。 

- Scaffolding needs to be suitable for installation of the field parts (platforms, insulation, etc.) as well. 
- 施工架亦須適用於後續現場配件（平台、保溫等）的安裝作業。 

#### 預組裝作業 Pre-assembly

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the segments. 
- 吊裝、對口並定位銲（點銲）各弧形分段。 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- During erection check the position of longitudinal seams relative to the previously marked reference points. 
- 吊裝期間，應檢查縱向銲道相對於先前標記之基準點的位置。 

- Verify elevation, roundness and dimensions of the segments to the tolerances specified in the drawings. 
- 驗證各分段的高程、真圓度及尺寸，使其符合圖面規定的公差要求。 

- Stack segments shall be secured at several points by guy wires, see work method statement. 
- 煙囪分段應使用拉線（纜風繩）在數個位置進行固定，詳見施工計畫書。 

#### 煙囪分段銲接 Welding of stack segments

- Weld the longitudinal seams of the stack segments. 
- 銲接煙囪分段的縱向銲道。 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面上的銲接細部圖／典型銲接圖及銲接程序書 (WPS) 進行作業。 

- Check elevation, roundness and dimensions of the stack section to match the tolerances specified in the drawings. 
- 檢查煙囪分段的高程、真圓度及尺寸，以符合圖面規定的公差。 

- Release for erection field parts of stack section with a list of outstanding items. 
- 釋放煙囪分段之現場配件安裝作業，並附上未完工項目清單（Punch List）。 

#### 現場配件 Field parts

Field parts for the stack can be stiffener plates, U-channels, trunnions, measurement tubes, instrument nozzles and secondary steel components like supporting and platforms. Identify all required field parts indicated on the drawings. 
煙囪的現場配件可能包括加強板、U型鋼（槽鋼）、吊裝軸銷 (Trunnions)、量測管、儀表管嘴，以及支撐架與平台等二次鋼結構元件。請確認圖面上標示的所有必要現場配件。 

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the field parts. _Note:_ 
- 吊裝、對口並定位銲（點銲）現場配件。_注意事項：_ 

   - Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings for the field parts. 
   - 現場配件應遵循圖面上典型銲接圖的要求。 

   - Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawing. 
   - 確認圖面上標示的所有必要現場配件。 

   - Erect the supports for the cable trays. 
   - 安裝電纜線架的支撐架。 

#### 現場配件銲接 Welding field parts

- Weld the Erected field parts. 
- 銲接已安裝的現場配件。 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings. 
- 請遵循圖面上的銲接細部圖或典型銲接圖進行作業。 

- Release without a list of outstanding items. 
- 釋放作業（此時應無未完工項目清單）。 

### 6.4.4. 煙囪二次鋼結構 Secondary steel stack

Erection of secondary steel for the stack parts during the pre-assembly phase is based on the requirements stipulated in the chapter “Secondary steel”. 
在預組裝階段進行煙囪分段之二次鋼結構（扶手平台樓梯）吊裝架設時，應依據「二次鋼結構」章節中所規定的要求辦理。 

### 6.4.5. 煙囪煙氣消音器 Flue gas silencers stack

Erect the flue gas silencers according the installation manual and documents of the silencer supplier. 
請依據消音器供應商的安裝手冊及文件，進行煙氣消音器的吊裝架設。 

### 6.4.6. 外部保溫（若適用）（非 HTT 供應範圍） External insulation (if applicable) (not in HTT scope)

The Erection of external insulation for the stack sections is recommended during the pre-assembly phase. 
建議在預組裝階段進行煙囪分段外部保溫的施工作業。 

#### 安裝施工 Erection

- Erect the external insulation according the applicable drawing / specification instructions and requirements stipulated. _Note:_ 
- 依據適用的圖面／規範說明及規定的要求進行外部保溫施工。_注意事項：_ 

   - Before any insulation material is applied, surfaces to be insulated must be clean and dry. 
   - 在鋪設任何保溫材料之前，待保溫的表面必須保持清潔與乾燥。 

   - Insulation materials are to be kept dry during erection. 
   - 保溫材料在安裝施工期間必須保持乾燥。 

   - Insulation shall be protected to prevent water ingress or pollution of the insulation material. 
   - 應對保溫材料採取保護措施，以防止水分滲入或材料受到污染。 

   - In case of multiple layers the insulation joints shall be Erected staggered. 
   - 若採用多層保溫，保溫接縫應採交錯（錯開）方式安裝。 

   - Ensure that no gaps or hollow spaces are formed at the insulation blanket joints, i.e. in the longitudinal and circumferential direction. 
   - 確保在保溫毯接縫處（即縱向與環向）不會形成縫隙或空洞。 

   - In order to prevent water ingress insulation sheeting seams are to be sealed. Before applying any sealant, respective surfaces need to be free from dirt, grease and other pollution. 
   - 為防止水分滲入，保溫金屬外包皮（護板）的接縫必須進行密封。在塗抹任何密封膠之前，相關表面不得有髒污、油脂及其他污染。 

   - Sheeting and insulation penetrations must be cut out as small and efficient as possible. 
   - 外包皮與保溫層的穿孔開口裁剪應儘可能小且緊湊。 

   - Keep the lifting trunnions temporary free from external insulation (to be closed after hoisting). 
   - 吊裝軸銷 (Trunnions) 處暫時不要包覆外部保溫（待吊裝完成後再行封閉）。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
請依據適用的現場品質計畫書 (FQP) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

### 6.4.7. 其他設備 Other equipment

After completion of the pre-assembly of a stack section, please assure all other stack equipment (e.g. Davits, cable trays, CEMS provisions, AWL’s etc.) are installed, mitigating the need for additional scaffold works or work at height in a later stage. 
當煙囪分段預組裝完成後，請務必確認所有其他煙囪附屬設備（例如：旋臂吊桿、電纜托架、連續排放監測系統 (CEMS) 預留設施、航空障礙燈等）皆已安裝完畢，以減少後續階段對額外鷹架搭設或高處作業的需求。

### 6.4.8. 煙囪第 6+7 節吊裝架設至第 5 節上 Erection stack part 6+7 onto stack part 5

The pre-assembled stack section 7 can be erected onto pre-assembled stack section part 6. The combined sections 6+7 and stack part 5 can either be separately lifted onto the stack, or section 6+7 (top section) can be pre-assembled onto section 5 (lower section), as long as SWL of top trunnion supports the combined weight and correct crane and sufficient lifting space are available. 
預組裝完成的煙囪第 7 節可吊裝架設至預組裝完成的煙囪第 6 節上。合併後的第 6+7 節與煙囪第 5 節，既可分別吊裝至煙囪本體上，亦可在具備合適起重機與足夠吊裝空間，且頂部吊耳的安全工作負荷 (SWL) 足以承受合併重量的前提下，將第 6+7 節（頂部區段）預先組裝至第 5 節（底部區段）上。

#### 頂部區段吊裝架設 Erection top section

- Align, fit up and tack weld the top section to the bottom section of the upper stack part 
- 將上部煙囪段的頂部區段與底部區段進行對心、組對並點銲固定。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- During erection check position, elevation and alignment of top section. 
- 在吊裝架設過程中，請檢查頂部區段的位置、高程與對心狀態。

- Stack sections to be secured by use of crane or guy wires during fit-up and tack welding. 
- 在組對與點銲期間，應使用起重機或拉線（風繩）將煙囪區段固定牢固。

- Check the fit-up between bottom section and top section. 
- 檢查底部區段與頂部區段之間的組對間隙與平整度。

- Check dimension, elevation and roundness for stack sections. 
- 檢查煙囪各區段的尺寸、高程與真圓度。

#### 銲接作業 Welding

- Weld stack top section onto bottom section. 
- 將煙囪頂部區段與底部區段進行銲接。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面與銲接程序書 (WPS) 上的銲接細節及/或典型標準。

#### 外部保溫（如適用） External insulation (if applicable)

- Complete the external insulation for the field splice between stack top and bottom section. _Note:_ 
- 完成煙囪頂部與底部區段之間工地接頭（現場接縫）的外部保溫。_注意事項：_ 

   - Erect the external insulation according the applicable drawing / specification instructions and requirements stipulated. 
   - 請依據適用的圖面/規範說明及規定的要求進行外部保溫安裝。

   - Check elevation and roundness of the stack assembly 
   - 檢查煙囪組合件的高程與真圓度。

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
   - 伴隨未完工項目清單（如有）進行階段驗收釋放。

### 6.4.9. 預組裝煙囪之最終檢驗 Final inspection of pre-assembled stack

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Final Inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群組的機械安裝施工完成後，應對其進行檢驗。未完工項目應彙整於未完工項目清單中。該未完工項目清單可隨附於最終檢驗合格證書。

Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities. 
此類證書旨在作為安裝施工活動已妥善完成的記錄。

The Final Inspection Certificate for pre-assembled stack describes the systems or components inspected. 
預組裝煙囪的最終檢驗合格證書中應詳細說明已檢驗的系統或組件。

By signing the Final Inspection Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of erection to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly. 
經由簽署最終檢驗合格證書，相關各方即確認所述系統或組件的安裝施工已達到足夠成熟的階段，可藉此確認系統移交試運轉前仍須處理的遺留項目；若無任何遺留項目，則可直接將系統移交試運轉。

#### 現場巡檢 (Walk-down) Walk-down

All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
機械完工證書中所述的所有系統或特定組件群組，均應進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性並檢查是否有損壞。

A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
現場巡檢後，應立即建立未完工項目記錄（如有）。

In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized: 
若有適用的未完工項目清單，應進行以下分類：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items) -  Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前須解決的項目（A 類項目） - 試運轉前須解決的項目（B 類項目）

- Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items) 
- 暫收（初步驗收）前須解決的項目（C 類項目）

- _Note:_ 
- _注意事項：_ 

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 證實相關系統所適用的現場品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有相關方簽署完畢。未完工項目應納入未完工點清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 證實所有不合格報告 (NCR) 均已結案。未完工項目應納入未完工點清單中。

## 6.5. 煙囪擋風門預組裝 Stack damper pre-assembly

This paragraph describes the pre-assembly of the stack damper 
本節說明煙囪擋風門的預組裝作業。

### 6.5.1. 煙囪擋風門 Stack damper

Preferably the pre-assembly area is near the stack location. 
預組裝區域建議優先選擇鄰近煙囪安裝位置之處。

The damper is delivered in two pieces. 
擋風門以兩件分段運抵現場。

Before stack damper pre-assembly can start some preparations need to be made in advance. 
在開始進行煙囪擋風門預組裝之前，需提前做好相關準備工作。

#### 準備工作 Preparation

- Prepare a suitable stable table (platform) for pre-assembly of the stack damper. 
- 準備一個適合且穩固的平台（工作檯），用於煙囪擋風門的預組裝。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- The table for pre-assembly needs to be levelled for correct erection of the stack damper. 
- 預組裝平台必須進行水平校正，以確保煙囪擋風門的正確安裝施工。

- Create sufficient height between table and ground for easy access to the inside of the damper part during pre-assembly. 
- 平台與地面之間應保持足夠的高度，以便在預組裝期間能輕易進入擋風門部件的內部。

#### 預組裝 Pre-assembly

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the damper segments. 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲固定擋風門各分段。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the stack damper supplier erection instructions. 
- 請遵循煙囪擋風門供應商的安裝施工說明。

- Components are secured by coloured fixations, which need to be removed for the pre-assembly and final erection. 
- 組件由彩色固定件鎖固，在進行預組裝與最終安裝施工時必須將其拆除。

#### 擋風門分段銲接 Welding of damper segments

- Weld the longitudinal seams of the damper segments. 
- 銲接擋風門分段的縱向接縫。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面與銲接程序書 (WPS) 上的銲接細節及/或典型標準。

- External insulation after final erection of stack damper. 
- 外部保溫作業應於煙囪擋風門最終安裝施工完成後進行。

- Lifting of the damper to take place according the supplier drawings and handling instructions. 
- 擋風門的吊裝應依據供應商圖面與搬運說明書進行。

## 6.6. 大小口徑蒸汽管路預組裝 Large & small bore piping pre-assembly

For the pre-assembly of the large & small bore piping, please follow the steps and requirements stipulated in chapter 15 “Piping”. 
關於大口徑與小口徑蒸汽管路的預組裝，請遵循第 15 章「蒸汽管路」中所規定的步驟與要求。

# 7. 鍋爐總則 BOILER GENERAL

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含以下各節：

# 1. 基礎 Foundation

# 2. 無收縮水泥灌漿 (Grouting) Grouting

# 3. 內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) Internal insulation and liner sheeting

:  paragraph 7.1 :  paragraph 7.2 :  paragraph 7.3 
:  第 7.1 節 :  第 7.2 節 :  第 7.3 節 

- 7.1. Foundation 
- 7.1. 基礎 

This paragraph describes the requirements for the review of the foundation. 
本節說明基礎審查與驗收之相關要求。

- 7.1.1. General 
- 7.1.1. 通則 

Review and verification of the HRSG foundation shall be performed for location, position, elevation and condition for all the related HRSG parts to be erected. 
針對所有待安裝之熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 相關組件，必須對其 HRSG 爐座基礎之位置、座標、高程及表面狀況進行審查與核對。

- 7.1.2. Documents and procedures 
- 7.1.2. 文件與程序書 

Documents and procedures required for review of the HRSG foundation . 
審查 HRSG 基礎 所需之文件與程序書。

   - Third party survey report foundation/anchors :  Review of actual dimensions 
   - 第三方基礎/地錨測量報告：實際尺寸審查 

- 7.1.3. Review of HRSG foundation 
- 7.1.3. HRSG 基礎審查 

Review of the HRSG foundation to be executed in advance and before start of pre-assembly. 
HRSG 基礎之審查作業應提前進行，且必須在預組裝工作開始前完成。

#### 審查與量測 Review

- Measure the entire HRSG foundation and anchor placement for position, location and elevations. 
- 量測整個 HRSG 基礎及地錨配置之位置、座標與高程。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Make a survey report of actual dimensions, locations and elevations of the entire HRSG foundation and anchors. 
- 製作整個 HRSG 基礎及地錨之實際尺寸、位置與高程的測量報告。

- Check pockets for cleanliness 
- 檢查地錨預留孔（Pockets）之清潔度 

- Check earthing for completion (if applicable) 
- 檢查接地系統是否已完工（若適用） 

- Check that the foundation around the area where the base plates will be installed is chipped and ready for grouting (chipping of concrete done) 
- 檢查欲安裝底座鋼板（Base plates）周邊之基礎混凝土表面是否已完成鑿毛（Chipping），並確認已準備好進行灌漿作業（混凝土鑿毛已完成） 

- Chipping of concrete shall be done in advance and before installation of the main steel portals. After installation of components it is very difficult to reach these areas. 
- 混凝土鑿毛作業應提前在主鋼結構架 / 門型排架 (Goalposts) 安裝前完成。組件安裝完成後，將很難觸及這些區域進行施工。

#### 品質管制 Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的現場品質計畫 (FQP) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Check foundation for completeness, damages and provide a report (official writing). 
- 檢查基礎之完整性、是否有受損，並提供正式書面報告。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 伴隨待辦事項清單（若有）進行放行。

#### 後續工項放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Foundation ready for erection main steel structure 
- 本節所述之活動成功完成後，即可放行以下後續工項：- 基礎已準備就緒，可進行主鋼結構安裝施工 

## 7.2. 無收縮水泥灌漿 (Grouting) Grouting

The chapter for grouting is generic and is referred to throughout this manual. 
本章所述之灌漿規範為通用性要求，貫穿本手冊之各項作業。

### 7.2.1. 通則 General

Grout is used underneath the base plates for the foundation and other steel structure bearing plates. Grouting ensures a consistent bearing between the bearing plate and the concrete. 
無收縮水泥灌漿料用於基礎底座鋼板及其他鋼結構承壓板下方。灌漿作業可確保承壓板與混凝土基礎之間達到均勻一致的承載接觸。

Specific requirements regarding grouting are mentioned in document 60031-730-01-007 “ _Grouting procedure_ ” 
有關灌漿之具體要求，請參閱文件編號 60031-730-01-007《灌漿施工程序書》。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Keep in mind the required duration for curing of the grout, before the next installation activity can start. Typical grout curing time is around 5 days, but will vary depending on grout type used and local ambient conditions. 
- 請務必注意灌漿料養護所需之時間，方可開始下一階段的安裝作業。一般而言，灌漿養護時間約為 5 天，但具體時間將視所使用的灌漿料類型及現場環境條件而定。

### 7.2.2. 文件與程序書 Documents and procedures

Documents and procedures required for installation of grouting . 
執行 無收縮水泥灌漿 (Grouting) 施工作業所需之文件與程序書。

- Work method statement 
- 施工計畫書 / 工法說明書 

- FQP 
- 現場品質計畫 (FQP) 

:  Grouting application. :  Grouting 
:  灌漿施作。 :  無收縮水泥灌漿 

### 7.2.3. 灌漿澆置 Pouring of grouting

Grouting is used for the following major HRSG components: 
無收縮水泥灌漿適用於以下 HRSG 主要組件：

- Main steel structure boiler 
- 鍋爐主鋼結構 

- Secondary steel structures 
- 二次鋼結構 / 扶手平台樓梯 

- Pipe supports 
- 管路支架 

- Tanks / vessels 
- 槽體 / 壓力容器 

- Supports 
- 支撐架 

- Equipment (if any) 
- 設備（若有） 

#### 準備工作與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述章節中所提及之文件與程序書必須準備就緒，並經由負責單位（或各方）審查核可。

#### 施工作業 Installation

- Perform the grouting 
- 執行灌漿作業 

- Testing of grout 
- 灌漿料試體試驗 

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Grouting and testing shall be executed according the applicable procedures and requirements. 
- 灌漿與試驗作業應嚴格依照適用的程序書及規範要求執行。

#### 品質管制 Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的現場品質計畫 (FQP) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

### 7.2.4. 灌漿最終檢驗 Final inspection of Grouting

When the mechanical installation of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Final Inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群組之機械安裝完成後，應對其進行檢驗。所有待辦事項應彙整於待辦事項清單（Outstanding items list）中。該待辦事項清單可作為「最終檢驗合格證明書」之附件。

Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the installation activities. 
此證明書係作為安裝作業已妥善完成之正式紀錄。

The Final Inspection Certificate for grouting describes the systems or components inspected. 
無收縮水泥灌漿 (Grouting) 之「最終檢驗合格證明書」中應詳細載明已檢驗之系統或組件。

By signing the Final Inspection Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly. 
經由簽署「最終檢驗合格證明書」，相關各方即共同確認：所述系統或組件之安裝進度已達足夠階段，可據以釐清系統移交至試運轉（Commissioning）前所需完成之剩餘待辦事項；若無任何待辦事項，則可直接將系統移交予試運轉階段。

#### 現場走訪檢查 (Walk-down) Walk-down

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages. 
- 「機械完工證明書」中所列之所有系統或特定組件群組，均應進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及是否有受損。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場走訪檢查後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized: 
- 若有適用之待辦事項清單，應進行分類：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前必須解決的項目（A類項目）。

   - - Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items) 
   - - 試運轉前必須解決的項目（B類項目）。 - 臨時驗收前必須解決的項目（C類項目）。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 確認相關系統所適用的施工品質計畫 已由所有相關方簽署完成。未決事項應列入缺點改善清單（Punch List）中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 確認所有不合格報告 (NCR) 均已結案。未決事項應列入缺點改善清單中。

## 7.3. 內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板 Internal insulation and liner sheeting

This paragraph describes the installation of the internal insulation and liner sheeting. 
本節說明內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 的安裝施工。

### 7.3.1. 通則 General

Internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on 60031-205-10 “Specification for internal insulation”. 
內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 的安裝應依據 60031-205-10「內部保溫技術規範」辦理。

For project specific requirements, the standard specifications shall be read in conjunction with the overruling amendment applicable to the project. 
針對本專案的特定需求，標準規範應與適用於本專案且具優先效力的修訂條款一併閱讀與執行。

### 7.3.2. 文件與程序書 Documents and procedures

Documents and procedures required for installation of the internal insulation and liner sheeting . 
內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝施工所需的文件與程序書如下：

- Work method statement : Installation casing and ducting 
- 施工計畫書：鍋爐外殼 (Casing) 與煙道安裝

- - FQP : HRSG casing and HRSG ducting - WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts. - Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts. 
- - 施工品質計畫：熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 外殼與煙道 - 銲接程序書 (WPS) / 程序檢定記錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格檢定記錄 (WPQ)：非受壓件。 - 典型銲接細部圖 / 銲接紀錄：非受壓件。

- Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲材管制程序書：非受壓件。

- - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts. 
- - 非破壞檢測 (NDT/NDE) 程序書 / 檢測人員資格：非受壓件。

### 7.3.3. 保溫釘 Insulation pins

Installation of insulation pins is required in field in certain areas. These are indicated on the drawings. The field installation of the insulation pins, needs to be performed before installation of the internal insulation. 
部分特定區域需在工地現場安裝保溫釘，這些區域均已在圖面上標示。現場保溫釘的安裝作業，必須在施作內部保溫之前完成。

Before installation of the insulation pins can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝保溫釘之前，必須提前做好相關準備工作。

#### 準備工作與先決條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落中所提及的文件與程序書必須準備就緒，並已由權責單位（或各方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 以下準備工作／活動必須已完成，且若適用，已在施工品質計畫 中簽認完畢。

   - Casing panels installed 
   - 爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 板片已安裝完畢

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已運抵現場，且其數量與品質已檢驗完畢（開箱檢驗與損壞報告，OSD Report）

#### 後續作業放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Internal insulation installation 
- 順利完成本節所述之各項作業後，即可放行以下後續作業： - 內部保溫安裝施工

#### 安裝施工 Installation

- Install, fit and tack-weld the insulation pins. 
- 安裝、對位並定位銲（點銲）保溫釘。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Before welding of the pins, the surface shall be cleaned. 
- 銲接保溫釘之前，應先將鋼板表面清理乾淨。

- Prior to welding, the exact location of the pins shall be established according the drawings. 
- 銲接前，應依據圖面確定保溫釘的準確位置。

- Strictly follow the instructions in the mentioned specifications from the manufacturer for welding of the carbon and / or stainless steel pins. 
- 進行碳鋼及／或不銹鋼保溫釘的銲接時，必須嚴格遵守製造商技術規範中的指示。

#### 保溫釘銲接 Welding pins

- Weld the pins. 
- 進行保溫釘銲接。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 應遵循圖面上的銲接細部圖或典型圖樣，以及銲接程序書 (WPS) 進行銲接。

#### 品質管制 Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的施工品質計畫 及／或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Verification of the correct location and fit-up of the pins before welding. 
- 銲接前應確認保溫釘的位置正確且組對（對位）無誤。

- Release without a list of outstanding items. 
- 確認無任何未決事項（缺點項目）後方可放行。

- Manufacturer shall visually check (random) welding of the insulation pins. 
- 原廠技術指導工程師 (Supervisor) 應對保溫釘的銲接進行目視抽檢。

### 7.3.4. 內部保溫 Internal insulation

Before installation of the internal insulation can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在內部保溫材料安裝作業開始之前，有些活動需要事先準備。

#### 準備工作與前置條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落中提及的文件與程序需備妥，並經由負責單位（或相關單位）審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 以下準備工作/活動需已完成，如適用，並在FQP（現場品質計畫書）中簽核放行。

   - Casing panels installed
   - 爐牆氣密鋼板安裝完成

   - Field insulation pins installed (where applicable)
   - 現場保溫釘安裝完成（如適用）

#### 後續活動放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Liner sheeting installation
- 本段落中的活動順利完成後，即可放行以下活動： - 不銹鋼內護板安裝

#### 安裝作業 Installation

- Install the internal insulation. _Note:_
- 安裝內部保溫材料。 _注意事項：_

   - Strictly follow the instructions in the specifications.
   - 嚴格遵循規範中的指示。

   - Surfaces to be insulated must be clean and dry before any insulation material is applied.
   - 在施作任何保溫材料之前，待保溫的表面必須清潔乾燥。

   - Insulation materials shall be kept completely dry during installation and shall be protected from water ingress or pollution as good as practically possible.
   - 保溫材料在安裝期間應保持完全乾燥，並盡可能地妥善保護，防止水氣滲入或污染。

   - Multi-layer joints shall be installed staggered at all joint sides.
   - 多層接縫在所有接縫處應交錯安裝。

   - Ensure that no gaps or hollow spaces exist.
   - 確保沒有間隙或空隙。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的FQP（現場品質計畫書）和/或程序，執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Verify correct installation of insulation layers and no gaps exist, before installing the liner sheeting.
- 在安裝不銹鋼內護板之前，請確認保溫層安裝正確且沒有間隙。

- Release without a list of outstanding items.
- 無待辦事項清單即可放行。

### 7.3.5. 不銹鋼內護板 Liner sheeting

Before installation of the liner sheeting can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在不銹鋼內護板安裝作業開始之前，有些活動需要事先準備。

#### 準備工作與前置條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落中提及的文件與程序需備妥，並經由負責單位（或相關單位）審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 以下準備工作/活動需已完成，如適用，並在FQP（現場品質計畫書）中簽核放行。

   - Internal insulation installed
   - 內部保溫材料安裝完成

#### 後續活動放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 本段落中的活動順利完成後，即可放行以下活動：

   - Tack welding nuts and washer
   - 螺帽與墊圈的點銲作業

#### 安裝作業 Installation

- Install liner sheeting.
- 安裝不銹鋼內護板。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Strictly follow the instructions in the specifications.
- 嚴格遵循規範中的指示。

- The liner sheeting shall be installed with an overlap as per the applicable drawing or typical.
- 不銹鋼內護板應依據適用的圖面或標準圖說，以搭接方式安裝。

- During installation verify the liner sheeting for having the correct overlap of the sheeting plates.
- 在安裝期間，請確認不銹鋼內護板的板材搭接是否正確。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的FQP（現場品質計畫書）和/或程序，執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

   - Verification of the correct installation of liner sheeting before tack-welding nuts.
   - 在點銲螺帽之前，確認不銹鋼內護板安裝正確。

   - Verification of tightness of nuts.
   - 確認螺帽鎖緊度。

   - Release without a list of outstanding items.
   - 無待辦事項清單即可放行。

- Manufacturer shall inspect (random) the tightness of the nuts before tack-welding.
製造商應在點銲前，隨機檢查螺帽的緊固度。

- Tack-welding nuts and washers.
螺帽與墊片的點銲作業。
• Tack-welding the nuts and washers.
• 執行螺帽與墊片的點銲作業。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 銲接作業應遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中所載明的細部圖說或標準圖。

#### 業主品質管制 Quality control client

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的現場品質計畫書 (FQP) 及/或相關程序書，執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有待辦事項，應連同缺失清單一併簽認放行。

### 7.3.6. 內部絕緣的最終檢查 Final inspection of the Internal insulation

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.
當某個系統或特定組件群的機械安裝施工完成後，應進行檢查。缺失項目應彙整成一份缺失清單，並附於最終檢查證明書上。

The Final inspection Certificate of the Internal insulation and liner sheeting describes the systems or components inspected.
內部絕緣及不銹鋼內護板的最終檢查證明書，應載明所檢查的系統或組件。

#### 檢查作業 Inspection

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.
- 最終檢查證明書上所提及的所有系統或特定組件群，應進行最終檢查，以確認安裝施工是否正確、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.
- 現場巡檢後，應立即建立缺失項目紀錄 (若有)。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :
- 若有缺失清單，應分類為：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)
   - 需在水壓試驗前解決的項目 (A類項目)

   - - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)
   - 需在熱機試運轉前解決的項目 (B類項目)
   - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)
   - 需在暫時驗收 (PAC) 前解決的項目 (C類項目)

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認相關系統的適用現場品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有相關方簽認。缺失項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認所有不符合報告 (NCR) 已結案。缺失項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

# 8. 鍋爐 BOILER

The chapter for the HRSG erection consists of the following paragraphs:
熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的安裝施工章節包含以下段落：

1. Main steel structure : paragraph 8.1
# 1. 主鋼結構：第 8.1 段
2. Scaffolding for main steel structure : paragraph 8.2
# 2. 主鋼結構施工架：第 8.2 段
3. Casing (bottom, side and top panels) : paragraph 8.3
# 3. 鍋爐外殼 (Casing) (底部、側面及頂部面板)：第 8.3 段
4. Secondary steel components : paragraph 8.4
# 4. 二次鋼結構組件：第 8.4 段
5. Transverse bumpers : paragraph 8.5
# 5. 橫向緩衝器：第 8.5 段
6. Grouting goalpost rows main steel structure boiler : paragraph 8.6
# 6. 鍋爐主鋼結構門型排架 (Goalposts) 列的無收縮水泥灌漿 (Grouting)：第 8.6 段
7. Module erection : paragraph 8.7
# 7. 模組吊裝架設：第 8.7 段
8. Baffles : paragraph 8.8
# 8. 煙氣導流板：第 8.8 段

## 8.1. 熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構 HRSG main steel structure

This paragraph describes the erection of the main steel structure.
本段落說明主鋼結構的吊裝架設。

### 8.1.1. 概述 General

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the main steel shall be prepared by the installation contractor.
針對主鋼結構的吊裝架設，安裝承攬商應準備施工方法說明書、風險評估及吊裝計畫。

The erection sequence for the HRSG main steel is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構的吊裝架設順序顯示於文件 60031-730-05-001 中。

### 8.1.2. 文件與程序書 Documents and procedures

Documents and procedures required for erection of the HRSG main steel .
針對熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構的吊裝架設所需的文件與程序書。

- Work method statement : Installation HRSG main steel structure.
- 施工方法說明書：熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構安裝。

- - FQP : HRSG Main steel
- 現場品質計畫書 (FQP)：熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構。
- Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.
- 螺栓扭力程序書：非壓力部件。
- WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts.
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 程序資格紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格證明 (WPQ)：非壓力部件。
- Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts.
- 銲接標準圖 / 紀錄：非壓力部件。

- Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts.
- 銲材處理程序書：非壓力部件。

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts.
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序書 / 人員資格：非壓力部件。

### 8.1.3. 主鋼結構吊裝架設 main steel structural erection

Before erection of main steel structural portals can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在主鋼結構門型排架 (Goalposts) 吊裝架設開始前，需預先準備一些活動。

#### 準備工作與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前一段落提及的文件與程序書需到位，並經由負責方審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 以下準備工作/活動需已完成，且若適用，已於現場品質計畫書 (FQP) 中簽認。

   - Foundation ready and released by civil department
   - 基礎已備妥並經土建部門放行

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)
   - 材料已收料並已進行數量與品質清點 (超短溢損報告 OSD report)

   - Erection of transverse bumper supports while the panelised main steel is still in horizontal position.
   - 當板片式主鋼結構仍處於水平位置時，應進行橫向緩衝器支撐的安裝施工。

   - Erect shim stacks and level to the correct elevation, before placement of the base plate / goalpost.
   - 在放置底板 / 門型排架 (Goalposts) 前，應疊放墊片組並校準至正確高程。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- It is important that the shims (for levelling of the main steel structure portals) are underneath the base plates and do not protrude.
- 重要的是，墊片 (用於主鋼結構門型排架 (Goalposts) 的水平校準) 應位於底板下方，且不得突出。

#### Release subsequent activities
釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection main steel structure bracing beams.
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，即可釋放以下作業： - 主鋼結構橫向支撐樑的吊裝架設。

   - Erection drum supporting beams.
   - 汽鼓支撐樑的吊裝架設。

   - Erection of transverse bumper supports
   - 橫向防撞支撐的吊裝架設。

   - Installation of earthing protection
   - 接地保護的施工作業。

Erection
吊裝架設

- Erect the pre-assembled main steel structural portals .
- 吊裝架設預組裝完成的主鋼結構門型排架。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- No lifting lugs are foreseen on the top girder, for lifting the complete main steel portal, so in case of lifting a complete portal use slings for lifting.
- 頂部大樑未預留吊耳，若需吊裝完整的門型排架，請使用吊索進行吊裝。

- Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening (see 60031-730-01-008).
- 螺栓鎖緊時請施加正確的扭力值（請參閱文件編號 60031-730-01-008）。

- During installation use temporary attachments (guy wires) for stability of the goalpost rows at the correct location and position..
- 施工作業期間，請使用臨時固定裝置（拉索）以確保門型排架列在正確位置上的穩定性。

- During installation check position, alignment and elevation of the goalpost rows.
- 施工作業期間，請檢查門型排架列的位置、對心及高程。

- Splices in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing.
- 螺栓連接處不允許有拼接，除非圖面另有標示。

- When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment of the bolt holes can only be made after consultation with the manufacturer.
- 若發現螺栓孔未對心，螺栓孔的調整必須在諮詢原廠後方可進行。

- After completion of the goalpost rows, inform client and request connection of the earthing to the columns.
- 門型排架列完成後，請通知業主並要求將接地線連接至柱體。

#### 主鋼結構門型排架的對心校準 Alignment main steel portals

- Final alignment of the main steel portals needs to be executed with loose guy wires.
- 主鋼結構門型排架的最終對心校準需在拉索鬆弛的狀態下進行。

- For tolerances see (60031-730-06 drawing series)
- 容許公差請參閱（圖面系列 60031-730-06）。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Verify alignment of the main steel portals during final alignment from “inside” of the goalpost rows.
- 最終對心校準時，請從門型排架列的「內部」驗證主鋼結構門型排架的對心狀況。

- Strong advice / recommendation from the manufacturer is to take the necessary time for alignment and verification of the main steel structure to be within the tolerances specified. Erection of the HRSG with a properly aligned steel structure will be easier, quicker and result in higher overall quality.
- 原廠強烈建議，務必預留足夠時間進行主鋼結構的對心校準與驗證，以確保其符合規範的容許公差。若鋼結構對心校準得當，HRSG 的吊裝架設將會更輕鬆、更快速，並能提升整體品質。

- Tolerances on the drawings are given to the X and Y direction with + or -.
- 圖面上的容許公差以 X 和 Y 方向的「正負值」表示。

- Final alignment needs to be performed to one side + or - and shall be equal for the complete main steel structure.
- 最終對心校準需以單一方向的正負值進行，且應確保整個主鋼結構的一致性。

- Contact the manufacturer in case of deviations.
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫原廠。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 請依據適用的 FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序執行品質管制作業。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Check alignment, elevation and dimensions with the manufacturer’s tolerance drawings for the goalpost rows.
- 請依據原廠的容許公差圖面，檢查門型排架列的對心、高程及尺寸。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何未完成項目，請列出清單後再行放行。

### 8.1.4. 主鋼結構橫向支撐樑 Main steel bracing beams

Before erection of the horizontal bracing beams can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始吊裝架設水平橫向支撐樑之前，需預先完成一些準備作業。

#### 準備作業與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前一段落提及的文件與程序需已備妥，並經由負責單位（或相關單位）審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP
- 以下準備作業/活動需已完成，並在 FQP (現場品質計畫) 中簽核（如適用）：

   - Main steel structure portals installed.
   - 主鋼結構門型排架已安裝完成。

- Measure the bolt hole distance between two adjacent main steel columns and compare the actual distances found with the relevant distances for the bolted connections on the main steel bracing beams. Compare the measurements found with the actual length of the respective goalpost row bracing beam.
- 測量兩相鄰主鋼柱之間的螺栓孔距離，並將實際測量值與主鋼結構橫向支撐樑上螺栓連接的相關距離進行比較。同時，將測量值與各門型排架列橫向支撐樑的實際長度進行比對。

- It is advisable to erect the scaffolding for the goalpost rows together with the bracings in order to prevent clashes and provide good access to the bracings during erection.
- 建議在吊裝架設橫向支撐樑時，同時搭設門型排架列的施工架，以避免干涉並提供良好的橫向支撐樑施工作業通道。

#### 釋放後續作業 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，即可釋放以下作業：

   - Erection of loose casing panels.
   - 散裝爐牆氣密鋼板的吊裝架設。

#### 吊裝架設 Erection

- Erect main steel structure bracing beams between each main steel structure portal.
- 在每個主鋼結構門型排架之間，吊裝架設主鋼結構橫向支撐樑。

#### _Note:_
注意事項
- Erect shims between the bracing beam and the main steel column connection support, at the correct location.
- 在支撐樑與主鋼柱連接支撐之間，於正確位置安裝墊片。
- Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening (see 60031-730-01-008).
- 施加正確的扭力值進行螺栓鎖固（請參閱60031-730-01-008）。
- Splices in bolted connections are not permitted.
- 螺栓連接處不允許搭接。
- When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment of the bolt holes can only be made after consultation with the manufacturer.
- 當檢測到螺栓孔未對準時，螺栓孔的調整需與原廠協商後方可進行。

#### Quality control
品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的FQP和/或程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_
注意事項
- Verify the bracings are erected correctly and according the drawings.
- 確認支撐件已依圖說正確安裝施工。
- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有未完成項目，請列出清單後放行。

### 8.1.5. 門型排架組件的對心校準與螺栓扭力鎖固 Alignment and bolt torqueing of goalpost row assembly

#### a. Alignment
a. 對心校準
- Final alignment of main steel portals needs to be executed with loose guy wires. (if still in place)
- 主鋼結構門型排架的最終對心校準需在拉索鬆弛狀態下執行。（若拉索仍存在）
- For tolerances see (60031-730-06 drawing series)
- 公差請參閱（60031-730-06系列圖說）

#### _Note :_
注意事項
- Verify alignment of the main steel portals during final alignment from “inside” of the goalpost rows.
- 在最終對心校準時，請從門型排架的「內部」確認主鋼結構門型排架的對心校準狀況。
- Strong advice / recommendation from the manufacturer is to take the necessary time for alignment and verification of the main steel structure to be within the tolerances specified. Erection of the HRSG with a properly aligned steel structure will be easier, quicker and result in higher overall quality.
- 原廠強烈建議，務必預留足夠時間進行主鋼結構的對心校準與驗證，以確保其在規範的公差範圍內。若HRSG的鋼結構對心校準得當，將使安裝施工更輕鬆、更快速，並提升整體品質。
- Tolerances on the drawings are given to the X and Y direction with + or -.
- 圖說上的公差值以X軸和Y軸方向的「+」或「-」表示。
- Final alignment needs to be performed to one side + or - and shall be equal for the complete main steel structure.
- 最終對心校準需以單一方向的「+」或「-」為基準，並確保整個主鋼結構的對心校準一致。
- - Contact the manufacturer in case of deviations.
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫原廠。

#### b. Final bolt torqueing
b. 最終螺栓扭力鎖固
- Perform a final bolt torque verification for the goal post row assembly
- 對門型排架組件執行最終螺栓扭力驗證。

#### _Note :_
注意事項
- Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening (see 60031-730-01-008)
- 施加正確的扭力值進行螺栓鎖固（請參閱60031-730-01-008）。
- Splices in bolted connections are not permitted
- 螺栓連接處不允許搭接。
- Use the correct bolt material and length, according the applicable bolt list.
- 請依據適用的螺栓清單，使用正確的螺栓材質與長度。
- Contact the manufacturer in case of deviations.
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫原廠。

#### c. Quality control
c. 品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的FQP和/或程序執行品質管制活動。

### 8.1.6. 汽鼓支撐樑 Drum supporting beams
Before installation of the drum supporting beams can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在汽鼓支撐樑的施工作業開始之前，需預先完成一些準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions
準備工作與前提條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前段所述的文件與程序需已備妥並經由負責單位（或相關單位）審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP - Module installation complete.
- 下列準備工作/活動需已完成，並在FQP中簽核「模組安裝完成」。

- Measure the distance between the top girders and length of the drum supporting beams. _Note:_
- 測量頂部大樑之間的距離以及汽鼓支撐樑的長度。注意事項：

   - These measurements are required in order to determine the thickness of the shims to be installed.
   - 這些測量數據是用來決定所需安裝墊片的厚度。

#### Release subsequent activities
後續活動放行
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Drum installation.
- 本段所述活動成功完成後，將放行下列活動：- 汽鼓安裝。

#### Installation
安裝

- Install drum supporting beams. _Note:_
- 安裝汽鼓支撐樑。注意事項：

   - Install shims between the drum support beam and top girder support on the correct location.
   - 在汽鼓支撐樑與頂部大樑支撐之間，於正確位置安裝墊片。

   - Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening.
   - 施加正確的扭力值進行螺栓鎖固。

   - Splices (gaps) in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing.
   - 螺栓連接處不允許有搭接（間隙），除非圖說另有標示。

   - When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment of the bolt holes can only be made after consultation with the manufacturer.
   - 當檢測到螺栓孔未對準時，螺栓孔的調整需與原廠協商後方可進行。

- Make a survey report for the actual elevations of the drum support beams.
- 針對汽鼓支撐樑的實際高程進行測量報告。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的最終品質計畫書 (FQP) 和/或相關程序，執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意：_ _Note:_

- Verify the supports are installed correctly according the drawings before installing the drums.
- 在安裝汽鼓之前，請確認支撐件已依照圖面正確安裝。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何未完成項目，請列出清單並予以放行。

### 8.1.7. Transverse bumper supports
Before installation of the transverse bumper supports can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
### 8.1.7. 橫向防撞支撐件
在橫向防撞支撐件的施工作業開始之前，需要預先準備一些活動。

#### 準備工作與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前一段落中提及的文件和程序必須到位，並經由負責單位（或相關單位）審查。

#### 後續活動放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Transverse bumper installation
- 本段落中的活動成功完成後，將放行以下活動： - 橫向防撞件安裝

- Installation
- 安裝

- Install transverse bumper supports. _Note:_
- 安裝橫向防撞支撐件。 _注意：_

- Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening.
- 螺栓鎖緊時，請施加正確的扭力值。

- Splices (gaps) in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing.
- 螺栓連接處不允許有接縫（間隙），除非圖面另有標示。

- When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment of the bolt holes can only be made after consultation with the manufacturer.
- 若發現螺栓孔未對準，僅能在與原廠協商後進行調整。

- Make a survey report for the actual elevations of the transverse bumper supports.
- 針對橫向防撞支撐件的實際高程進行測量報告。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的最終品質計畫書 (FQP) 和/或相關程序，執行品質管制活動。

#### _注意：_ _Note:_

- Verify the supports are installed correctly according the drawings before installing the transverse bumpers.
- 在安裝橫向防撞件之前，請確認支撐件已依照圖面正確安裝。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何未完成項目，請列出清單並予以放行。

### 8.1.8. 汽鼓中心固定鋼結構 Drum centre fixation steel

The erection of the drum centre fixation steel is described in Chapter 9: drum erection.
汽鼓中心固定鋼結構的吊裝架設作業，詳述於第九章：汽鼓吊裝。

The erection of the drum centre fixation steel is executed after final alignment of the drums.
汽鼓中心固定鋼結構的吊裝架設作業，應在汽鼓最終對心校準後執行。

### 8.1.9. 熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構最終檢查 Final inspection of the HRSG main steel

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate.
當特定系統或特定組件群的機械吊裝架設作業完成後，應進行檢查。未完成項目應彙整成未完成項目清單，並附於最終檢查證明書。

The Final inspection Certificate of the HRSG main steel describes the systems or components inspected.
熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構的最終檢查證明書，應說明所檢查的系統或組件。

#### 檢查 Inspection

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.
- 最終檢查證明書上所提及的所有系統或特定組件群，均應進行最終檢查，以確認吊裝架設正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.
- 若有任何未完成項目，應在現場巡檢後立即建立記錄。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :
- 若有未完成項目清單，應將其分類為：

- Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)
- 需在水壓試驗前解決的項目 (A類項目)

- - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)
- - 需在熱試運轉前解決的項目 (B類項目) - 需在臨時驗收 (PAC) 前解決的項目 (C類項目)

#### _注意：_ _Note:_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認相關系統的適用現場最終品質計畫書 (FQP) 已由所有相關方簽署。未完成項目應列入未完成點清單。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認所有不符合報告 (NCR) 均已結案。未完成項目應列入未完成點清單。

#### 8.2.
#### 8.2.

#### 主鋼結構施工架 Scaffolding for main steel structure

This paragraph describes the scaffolding erection for the boiler main steel goalpost rows. The scaffolding is positioned on the outside of the columns, along the complete length of the columns for the boiler left and right side main steel structure.
本段落說明鍋爐主鋼結構門型排架的施工架搭設作業。施工架應設置於鍋爐左右兩側主鋼結構的柱子外側，沿著柱子的完整長度。

### 8.2.1. 門型排架施工架（右側 / 左側）「外側」 Scaffolding goalpost rows (right / left) “outside”

Work method statements / risk assessments for scaffolding erection shall be prepared by the erection contractor. All scaffolding built to be as per Method statement applicable.
施工架搭設的施工方法說明書 / 風險評估應由吊裝架設承攬商準備。所有搭設的施工架均應符合適用的施工方法說明書。

#### a. 吊裝架設 a. Erection

- Scaffolding to be erected on the “outside” of the goalpost rows on the right and left side. Properly plan the erection of scaffolding along the HRSG main steel structure in order to minimize rebuild requirements once Erecting casing, secondary steel and piping.
- 施工鷹架應架設在左右兩側「門型排架 (Goalposts)」的外側。請妥善規劃沿著熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 主鋼結構架設鷹架，以盡量減少在吊裝爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing)、二次鋼結構 (Secondary steel) 和蒸汽管路 (Piping) 後，需要重新搭設的需求。

#### _備註：_ _Note:_

- Erect the scaffolding in such a way that the main staircase and the top platform can be easily erected and without interference.
- 鷹架的架設方式應確保主樓梯和頂部平台能夠輕鬆架設，且不受任何干擾。

- Scaffolding need to be suitable for erection of the main steel bracings, casing panels, secondary steel platforms, piping and piping supports.
- 鷹架需適用於主鋼結構斜撐、爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板、二次鋼結構 (Secondary steel) 平台、蒸汽管路 (Piping) 及管路支撐的吊裝架設作業。

#### b. 品質管制 (QC) b. Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用的最終品質計畫書 (FQP) 和/或相關程序書執行品質管制 (QC) 活動。

#### _備註：_ _Note:_

- Periodically inspect scaffold for safety & falling hazards and apply “green/red card system”
- 定期檢查鷹架是否存在安全及墜落危險，並實施「綠/紅卡系統」管理。

- Inspections and rebuilds by authorized personnel only
- 僅限經授權人員方可進行檢查和重新搭設作業。

## 8.3. 爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) (底部及側壁面板) Casing (bottom and side wall panels)

This paragraph describes the erection of the casing panels.
本段落說明爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板的吊裝架設作業。

### 8.3.1. 概述 General

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the casing panels shall be prepared by the erection contractor.
爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板的吊裝架設作業，其施工方法說明書/風險評估報告及吊裝計畫應由吊裝承攬商 (Erection contractor) 準備。

The erection sequence for the casing panels is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板的吊裝架設順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 8.3.2. 文件與程序 Documents and procedures

Documents and procedures required for erection of the casing panels .
爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板 吊裝架設所需的相關文件與程序。

- Work method statement : Erection boiler casing panels
- 施工方法說明書：鍋爐爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板吊裝架設

- - Work method statement : Erection elevated work platform (inside boiler)
- - 施工方法說明書：高空作業平台吊裝架設 (鍋爐內部)

- - Work method statement : Scaffolding
- - 施工方法說明書：鷹架搭設

- - Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.
- - 螺栓扭力鎖固程序：非壓力部件。

- - FQP : HRSG boiler casing
- - 最終品質計畫書 (FQP)：熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 鍋爐爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing)

- - WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts
- - 銲接程序規範書 (WPS) / 銲接程序檢定記錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格檢定 (WPQ)：非壓力部件

- Weld typical / record
- 典型銲接圖 / 銲接記錄

- Welding consumable handling procedure
- 銲材處理程序

   - : Non-pressure parts
   - ：非壓力部件

   - : Non-pressure parts
   - ：非壓力部件

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格：非壓力部件

### 8.3.3. 底部面板 Bottom panels

Erect the bottom panels on all the boxes, except the vertical bottom panels on the outside goalpost rows (HRSG front and rear side), as well as the vertical panels at the SCR duct.
除了熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 前後側外部門型排架 (Goalposts) 上的垂直底部面板，以及選擇性觸媒還原脫硝系統 (SCR) 煙道處的垂直面板外，所有箱體上的底部面板均應進行吊裝架設。

These panels shall be placed after erection of the modules.
這些面板應在模組吊裝架設完成後再行安裝。

Before and during erection of the casing panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板吊裝架設之前及期間，部分作業需提前準備。

Parallel to the erection of the casing panels other activities can be carried out.
在爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板吊裝架設的同時，其他作業亦可同步進行。

#### 準備與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落中提及的文件與程序需到位，並經由負責單位 (或相關單位) 審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備/作業需已完成，並在適用情況下於最終品質計畫書 (FQP) 中簽核。

   - Erection and alignment of main steel structure
   - 主鋼結構件 (Main steel structure) 的吊裝架設與校準

- Scaffolding for access to the boiler “bottom inside”.
- 進入鍋爐「底部內部」的鷹架。

#### _備註：_ _Note:_

   - Before erection of the bottom casing panels can start, prepare scaffolding for access to the boiler “bottom inside”.
   - 在底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板吊裝架設開始前，請準備進入鍋爐「底部內部」的鷹架。

   - Place the scaffolding on the outside of the goalpost rows. Scaffolding to be built-up from ground level to the top of the bottom girder.
   - 將鷹架架設在門型排架 (Goalposts) 的外側。鷹架應從地面搭設至底部大樑的頂部。

   - Provide access from both the left and right side of the boiler.
   - 應從鍋爐的左側和右側提供進出通道。

- Use and apply plywood on the bottom casing panels.
- 在底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板上使用並鋪設夾板。

#### _備註：_ _Note:_

- Prepare the plywood panels (for protection of the bottom panels) during the pre-assembly of the goalpost rows for the boiler main steel.
- 在鍋爐主鋼結構的門型排架 (Goalposts) 預組裝期間，準備夾板 (用於保護底部面板)。

- To avoid damaging of the boiler casing panels liner sheeting use plywood panels. Erect the plywood panels during erection of the bottom panels.
- 為避免鍋爐爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板的不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 受損，請使用夾板。在底部面板吊裝架設期間，同時架設夾板。

- Open the plywood panels during the fit-up and weld activities, but keep the panels as closed to each other as far as possible.
- 在組裝和銲接作業期間，請打開夾板，但盡可能讓面板彼此保持密合。

- Plywood on the bottom panels liner sheeting needs to be in place until the end of the construction phase.
- 底部面板不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 上的夾板需保持在位，直到施工階段結束。

- After finalizing the inside bottom casing, modify the plywood in such a way that the “floor is protected” during further erection.
- 在完成內部底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 後，請修改夾板，使其在後續吊裝架設期間能「保護地板」。

- Cut holes in the plywood for piping activities and close the holes until the relevant piping is erected.
- 在夾板上切割孔洞以進行蒸汽管路 (Piping) 作業，並在相關蒸汽管路 (Piping) 吊裝架設完成前，將孔洞封閉。

   - Plywood erected shall be checked for correct erection, acceptance by the manufacturer.
   - 已架設的夾板應檢查其架設是否正確，並經製造商驗收。

- Elevated platform (after erection of the bottom casing and during or after the erection of the sidewall casing).
- 高空作業平台 (在底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 吊裝架設完成後，以及在側壁爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 吊裝架設期間或之後)。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- An elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler is useful for erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.
- 在鍋爐內部設置高空作業平台（吊籃）有助於在爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 側壁絕緣現場接縫處進行內部絕緣的吊裝架設。

- Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.
- 高空作業平台的吊裝架設可在側壁爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板吊裝架設期間開始進行。

- Elevated platforms to be erected on both sides (right / left side) of the boiler in such a way that proper access along the complete length and height of the boiler sidewalls can be provided.
- 高空作業平台應在鍋爐的兩側（右側/左側）進行吊裝架設，以確保沿著鍋爐側壁的整個長度和高度都能提供適當的進出通道。

#### 後續活動的放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Insulation and liner sheeting bottom field splices.
- 本段落活動成功完成後，將放行以下活動：- 底部現場接縫的絕緣和不銹鋼內護板 (Liner Sheet) 施作。

   - Angle bar connections (where applicable).
   - 角鋼連接（如適用）。

   - Erection casing sidewall panels
   - 爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 側壁面板的吊裝架設

#### 吊裝架設 Erection

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom casing panels. _Note:_
- 吊裝架設、組裝並點銲底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板。_注意事項：_

   - Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.
   - 在吊裝架設前，請從爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 穿孔處移除塑膠和絕緣棉。請使用刀具正確切割塑膠和絕緣棉。切勿用力拉扯。
