   - First erect a single bottom panel on the HRSG front or rear side.
   - 首先在熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 的前側或後側吊裝架設一塊底部面板。

   - Align the panel to the correct position and bolt the U-channels to the girders.
   - 將面板對準正確位置，並將U型槽鋼螺栓固定到大樑上。

   - DO NOT MOVE THE PANEL from the aligned position.
   - 請勿將面板從已對準的位置移動。

   - Erect and align the consecutive panels to the first erected panel bolting the U-channels to each other only.
   - 吊裝架設並將後續面板與第一個已吊裝架設的面板對齊，僅將U型槽鋼相互螺栓固定。

   - Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the bottom panels.
   - 從底部面板上切除內部絕緣保護塑膠。

   - Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.
   - 組裝並點銲面板，確保無間隙。根據圖面要求，在需要處使用填補板。

   - - During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
   - - 在點銲作業期間，請使用銲接毯覆蓋絕緣棉，以防止火花飛濺。

   - Erect the remaining bolts and nuts. When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.
   - 吊裝架設剩餘的螺栓和螺帽。如果發現螺栓孔未對準，調整只能在諮詢製造商後進行。

   - Use taper washers for the connection to the U-channels.
   - 連接到U型槽鋼時，請使用錐形墊圈。

#### 底部面板的銲接作業 Welding bottom panels

- Weld the bottom casing panels _Note:_
- 銲接底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板。_注意事項：_

   - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
   - 請遵循圖面和銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中關於銲接作業的詳細說明和/或典型要求。

   - All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.
   - 所有外部銲道應為連續銲，不允許在外部進行斷續銲。

   - Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see the details on drawings.
   - 斷續銲僅允許在內部接頭處進行，尺寸請參閱圖面上的詳細說明。

   - For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.
   - 對於所有槽鋼端部，銲道應為連續銲。

   - During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
   - 在銲接作業期間，請使用銲接毯覆蓋絕緣棉，以防止火花飛濺。

#### 底部面板的現場零件 Field parts bottom panels

- Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary field parts.
- 吊裝架設、組裝並點銲所有必要的現場零件。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Field parts for the bottom casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.
- 底部爐牆氣密鋼板 (Casing) 面板的現場零件可以是填補板、導向板和加勁板。請根據圖面指示識別所有所需的現場零件。

- Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings.
- 請遵循現場零件圖面上銲接典型的要求。

- All gaps at corners have to be closed (seal welded) using filler plates (6 mm thickness).
- 所有角落的間隙必須使用填補板（厚度6毫米）封閉（密封銲接）。

#### 底部面板現場零件的銲接作業 Welding field parts bottom panels

- Weld all erected field parts.
- 銲接所有已吊裝架設的現場零件。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.
- 請遵循圖面上關於銲接作業的詳細說明和/或典型要求。

- All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welding on the outside allowed.
- 所有外部銲道應為連續銲，不允許在外部進行斷續銲。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 根據適用的現場品質計畫 (FQP) 和/或程序執行品質管制 (QC) 活動。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

   - Check fit-up of the bottom panels before welding.
   - 在銲接作業前，請檢查底部面板的組裝狀況。

   - Erection of the internal insulation after release without a list of outstanding items (if any).
   - 在放行後，進行內部絕緣的吊裝架設，且不應有任何未完成項目清單（如果有的話）。

- 8.3.4. Side wall panels
- 8.3.4. 側牆板

The described erection for Side wall panels is set-up generally and applies for all Side wall panel erection works. Parallel to the erection of Side wall panels, other activities can be carried out.
本文件所述之側牆板吊裝架設作業為一般性說明，適用於所有側牆板的吊裝架設工程。在側牆板吊裝架設的同時，其他相關作業亦可同步進行。

Before and during erection of the Side wall panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在側牆板吊裝架設之前及期間，部分作業需事先準備。

#### 準備工作與前提條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序需已備妥，並經由負責單位(或相關單位)審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，並依適用情況於FQP(最終品質計畫書)中簽署確認。

   - Installation and alignment of main steel structure.
   - 主鋼結構件的施工作業與校準。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).
   - 材料已收料並完成數量與品質清點(OSD報告)。

- Scaffolding for access to the boiler “inside”.
- 進入鍋爐內部的施工架。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Place the scaffolding on the inside of the main steel structure. Scaffolding to be built-up from ground level to the top girder.
- 將施工架設置於主鋼結構件內部。施工架需從地面搭建至頂部大樑。

- When there is no scaffolding available, an elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler can be useful for inside casing welding and erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.
- 若無施工架可用，可使用鍋爐內部的升降工作平台(吊籠)，以便進行爐牆氣密鋼板內部的銲接作業，以及爐牆側板保溫現場接縫處的內部保溫材安裝。

- Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.
- 升降工作平台的吊裝架設可在側牆爐牆氣密鋼板板片吊裝架設期間開始進行。

#### 後續作業放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，將放行下列後續作業：

   - Insulation and liner sheeting field splices.
   - 保溫材與不銹鋼內護板現場接縫。

   - Angle bar connections (where applicable).
   - 角鋼連接(如適用)。

#### 吊裝架設 Erection

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the Side wall panels. _Note:_
- 吊裝架設、組裝並點銲側牆板。 _注意事項：_

   - Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as indicated on the drawings.
   - 依圖面所示，確認組裝高程與公差。

   - Before welding, remove the plastic and insulation wool where required. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.
   - 銲接前，依需求移除塑膠膜與保溫棉。使用刀具正確切割塑膠膜與保溫棉。請勿用力拉扯。

   - Align the panel to the correct position. Do not move the panel from the aligned position.
   - 將板片校準至正確位置。請勿將板片從已校準的位置移動。

   - In case of a welded connection between two adjacent panels erect and align the consecutive panels to the first aligned panel.
   - 若為兩相鄰板片之間的銲接連接，請將後續板片吊裝架設並校準至第一個已校準的板片。

   - In case of a UNP to UNP connection between two adjacent panels, bolt the two channels together prior to welding.
   - 若為兩相鄰板片之間的UNP對UNP連接，請在銲接前將兩個槽鋼螺栓連接。

   - Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.
   - 組裝並點銲板片，確保無間隙。依圖面所示，必要時使用填縫板。

   - During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
   - 點銲期間，請使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

#### 側牆板銲接作業 Welding Side wall panels

- When alignment and final position of the Side wall panels is achieved and verified for correctness, weld the Side wall panel field splices.
- 當側牆板的校準與最終位置已達成並確認無誤後，即可進行側牆板現場接縫的銲接作業。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds are allowed.
- 所有外部與內部銲道均應連續，不允許斷續銲。

- For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.
- 所有槽鋼端部的銲道均應連續。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS closely, as these may differ per location. (E.g. inside welding, outside welding or seal welding of panels).
- 請嚴格遵循圖面與WPS(銲接程序規範)上所示的銲接細節或典型，因為這些可能因位置而異。(例如：內部銲接、外部銲接或板片的密封銲接)。

- During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
- 銲接期間，請使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

#### 現場組件 Field parts

- Fit up and tack-weld all necessary field parts. _Note:_
- 組裝並點銲所有必要的現場組件。 _注意事項：_

   - Field parts for the casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.
   - 爐牆氣密鋼板板片的現場組件可為填縫板、導板與加勁板。請依圖面所示，識別所有所需的現場組件。

   - - Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners / U-channels, need to be installed using the correct weld preparation.
   - - 導板/加勁板/U型槽鋼的交叉點與連接點，需使用正確的銲接坡口進行安裝。

   - - Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings. - All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded), using filler plates (6 mm thick).
   - - 請遵循現場組件圖面上的銲接典型要求。 - 所有角落與現場接縫處的間隙都必須使用填縫板(6毫米厚)封閉(密封銲接)。

#### 爐牆氣密鋼板板片現場組件銲接作業 Welding field parts casing panels

- Weld all fitted-up field parts. _Note:_
- 銲接所有已組裝的現場組件。 _注意事項：_

   - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings.
   - 請遵循圖面上的銲接細節或典型。

   - All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.
   - 所有外部銲道均應連續，不允許外部斷續銲。

   - Except for the cover plates for the penetrations of the header strand jacks These can only be installed after removal of strand jacks.
   - 集管箱鋼絞線千斤頂穿孔的蓋板除外，這些蓋板只能在鋼絞線千斤頂移除後才能安裝。

#### Quality control
品質管制 (QC)

   - Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). _Note:_
   - 依據適用的FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序書，執行品質管制作業。注意事項：

      - Check alignment, elevation and dimensions and tolerances of the casing panels before welding.
      - 銲接前，檢查爐牆氣密鋼板 (casing panels) 的對心、高程、尺寸及公差。

      - - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
      - - 若有未完成項目，應列出清單後方可放行。

- 8.3.5. Top wall casing panels (included in the boiler harp module) The Top wall casing panels are implemented and lifted with the boiler harp modules. The top wall casing panels are to be welded gastight to the bottom flanges of the top girders, the side wall panels by means of angle bar and strip connections and the field splice between each top casing panel is closed by means of a T-bar or strip. The described erection for Top wall casing panels is set-up generally and applies for all Top wall casing panel erection works. Parallel to the erection of Top wall casing panels, other activities can be carried out. Before and during erection of the Top wall casing panels, some activities need to be prepared in advance. Preparations and preconditions • The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 8.3.5. 頂部爐牆氣密鋼板 (包含於鍋爐管排模組內) 頂部爐牆氣密鋼板將與鍋爐管排模組一併安裝及吊裝。頂部爐牆氣密鋼板需與頂部大樑的下翼板、側牆板透過角鋼及鋼帶連接方式進行氣密銲接，而各頂部爐牆氣密鋼板之間的現場接合處則透過T型鋼或鋼帶封閉。上述頂部爐牆氣密鋼板的吊裝架設方式為通用原則，適用於所有頂部爐牆氣密鋼板的吊裝架設作業。在吊裝架設頂部爐牆氣密鋼板的同時，其他作業亦可同步進行。在吊裝架設頂部爐牆氣密鋼板之前及期間，部分作業需提前準備。準備工作與前提條件 • 前述段落提及之文件及程序書需已備妥，並經由負責單位審查。

- • The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. - Installation and alignment of boiler harp modules. - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).
- • 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，並在FQP (現場品質計畫) 中簽核 (如適用)。 - 鍋爐管排模組的安裝與對心。 - 材料已收料並完成數量及品質清點 (OSD報告)。

#### Release subsequent activities
後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Filler plates goal post rows - Angle bar connections (where applicable). - T-bar or strip connection between separate top casing panels - Insulation and liner sheeting field splices.
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，將放行下列作業： - 門型排架 (goal post rows) 填充板 - 角鋼連接 (如適用)。 - 各頂部爐牆氣密鋼板之間的T型鋼或鋼帶連接 - 保溫層及不銹鋼內護板 (liner sheeting) 現場接合。

- Erection • Erect, fit and tack-weld the Top wall casing panels. _Note:_ - Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as indicated on the drawings. - Before welding, remove the plastic and insulation wool where required. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force.
- 吊裝架設 • 吊裝、組裝並點銲頂部爐牆氣密鋼板。注意事項： - 依圖面所示，確認組裝高程及公差。 - 銲接前，依需求移除塑膠膜及保溫棉。請使用刀具正確切割塑膠膜及保溫棉，切勿用力拉扯。

- - Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing. - During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
- - 組裝並點銲鋼板，確保無間隙。依圖面需求使用填充板。 - 點銲作業期間，使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

- Welding Top wall casing panels • When alignment and final position of the Top wall casing panels is achieved and verified for correctness, weld the Top wall casing panel field splices. _Note:_ - All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds are allowed. - For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous. - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS closely, as these may differ per location. (E.g. inside welding, outside welding or seal welding of panels).
- 頂部爐牆氣密鋼板銲接作業 • 當頂部爐牆氣密鋼板的對心及最終位置已達成並確認無誤後，進行頂部爐牆氣密鋼板的現場接合銲接。注意事項： - 所有外部及內部銲道均應連續，不允許斷續銲接。 - 所有槽鋼端部之銲道均應連續。 - 請嚴格遵循圖面及銲接程序書 (WPS) 中關於銲接細節或典型圖的指示，因為這些可能因位置而異。(例如：內部銲接、外部銲接或鋼板的密封銲接)。

- - During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
- - 銲接作業期間，使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

- Field parts • Fit up and tack-weld all necessary field parts. _Note:_ - Field parts for the casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings.
- 現場組件 • 組裝並點銲所有必要的現場組件。注意事項： - 爐牆氣密鋼板的現場組件可為填充板、導向板及補強板。請依圖面所示，識別所有所需的現場組件。

- - Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners / U-channels, need to be installed using the correct weld preparation.
- - 導向板/補強板/U型槽鋼的交叉點及連接點，需採用正確的銲接坡口進行安裝。

- - Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings. - All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded), using filler plates (6 mm thick).
- - 請遵循現場組件圖面中銲接典型圖的要求。 - 所有角落及現場接合處的間隙，必須使用填充板 (6毫米厚) 進行封閉 (密封銲接)。

- Welding field parts casing panels
- 爐牆氣密鋼板現場組件銲接作業

- • Weld all fitted-up field parts. _Note:_ - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings. - All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed. - Except for the cover plates for the penetrations of the header strand jacks These can only be installed after removal of strand jacks.
- • 銲接所有已組裝完成的現場組件。注意事項： - 請遵循圖面中關於銲接細節或典型圖的指示。 - 所有外部銲道均應連續，不允許外部斷續銲接。 - 集管箱 (header) 鋼絞線千斤頂穿透處的蓋板除外，這些蓋板只能在鋼絞線千斤頂移除後才能安裝。

- Quality control • Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). _Note:_ - Check alignment, elevation and dimensions and tolerances of the casing panels before welding. - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 品質管制 (QC) • 依據適用的FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序書，執行品質管制作業。注意事項： - 銲接前，檢查爐牆氣密鋼板 (casing panels) 的對心、高程、尺寸及公差。 - 若有未完成項目，應列出清單後方可放行。

### 8.3.6. 門型排架 (goal post rows) 填充板 Filler plates goal post rows

Filler plate connections are the plates placed to fill the gap located at each goalpost row bottom side for the main steel structure boiler, between two adjacent sidewall panels.
填充板連接是指放置於鍋爐主鋼結構架 (main steel structure boiler) 各門型排架 (goalpost row) 底部，介於兩相鄰側牆板之間的間隙，用以填補該間隙的板件。

Sealing plate connections are used as filler plates and provide gas tightness in boiler duct at these locations, once the angle bar connections are erected.
密封板連接作為填充板使用，一旦角鋼連接安裝完成，即可在這些位置提供鍋爐煙道內的氣密性。

#### Preparations and preconditions
準備工作與前提條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件及程序書需已備妥，並經由負責單位審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，並在FQP (現場品質計畫) 中簽核 (如適用)。

   - Erection of bottom and side wall casing panels
   - 底部及側牆爐牆氣密鋼板的吊裝架設。

#### Release subsequent activities
後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，將放行下列作業：

   - Angle bar connections
   - 角鋼連接

#### Erection
吊裝架設

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the filler plates for each goalpost row bottom side, between two adjacent sidewall panels on the left and right side.
- 吊裝、組裝並點銲各門型排架 (goalpost row) 底部，介於左右兩側相鄰側牆板之間的填充板。

#### _Note:_
注意事項：

- Fit the filler plates to fill the complete existing gap at the required locations for each goalpost row.
- 組裝填充板，以完全填補各門型排架 (goalpost row) 所需位置的現有間隙。

#### Welding filler plate connections
填充板連接銲接作業

- Weld the filler plate connections.
- 銲接填充板連接。

#### _Note:_
注意事項：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 請遵循圖面及銲接程序書 (WPS) 中關於銲接細節或典型圖的指示。

- During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
- 銲接作業期間，請使用防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 請依據適用的FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制作業。

- 8.3.7. Angle / flat bar connections and T-bar connections (general)
- 8.3.7. 角鋼/扁鋼連接件與T型鋼連接件 (通則)

Angle / flat bar and T bar connections are the connections used at corner and straight casing field splices. Angle / flat bar connections provide in boiler duct gas tightness and rigidness at these locations.
角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件主要用於爐牆外殼的轉角處及直線段的現場接合。這些角鋼/扁鋼連接件能確保鍋爐煙道在這些位置的氣密性與結構剛性。

#### 準備工作與前置條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落中提及的文件與程序，需已備妥並經由負責單位(或相關單位)審查確認。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，並在FQP (現場品質計畫) 中簽認(如適用)。

   - Installation of subsequent casing panels.
   - 後續爐牆外殼板的安裝。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report).
   - 材料已收料並完成數量與品質清點 (需有OSD報告)。

#### 後續作業放行 Release subsequent activities

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 本段落所述作業成功完成後，即可放行下列後續作業：

   - Insulation and liner sheeting casing panels.
   - 爐牆外殼板的保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝。

#### 吊裝架設 Erection

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the angle / flat bar and T-bar connections at the relevant field splice location.
- 在相關的現場接合位置，吊裝、組裝並點銲角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Align the angle / flat bar and T-bar connection to the casing panel without gap.
- 將角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件與爐牆外殼板對齊，確保無間隙。

- Angle / flat bar and T-bar connection cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation. For details see the drawings.
- 角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件的斷面及連接點，需依據正確的銲接坡口進行架設。詳細資訊請參閱圖面。

#### 角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件的銲接作業 Welding angle / flat bar and T-bar connections

- Weld all angle / flat bar and T-bar connections.
- 銲接所有角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- All external and internal welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed.
- 所有外部與內部銲道均應連續，外部不允許有斷續銲。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 請依據圖面及銲接程序書 (WPS) 中的銲接細節或典型作法執行。

- During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.
- 銲接作業期間，請使用防火毯覆蓋保溫棉，以防止火花飛濺。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 請依據適用的FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制作業。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

   - Check fit-up of the angle / flat bar and T-bar connections before welding.
   - 銲接前，請檢查角鋼/扁鋼與T型鋼連接件的組裝密合度。

   - Release for internal insulation with a list of outstanding items (if any).
   - 內部保溫作業可放行，並附上待辦事項清單 (如適用)。

- 8.3.8. Internal insulation and liner sheeting boiler casing (general)
- 8.3.8. 鍋爐外殼的內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝 (通則)

Installation of internal insulation and liner sheeting for field splices, can be performed after respective casing panels are installed and corner connections have been finished. The installation is based on chapter “ _Internal insulation and liner sheeting”_ .
現場接合處的內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝，可在相關爐牆外殼板安裝完成且轉角連接件施工完畢後進行。此安裝作業應依據「 _內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝_ 」章節的規定。

#### 吊裝架設 Erection

- For casing internal insulation and liner sheeting erection, follow the steps and requirements stipulated in chapter “Internal insulation and liner sheeting”.
- 爐牆外殼的內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板的吊裝架設，請遵循「內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝」章節中規定的步驟與要求。

#### 品質管制 (QC) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 請依據適用的FQP (現場品質計畫) 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制作業。

#### _注意事項：_ _Note:_

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 放行時需附上待辦事項清單 (如適用)。

- Quality control for the internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on chapter 7.3:
- 內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板的品質管制，應依據第7.3章節：

   - “Internal insulation and liner sheeting”.
   - 「內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝」。

## 8.4. Secondary steel components 二次鋼結構
### 8.4.1. General 通則

Erection of the secondary steel components is based on the description in chapter 13 “Secondary steel” 
二次鋼結構的吊裝施工應依據第 13 章「二次鋼結構」之說明。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the secondary steel components shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
安裝施工承攬商應針對二次鋼結構的吊裝施工，準備施工計畫書 (WMS) / 風險評估及吊裝計畫。

The erection sequence for the secondary steel components is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
二次鋼結構的吊裝順序如文件 60031-730-05-001 所示。

### 8.4.2. Erection of Boiler top platforms (partly) 鍋爐頂部平台安裝 (部分)

Before erection of the top platforms can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始進行頂部平台吊裝之前，需提前做好部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- Verify the possibility of which parts of the top platform can be erected before loading modules with reference to the locations of the platform parts. 
- 請配合平台部件的位置，確認在裝載模組之前，有哪些頂部平台部件可以先進行吊裝。

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前段所述之文件與程序書皆需準備就緒，並經負責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，且如適用時應於施工品質計畫 中簽收。

   - Pre-fabrication secondary steel components 
   - 二次鋼結構組件之預製

   - Main steel erected 
   - 主鋼結構已吊裝完成

#### Erection 吊裝架設

- Erect the pre-assembled platforms only at the right and left side of the goalpost rows. The top platforms at the front and rear side of the boiler will be erected, after erection of the inlet and outlet duct. 
- 僅在門型架排的左右兩側吊裝預先組裝完成的平台。鍋爐前後側 the 頂部平台將於入口與出口煙道吊裝完成後方進行吊裝。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_ 

- With all involved / affected parties properly coordinate the exact location and erection of the top platforms erected at this stage. 
- 與所有相關與受影響之單位妥善協調整個階段所吊裝頂部平台的確切位置與吊裝施工。

### 8.4.3. Boiler staircase 鍋爐樓梯

Before erection of the top platforms can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始進行樓梯吊裝之前，需提前做好部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前段所述之文件與程序書皆需準備就緒，並經負責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，且如適用時應於施工品質計畫 中簽收。

   - Pre-fabrication secondary steel components 
   - 二次鋼結構組件之預製

#### Erection 吊裝架設

- Lift the already pre-assembled staircase parts into final position. 
- 將已頂定預組完成的樓梯部件起吊至最終定位位置。

- For erection follow the erection steps and requirements stipulated in the chapter 13“ _Secondary steel”_ . 
- 吊裝施工請遵循第 13 章「 _二次鋼結構_ 」中所規定之步驟與要求。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Execute the lifting works according the applicable WMS instructions. 
- 請依據適用的施工計畫書 (WMS) 說明執行起吊作業。

#### Quality control 品質管制 (QC)

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 請依據適用的施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制作業。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Release without any outstanding items. 
- 放行時不得有任何待辦事項 (Outstanding items)。

## 8.5. Transverse bumpers 橫向緩衝器

This paragraph describes the erection of the transverse bumpers. 
本段落說明橫向緩衝器的吊裝施工作業。 

### 8.5.1. General 通則

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the transverse bumpers shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
安裝施工承攬商應針對防震擋塊 (橫向緩衝器) 的安裝施工，準備施工計畫書 (WMS) / 風險評估及吊裝計畫。

The erection sequence for the transverse bumpers is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
橫向緩衝器的吊裝順序如文件 60031-730-05-001 所示。

### 8.5.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序書

Documents and procedures required for erection of the transverse bumpers . 
橫向緩衝器吊裝施工所需的文件與程序書。

|-|Work method statement|:  Erection transverse bumpers.|
|---|---|---|
|—|施工計畫書|：橫向緩衝器安裝施工|
|-|FQP|:  HRSG boiler modules|
|—|施工品質計畫|：熱回收蒸汽產生器鍋爐模組|
|-|WPS / PQR / WPQ|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|—|WPS / PQR / WPQ|：非受壓件銲接程序書|
|-|Weld typical / record|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|—|典型銲道圖 / 銲接紀錄|：非受壓件|
|-|Welding consumable handling procedure|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|—|銲材管理程序書|：非受壓件銲接|
|-|NDE procedures / personnel qualifications|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|—|非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序書 / 檢測人員資格證明|：非受壓件|

### 8.5.3. Transverse bumper erection per row 每排橫向緩衝器之吊裝施工

Before erection of the transverse bumpers can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始進行橫向緩衝器之吊裝施工之前，需提前做好部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前段所述之文件與程序書皆需準備就緒，並經負責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，且如適用時應於施工品質計畫 中簽收。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已運抵現場並完成數量與外觀品質檢驗 (OSD 開箱報告)

- Bumpers and supports 
- 緩衝器與其支架

   - Transverse bumpers are positioned on each row as indicated on the drawings. Transverse bumpers and the corresponding guide plates are indicated by numbering and material group marking, for each row. 
   - 橫向緩衝器應依圖示擺放在每排。每排的橫向緩衝器與對應的導向板均有編號與材質特性標示。

   - Check the bumper supports for correct position and level 
   - 檢查緩衝器支架定位與水平度是否正確。

   - Verify having the correct bumper number and material marking group for each position. 
   - 確認每個位置的緩衝器編號與材質特性與圖面標示相符。

   - Store the bumpers, including the guide plates together for each row. 
   - 每排擺放的緩衝器（含導向板）應集中妥善存放。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- In case of any deviation regarding the bumper preparation, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若發現緩衝器的準備工作有任何異常偏差，請立即與原廠聯繫。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Module erection. 
- 當本節之工作成功完成並查驗合格後，可放行以下後續施工： - 模組吊裝。

   - Temporary storage of baffles and sealing plates 
   - 擋風板 (導流板) 與密封板之臨時存放。

#### Erection transverse bumpers per row 每排橫向緩衝器之吊裝施工

- Erect the transverse bumpers. 
- 吊裝橫向緩衝器。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

   - Start with the erection of the lowest transverse bumper for each row and continue the erection from top to bottom for that row. Erect all bumpers per row. 
   - 從每排位置最低的橫向緩衝器開始吊裝，並在該排依序由下至上進行吊裝。吊裝每排的所有緩衝器。

   - After erection of a bumper adjust respective bumper for correct position. 
   - 各該擺放就定位後，請調整其對位。

   - Finalize each bumper as described before starting with the next bumper, this to avoid accidents during the erection. 
   - 為防吊裝施工發生意外事故，在開始安裝下一組緩衝器前，需先完全固定或定位前一組。

   - Maintain a free gap between the bumper support and the bumper. Transverse bumpers are to be adjusted to the correct location between the bumper supports. For each row, the free gap (indicated with “A”) required is indicated on the drawing. 
   - 緩衝器支吊架與緩衝器本體之間需保持自由間隙。橫向緩衝器需微調至各支吊架間的正確位置。每排所需的自由間隙 A 值各載於圖面中。

   - Once positioned, the bumper shall touch the bumper support over the complete surface. 
   - 一旦定位，緩衝器應與支吊架之接觸面完全貼合。

   - In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer. 
   - 如有任何偏差，請立即聯繫原廠。

- Erect the guide plate at both bumper ends. 
- 在緩衝器兩端安裝導向板。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Weld the bumper guide to the bumper only. 
- 緩衝器導架僅能與緩衝器之本體進行銲接。

#### Welding guide plate 導向板銲接作業

- Weld the guide plate. 
- 進行導向板銲接。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.. 
- 請遵循銲接程序規格書 (WPS) 及圖面的大樣與細節要求。

#### Quality control 品質管制 (QC)

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 請依據適用的施工品質計畫 及相關程序書執行品質管制工作。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- The free gap “A” mentioned on the drawings shall be verified. 
- 圖面所載之自由間隙 A 值需進行現場驗證。

- Verify that the guide plate is not welded to the bumper support 
- 驗證導向板絕無與緩衝器支承座銲死

- Release without a list of outstanding items. 
- 工作放行時應無任何待辦事項 (Outstanding items)。

#### _Note :_ ## _注意事項：_

- Manufacturer shall review the actual survey report of the gap between the bumper ends and inner liner sheeting according the applicable tolerance drawings. 
- 原廠應審查緩衝器端部與不銹鋼內護板之間，其間隙之現場實際量測報告，量測需符合適用的公差圖面。

### 8.5.4. Final inspection of the transverse bumpers 橫向緩衝器完工現場檢驗學檢

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或某組特定組件之機械安裝施工作業完成後，應進行完工檢驗。若有任何待辦事項 (Outstanding items)，皆需彙整於待辦事項清單 (OIL) 中，並作為完工檢驗證書的附件。

The Final inspection Certificate of the transverse bumpers describes the systems or components inspected. 
橫向緩衝器完工檢驗證書應載明已檢驗合格之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 現場檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 所有列載於完工檢驗證書中的系統或特定組件群組，均應進行完工現場驗收，以確認其安裝無誤、完整且無任何損傷。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 於步檢 (Walk-down) 完工查勘後，應立即建立待辦事項表 (若有)。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若適用待辦事項，其分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - A類項目：在進行水壓試驗前，必須改善並結案之項目

   - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) 
   - B類項目：在熱試俥 (Hot-commissioning) 開始之前，必須改善並結案之項目

   - - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
   - C類項目：在臨時驗收證書 (PAC) 簽署前完成即可之項目

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 請驗收確認涉及該等系統之適用施工品質計畫 均已由各方會簽。所有未結案事項必須彙整於待辦項目清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 驗證所有不符合報告 (NCR) 均已完成结案。未完結事項應一併列入待辦事項清單中。

## 8.6. Grouting goalpost rows main steel structure boiler 鍋爐主鋼結構門型架基礎灌漿安裝施工

Grouting erection is based on paragraph 7.2. 
無收縮水泥灌漿施工方法依據第 7.2 節之規定。

### 8.6.1. Grouting 基礎灌漿

Before pouring of the grouting can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始無收縮水泥灌漿基礎澆置之前，必須先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- Formwork and chipping of the concrete is to be prepared in advance. 
- 混凝土接觸面鑿毛與模板工程支設需提前施工完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列各項準備工作需已完成，且如適用時應於施工品質計畫 中會簽收訖。

   - Bottom and sidewall casing panels erected. 
   - 爐底與爐側牆外殼板已安裝完成。

   - Transvers bumpers erected 
   - 橫向緩衝器已安裝完成。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 當本節之工作成功完成並查驗合格後，可放行以下後續施工：

   - Erection of Modules. 
   - 模組吊裝。

#### Erection 吊裝施工作業

- Pour the grouting according the grouting procedure, paragraph 7.2 
- 依據第 7.2 節所述之灌漿工程程序書，澆置灌漿無收縮水泥。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Keep in mind the duration required for curing and testing of the grout. 
- 請留意水泥灌漿料養護 (Curing) 與抗壓強度試體檢驗所需之法定時間。

#### Quality control client 業主/現場品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 請依施工品質計畫 及相關程序書執行品質管制查驗。

#### _Note:_ ## _注意事項：_

- Check the grouting according the check sheet for grouting. 
- 請依據灌漿工程自主檢查單檢驗其灌漿品質。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 灌漿工程放行可隨附待辦事項（若有）。 

## 8.7. Module erection 模組吊裝

This paragraph describes the erection of the Modules. 
本節說明模組的吊裝。

### 8.7.1. General 通則

Module erection is an erection sequence with several preparation and erection activities linked to each other, which need to be executed for each box consecutively. 
模組吊裝為一項包含數個相互關聯之準備與安裝步驟的吊裝程序，必須針對每個箱體依序執行。

The sequence for the erection of the module is described in the following paragraphs and the erection sequence drawings (document 60031-730-05-001). 
模組的吊裝順序詳述於以下各節及吊裝順序圖面（文件編號 60031-730-05-001）。

Activities mentioned in this chapter are general and do not have to be applicable for all boxes. Erection details and requirements for each box can be found in the applicable drawings. 
本章所提之活動為一般性原則，未必適用於所有箱體。各箱體的吊裝細節與要求請參閱適用之圖面。

Specific requirements for the erection are mentioned in the relevant paragraph. 
吊裝之特定要求已於相關章節中敘述。

All the modules will be transported in a shipping frame to site. 
所有模組皆會裝載於運輸框架中運抵工地。

One hoisting beams for horizontal handling of modules is foreseen. 
已規劃一組用於模組水平搬運之起吊架。

One strong back with top hoisting frame to get the modules from horizontal to vertical position is foreseen. 
已規劃一組附有頂部起吊框架的強背架，用以將模組從水平位置翻轉至垂直位置。

One top spreader beam for the main crane and one tail spreader beam for the tail crane are foreseen. 
已規劃一組用於主起重機的頂部扁擔樑，以及一組用於尾車起重機的尾部扁擔樑。

To avoid the bundle shipping frame – strong back combination from tumbling, a temporary connection to the main steel is provided. 
為防止管束運輸框架與強背架組合傾倒，設有至主鋼構的臨時連接。

The modules shall be erected from the top (top loaders). 
模組應自頂部吊入安裝（頂部裝載式）。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for erection of the modules shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
吊裝承攬商應編製模組吊裝之施工說明書/風險評估及吊裝計畫書。

### 8.7.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序書

Documents and procedures required for erection of the modules . 
模組吊裝所需之文件與程序書。

|-|Work method statement|:  Erection modules.|
|-|施工說明書|: 模組吊裝。|
|---|---|---|
|---|---|---|
|-|Work method statement|:  Erection scaffolding modules.|
|-|施工說明書|: 模組施工架搭設。|
|-|FQP|:  HRSG boiler modules.|
|-|施工品質計畫|: 複循環鍋爐 (HRSG) 模組。|
|-|Bolt torque procedure|:  Non pressure parts.|
|-|螺栓扭力鎖緊程序書|: 非受壓件。|
|-|WPS / PQR / WPQ|:  Non-pressure parts|
|-|銲接工藝規格書 (WPS) / 銲接程序資格檢定報告 (PQR) / 銲工資格檢定證明書 (WPQ)|: 非受壓件|
|-|Weld typical / record|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|-|典型銲道 / 銲接紀錄|: 非受壓件。|
|-|Welding consumable handling procedure|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|-|銲材管理程序書|: 非受壓件。|
|-|NDE procedures / personnel qualifications|:  Non-pressure parts.|
|-|非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序書 / 人員資格證明|: 非受壓件。|

### 8.7.3. Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

Proper preparation before and during the module erection is essential for a safe, smooth and high quality erection of the modules. Before erection of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
模組吊裝前及吊裝期間的妥善準備，對於確保模組安全、順暢且高質量的吊裝至關重要。在開始模組吊裝之前，必須提前準備好某些活動。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述章節所提及之文件與程序書必須準備就緒，並已由權責方（或各方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 以下準備工作/活動必須完成，且若適用，須在施工品質計畫 中簽認。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已點收並進行數量及品質檢驗（材料異常 OSD 報告）

   - grouting of main steel 
   - 主鋼構之無收縮水泥灌漿

- Piping bottom panels (temporary storage): Temporarily store the piping (spools) which are available on site temporarily on the bottom casing panels. Piping (spools) delivered in a later stage, are brought into position via the boiler basement open front and rear sides. 
- 底部面板管路（臨時存放）：將目前已運抵工地的管路（管段）臨時存放在底部爐牆外殼板上。後續階段交貨的管路（管段）則經由鍋爐底座開放的前側和後側運送至定位。

#### _Note:_ 註：

   - Ensure storage is performed on plywood only and that the plywood panels remain properly positioned. 
   - 確保僅存放於合板上，並使合板維持在正確的位置。

   - Store the bottom piping in such a way that proper access to the basement boxes is still provided. 
   - 存放底部管路時，應確保仍留有適當通道以利進入基礎底座箱體。

   - Where possible store the bottom piping as low as possible, using the casing penetrations. 
   - 盡可能利用爐牆外殼板之穿孔處，將底部管路維持在最低高度存放。

- Temporary spacers under disc springs of suspensions: 
- 懸吊系統碟形彈簧下方之臨時填隙片：

Check if the temporary spacers under the disc springs are removed before lifting the module in vertical position. 
於模組垂直吊裝前，檢查碟形彈簧下方之臨時填隙片是否已拆除。

- Strong back and top hoisting frame: 
- 強背架及頂部起吊框架：

   - For erection of the strong back and top hoisting follow the steps and requirements stipulated in the chapter “Secondary steel” and the applicable drawings. 
   - 關於強背架與頂部起吊框架之組立，請遵循「二次鋼構」章節及相關圖面所規定之步驟與要求。

#### _Note:_ 註：

   - Level the area for the strong back and top hoisting frame. 
   - 將強背架與頂部起吊框架之作業區域整平。

   - The strong back and top hoisting frame parts are delivered completely fabricated and only require assembly on site. The strong back and top hoisting frame parts consist of a frame parts, beams, cables and shackles. 
   - 強背架與頂部起吊框架構件係以完全預製狀態運抵現場，僅需於現場進行組裝。強背架與頂部起吊框架構件包含框架本體、樑、鋼索及卸克（吊環）。

   - Pre-assemble the strong back and top hoisting frame according the requirements stipulated on the drawings. 
   - 依照圖面規定之要求，預組裝強背架與頂部起吊框架。

   - Verify the correct identification plate is present on the strong back frame. 
   - 確認強背架上具備正確之銘牌。

   - Validate marking and validity of the marking for lifting equipment (e.g. CE marking) for the strong back and top hoisting frame (if applicable). 
   - 驗證強背架與頂部起吊框架之起重設備標識及其有效性（如適用時之 CE 標識）。

   - Check all strong back and top hoisting frame material for integrity and absence of damages. 
   - 檢查所有強背架與頂部起吊框架材料之完整性，並確認無損壞情形。

   - In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

- Module hoisting beam for lifting modules: 
- 用於吊裝模組之模組起吊樑：

Execute the pre-assembly of the hoisting beam for lifting of the modules into the strong back frame. 
執行起吊樑之預組裝作業，以便將模組吊入強背架內。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- The hoisting beam parts are delivered completely fabricated and only require assembly on site. The hoisting beam parts consist of a frame, beams, cables, shackles and chains. 
- 起吊樑構件係以完全預製狀態運抵現場，僅需於現場進行組裝。起吊樑構件包含框架、樑、鋼索、卸克（吊環）及鏈條。

- Pre-assemble the hosting beam according the requirements stipulated on the drawings. 
- 依照圖面規定之要求，預組裝起吊樑。

- Verify the correct identification plate is present on the hoisting beam. 
- 確認起吊樑上具備正確之銘牌。

- Validate marking and validity of the marking for lifting equipment (e.g. CE marking) for the hoisting beam (if applicable). 
- 驗證起吊樑之起重設備標識及其有效性（如適用時之 CE 標識）。

- Verify all chains are of the same length.
- 確認所有鏈條長度均一致。

- Check all module hoisting beam material for integrity and absence of damages.
- 檢查所有管束模組起吊樑之材質完整性，確認無任何損傷。

- In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer.
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

### 8.7.4. Unloading / loading of modules 模組的裝卸車與卸載作業

#### Unloading / loading of modules 模組的裝卸車與卸載作業

Before unloading / loading of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始模組裝卸車與卸載作業前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述章節提及之文件與程序書皆須備妥，並經權責單位審核完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作與活動必須完成，且若適用時，須在施工品質計畫 中簽核完成。

   - Preparations for erection of modules ready
   - 模組安裝準備工作就緒

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Module erection per box
- 本章節活動順利完成後，即釋放後續相關作業：- 各箱模組安裝作業

#### Connecting the hoisting beam 連接起吊樑

- Connect the module hoisting beam to the shipping frame of the module on the SPMT.
- 將模組起吊樑連接至位於自行式模組運輸車 (SPMT) 上之模組運輸架。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Before connecting, verify the module condition to be without damages, or other abnormalities.
- 連接前，請確認模組狀態無損傷或其他異常情形。

- Verify the module to have the correct numbering and position. The module position in the strong back is depending on which box will be loaded from which side.
- 確認模組編號與位置正確。模組於強背架內之位置，取決於安裝箱體之裝載方向。

#### Loading of the modules onto the strong back and top hoisting frame 將模組裝載至強背架與頂部起吊框架

- Lift the module including shipping frame onto the strong back and connect the shipping frame to the strong back and top hoisting frame.
- 將包含運輸架之模組吊升至強背架上，並將運輸架連接至強背架與頂部起吊框架。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Loading of the modules onto the strong back can commence only when the strong back area is levelled. 
- 必須在強背架區域完成水平校正後，方可進行模組裝載至強背架之作業。

- Use the correct bolt material and torque values for bolting the connections on the top part. 
- 頂部連接處之螺栓鎖固，須使用正確材質之螺栓及扭力值。

- When loaded once more check the module to have the correct numbering and position. 
- 模組裝載後，應再次確認其編號及位置是否正確。

- Verify the module to be loaded as per the drawing instructions. 
- 須依照圖面說明，核對待裝載之模組。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若發生任何偏差或失效情形，請立即聯繫製造商。

- During unloading / loading frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape. 
- 於裝卸車過程中，應頻繁檢查設備狀態，確保其保持良好工況。

- During unloading / loading do not rush the connection process to avoid damaging of the modules. 
- 於裝卸車過程中，切勿倉促進行連接程序，以避免損壞模組。

### 8.7.5. 

#### Module erection per box 每箱體模組吊裝作業

Module erection can be started from the front and rear side of the HRSG, depending on the HRSG lay-out, delivery sequence and crane plan. The sequence for module erection per box shall be properly communicated to all parties involved. 
模組吊裝作業可視廢熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 之佈置、交貨順序及起重機吊裝計畫，選擇從前方或後方開始。每箱體模組之吊裝順序須與所有相關單位充分溝通。

Before erection of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始模組吊裝作業前，需預先完成各項準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與作業程序須準備就緒，並經負責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認（若適用）。

   - Preparation for module erection. 
   - 模組吊裝準備。

   - Unloading / loading of modules 
   - 模組之裝卸車與卸載作業

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 待本段落作業順利完成後，即予釋放並執行後續活動：

- Module alignment per box 
- 每一模組箱之管束模組對心作業

#### Unloading / loading of the modules 模組的裝卸車與卸載作業

- Unloading of the modules from the truck and loading onto the strong back frame, based on paragraph 8.8.5: “unloading/loading of modules” 
- 依據第 8.8.5 節「模組的裝卸車與卸載作業」之規定，執行模組由拖車卸載及安裝至強背架上之作業。

#### _Note:_ _註記：_

- In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若遇任何偏差或故障，請立即聯繫製造廠商。

- During unloading / loading frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape. 
- 於裝卸期間，應頻繁檢查設備狀況，確保設備處於良好狀態。

- During unloading / loading do not rush the connection process to avoid damaging of the modules. 
- 於裝卸期間，切勿倉促執行連接作業，以免造成管束模組損壞。

#### Erection of modules 模組吊裝作業

- Erect the modules per box. 
- 依照模組箱編號逐一進行吊裝。

#### _Note:_ _註記：_

- Follow the erection sequence as mentioned on the drawing for loading of the modules. 
- 執行模組吊裝時，應遵循圖面所示之安裝順序。

- Transfer the strong back module combination from horizontal to vertical position using a main and tail crane. Main crane is connected to the top hoisting frame and tail crane is connected to the bottom of the strong back. 
- 利用主吊車及尾車吊車，將結合強背架之管束模組由水平位置翻轉至垂直位置。主吊車連接於頂部起吊框，尾車吊車則連接於強背架底部。

- Once in vertical position connect the strong back to the temporary connections on the main steel. 
- 當模組轉至垂直位置後，將強背架連接至主鋼構之臨時連接點。

- Disconnect the top hoisting frame from the strong back and disconnect the module from the shipping frame. 
- 解除頂部起吊框與強背架之連接，並解除管束模組與運輸框之連接。

- Lift the module with use of the top hoisting frame into the boiler and connect the module suspension beams to the main steel. 
- 使用頂部起吊框將管束模組吊入爐內，並將模組懸吊樑連接至主鋼構。

- Be sure that during the erection of each module all the shims are erected and the bolted connections between the module suspension beams and the main steel structure are completely tightened before the crane is disconnected. 
- 於各模組吊裝期間，須確保所有墊片均已安裝定位，且在拆除吊車鋼索前，模組懸吊樑與主鋼構間之螺栓接頭均已完全鎖緊。

- Alignment of the modules will be performed in a later stage. 
- 管束模組之對心作業將於後續階段執行。

- Do not rush the erection of the modules and avoid unnecessary damaging of the modules. 
- 切勿倉促執行模組吊裝，並避免對管束模組造成不必要之損壞。

- In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若遇任何偏差或故障，請立即聯繫製造廠商。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

### 8.7.6. Sound baffles, sidewall gas baffles and attic baffles per row (if applicable) 各列隔音板、側牆導流板及頂棚導流板（如適用）

Temporarily erect/store the (pre-assembled) baffles per row at or near their final location, after acceptance of the transverse bumper erection per row.
在各列橫向緩衝器安裝驗收後，於各列最終安裝位置處或附近，暫時吊裝/存放（預組裝的）導流板。

Erection of the baffles per row shall be based on paragraph “Sound baffles” and/or “Module sidewall gas baffles”.
各列導流板之安裝作業應基於「隔音板」及/或「模組側牆導流板」章節規定執行。

The typical sequence for the erection of the baffles per row per row is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
各列導流板之典型安裝順序詳如文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 8.7.7. Scaffolding per row 各列施工架

Erect the scaffolding per row after acceptance of the transverse bumper erection per row and acceptance of the sound baffles / attic baffles and side wall gas baffles, where applicable.
於各列橫向緩衝器安裝驗收，且隔音板/頂棚導流板及側牆導流板（如適用）安裝驗收完成後，始得進行各列施工架之搭設。

The typical sequence for erection of the scaffolding per row is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
各列施工架之典型搭設順序詳如文件 60031-730-05-001。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Ensure the scaffold built is safe and provides access to the module surface, casing sidewalls, the sound baffles and the down comer piping.
- 確保施工架搭設安全，並能通達模組表面、爐牆外殼板側牆、隔音板及下降管管路。

- Properly coordinate building of the scaffolding to ensure the scaffold built will not interfere with final erection or assembly of materials in the vicinity.
- 妥善協調施工架搭設作業，確保施工架不會妨礙鄰近區域材料的最終安裝或組裝。

### 8.7.8. Alignment of the modules per box 各箱模組校正

Before alignment of the modules can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始模組校正作業前，需預先完成部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並由負責方（或各方）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動需完成，且如適用，須於施工品質計畫中完成簽認。

   - Modules per box erected.
   - 各箱模組安裝完成。

#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 隨本段落各項作業順利完成，下列活動將予以放行：

   - Connection plates top and bottom module headers.
   - 頂部與底部聯箱之連接板。

   - Module suspension sealing.
   - 模組懸吊密封。

   - Wrap around connections
   - 包覆式連接。

#### Alignment 校正

- Perform alignment of the modules per box.
- 執行各箱模組之對正作業。

- Alignment of modules per box can be performed in parallel with the remaining module erection works.
- 各箱模組之對正作業可與剩餘的模組吊裝工程同步進行。

- Align the modules to the correct position and elevation.
- 將模組對正至正確位置與標高。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Measure the elevations of the top and bottom header of the first row and verify the actual situation with the requirements as per drawing.
- 測量第一排上下聯箱之標高，並依據圖說要求核對現場實際狀況。

- Alignment of the modules is achieved by turning the nuts on the top of the module suspension rods. In order to achieve the correct elevation and position of the module headers, turn the nuts on the suspension rods clock or counter clockwise. It is important to have the measurements of the top header locations in order to determine which rods should be adjusted up or down in order to achieve the correct elevation.
- 模組之對正係透過旋轉模組吊桿頂部的螺帽來達成。為使模組聯箱達到正確標高與位置，請將吊桿上的螺帽進行順時針或逆時針旋轉。掌握頂部聯箱之量測數據至關重要，以判斷需調整哪些吊桿之升降，進而達成正確標高。

- When turning the nut on top of the suspension rods verify that the rod is static and not turning in, or out of the clevis at the clevis connection. For the required distances, see the drawings.
- 旋轉吊桿頂部螺帽時，務必確認吊桿維持靜止，且未於雙耳接頭處旋入或旋出。相關要求距離請參閱圖說。

- As most of the expansion is taking place at the bottom headers it is important to have the bottom headers levelled to the correct elevation. During adjustment of the nuts continuously verify the bottom header elevation.
- 由於絕大多數的熱膨脹發生於底部聯箱，確保底部聯箱水平於正確標高至關重要。調整螺帽過程中，須持續核對底部聯箱之標高。

- Verify the suspension rods are hanging straight.
- 確認所有吊桿皆保持垂直懸吊狀態。

- When a module is aligned, tack-weld the washer plate of the module suspension on the top, after which the second nut on top of suspension rod can be erected.
- 模組對正完成後，將頂部模組懸吊之墊圈板進行點銲，隨後即可安裝吊桿上的第二顆螺帽。

- Discuss the alignment sequence with the manufacturer to achieve the right alignment per box.
- 與製造商討論對正順序，以達成各箱正確之對正作業。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Perform alignment of the modules per box.
- 執行各箱模組之對正作業。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何遺留項目，須附上清單並予以放行。

- Manufacturer shall visually check the actual report of the measurements collected from the final alignment of the bundles to be in accordance with the applicable drawings.
- 製造商應目視檢查管束最終對正之實際量測報告，以確認符合適用圖說之規範。

### 8.7.9. Erection of modules consecutive boxes 8.7.9. 後續模組箱之吊裝作業

For erection of the, modules, down comer piping, sound baffles and scaffolding per box, repeat the previous steps as mentioned in this chapter under paragraph 8.7.1: “General” till paragraph 8.7.8: “Alignment of the modules per box”
- 關於各箱模組、下降管路、防音隔板及施工架之吊裝，請重複本章節第 8.7.1 節「概要」至第 8.7.8 節「各箱模組之對正」所述之步驟。

- 8.7.10. Connection plates top and bottom module headers 8.7.10. 上下模組聯箱之連接板

Before erection of the connection plates on top and bottom headers can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
- 在開始安裝上下聯箱之連接板前，須先行完成部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落所提及之文件與程序須已就位，並經權責單位（或相關方）審查核可。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作與活動須已完成，並依適用規定於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Module alignment. 
   - 模組對心作業。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行
#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, Iran for the following activity (activities) is given: - Shims between transverse bumpers. 
- 隨著本段落各項活動順利完成，下列活動准予放行：- 橫向緩衝器間之填隙片安裝。

#### Erection 安裝作業
#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect the connection plates on the top and bottom headers for the applicable modules. 
- 於適用之模組頂部與底部聯箱上安裝連接板。

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the mark numbers on the plates for correct erection. 
- 檢查板件上之標示號碼以確保正確安裝。

- In case of any deviation, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Quality control 品質管制
#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

   - Check the module header connection plates per box. 
   - 逐箱檢查模組聯箱連接板。

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
   - 若有遺留項目，須附帶清單予以放行。

- 8.7.11. Shims between transverse bumpers and module headers / wrap arounds 8.7.11. 橫向緩衝器與模組聯箱/包覆板間之填隙片
- 8.7.11. Shims between transverse bumpers and module headers / wrap arounds 8.7.11. 橫向緩衝器與模組聯箱/包覆板間之填隙片

Before erection of the shims between transverse bumpers and the module headers and wrap arounds can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝橫向緩衝器與模組聯箱及包覆板間之填隙片前，須預先準備相關活動。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落所提及之文件與程序須已就位，並經權責單位（或相關方）審查核可。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業項目必須已完成，並在施工品質計畫 中完成相關簽核（如適用）。

   - Module alignment. 
   - 模組對齊。 

   - Erection connection plates. 
   - 吊裝連接板。 

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料接收及數量與品質檢驗（OSD 報告）。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行
 
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection of wrap around fixations. 
- 本章節所述作業項目完成後，准予進行下列作業：- 包覆式固定件吊裝。 

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- The erection sequence for shims between the transverse bumpers and module headers / wrap arounds is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
- 橫向緩衝器與模組聯箱/包覆式結構間之墊片安裝順序，請參閱 60031-730-05-001 文件。 

- Fit and tack-weld the shims with temporary filler plates. 
- 安裝墊片並配合臨時填隙片進行銲接定位（假銲）。 

#### _Note:_ 註：

- To determine the correct position of the shims, verify the group marking number on the shims. 
- 為確認墊片的正確安裝位置，請核對墊片上的組別標記號碼。 

- Make sure modules per box are hanging plump before and “compressed” before taking measurements for shim erection. 
- 在進行墊片安裝測量前，務必確保各箱模組已懸吊垂直且處於「受壓」狀態。 

- Erect the shim plates as per the applicable drawings and tolerance drawings. 
- 依照適用圖面與公差圖面進行墊片安裝。 

It is very important to take into account the required free gap (for expansion possibilities) of headers and wraparounds. Carefully read the notes for shimming on the tolerances drawings. 
- 務必考量聯箱與包覆式結構所需的預留間隙（以滿足熱膨脹需求）。請仔細閱讀公差圖面上關於墊片安裝的說明。 

- When necessary adjust the shim plates to the correct length. In this case, first contact the manufacturer. 
- 如有必要，應將墊片修整至正確長度。若需進行此作業，請先聯繫製造商。 

- Before erection of the shim, place a temporary filler plate with the required free gap thickness to the shim. This will ensure the correct free gap between the shim and the header or wrap-around is provided. 
- 在安裝墊片前，先放置一片具有所需間隙厚度的臨時填隙片。此舉可確保墊片與聯箱或包覆式結構之間能維持正確的預留間隙。 

- Check the tolerance as given on the tolerance drawings, during erection of the shims. 
- 在安裝墊片過程中，請隨時檢查公差圖面上規定的公差值。 

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all shims. 
- 銲接所有墊片。 

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中的細節說明與標準銲接規範。 

#### Quality control client 業主品質控制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). _Note:_
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。_註：_

   - Check the shim plate tolerances before final welding of the plate.
   - 於墊片進行最終銲接前，確認墊片公差。

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
   - 檢附未完成項目清單（若有）進行放行。

   - Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report of the measurements between the headers - transverse bumpers and the headers - shims (located on the transverse bumpers) to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.
   - 製造商應目視檢查並審閱聯箱與橫向緩衝器之間，以及聯箱與墊片（位於橫向緩衝器上）之間的實際測量報告，以確保符合相關的 60031-730-06 系列公差圖面。

### 8.7.12. Warp around fixations 包覆式固定件
- 
Before erection of the wrap around fixations can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
- 在開始安裝包覆式固定件之前，須預先完成部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
- 

• The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書必須已備妥，並由權責單位（或相關單位）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並依適用規定在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Erection shim plates.
   - 安裝墊片。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)
   - 材料進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（開箱檢驗報告 OSD report）。

#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續作業
- 

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given:
- 順利完成本段落之作業後，准予放行執行下列活動：

   - Erection internal shoulders.
   - 安裝內部肩部固定件。

#### Erection 安裝作業
- 

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the fixations. _Note:_
- 安裝、組配並點銲固定件。_註：_

   - Check for correct location of the wrap-around fixations, using the group marking number.
   - 使用分組標記編號，檢查包覆式固定件之安裝位置是否正確。

   - Check the dimensions between the two (2) holes of the fixations, before welding.
   - 於銲接前，檢查固定件兩個 (2) 孔洞之間的尺寸。

   - Check the drawings for exact location of the fixations.
   - 查閱圖面以確認固定件之精確安裝位置。

- In case of any deviation, contact manufacturer. 
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld all wrap around fixations. 
- 銲接所有環繞式固定件。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業請遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細部說明或典型範例。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the tolerances before welding. 
- 銲接前應先檢查公差。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有待辦事項，應於放行時附上清單。

### 8.7.13. Internal shoulders 內部支撐肩部

Before erection of the internal shoulders can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝內部支撐肩部之前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書必須備妥，並經權責單位審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，且若適用，需在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Side wall casing panels including insulation and liner sheeting 
   - 側牆爐牆外殼板（含保溫隔熱棉與不銹鋼內護板）

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已收料並完成數量與品質檢驗（溢短損報告 OSD）

#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續活動

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 待本節所述活動順利完成後，方可放行進行下列活動：

   - Locking of bundles (modules) 
   - 管束模組鎖固

#### Erection and alignment 安裝與對心作業

- Erect the top and bottom internal shoulders per box according theoretical dimensions on relevant shoulder drawings.
- 依據相關支承座圖面之理論尺寸，安裝各箱體之上部與下部內部支承座。

- Align the top and bottom internal shoulders.
- 執行上部與下部內部支承座之對心作業。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- The free gap “a”, as mentioned on the drawings, needs to present between the shoulder and the module header covers top and bottom.
- 圖面所述之自由間隙「a」，必須存在於支承座與上下部管束模組聯箱封頭之間。

- During erection of the shoulders, the free gap “a” can be achieved by erecting or removing shim plates.
- 於支承座安裝期間，可透過增減調整墊片來達成自由間隙「a」。

- The final free gap “a” shall be checked after erection of the shoulders and after erection of the internal top and bottom piping.
- 最終之自由間隙「a」應於支承座安裝完成，且內部上下部管路安裝完成後進行檢查。

- After the internal piping erection is completed and the free gap “a” is correct, erect the shoulder bolt connections for the slotted and fixed holes as per the typical.
- 待內部管路安裝完成且自由間隙「a」無誤後，依標準規範安裝支承座之長孔與固定孔螺栓連接。

- In case of any deviation, contact the manufacturer.
- 若有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制工作。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Verify the tolerances.
- 核對公差。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何待辦事項，應附上清單後放行。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements between header caps and the internal shoulders, according the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.
- 製造商應依據適用之 60031-730-06 系列公差圖面，目視檢查並審閱聯箱封頭與內部支承座間量測之實測報告。

### 8.7.14. Locking of bundles (modules) 管束（模組）之鎖定作業

Before locking of the bundles (modules) can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始進行管束（模組）鎖定作業前，需預先完成若干準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書必須到位，並由相關權責單位進行審閱。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/作業必須完成，並於適用時在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Erection of internal shoulders
   - 內部支承座安裝

- Erection of wrap around fixations 
- 包覆式固定件之安裝

- Erection of shim plates between transverse bumpers, module headers and wrap arounds 
- 橫向緩衝器、模組聯箱與包覆式固定件之間墊片之安裝

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 隨著本段落作業之順利完成，准予執行下列作業：

   - Erection of internal piping 
   - 內部配管之安裝

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect a temporary profile (angle) between the shoulders and the header covers of the top and bottom headers. 
- 於頂部與底部聯箱之肩部（shoulder）與聯箱蓋板之間架設臨時型鋼（角鋼）。

- Tack weld the profile to the shoulders in order to lock the bundles in the boiler widthwise direction, maintaining the free gap required. Do not weld to the header! 
- 將型鋼點銲於肩部，以固定管束於鍋爐寬度方向之位置，並維持所需之自由間隙。切勿銲接至聯箱本體！

#### _Note:_ 【註】：

- The modules were already locked in the boiler longitudinal direction using the temporary filling plates on the shims. Through the erection of these temporary profile (angle) the complete module bundle is locked in both the boiler width wise and the longitudinal direction, ensuring the free gap requirements to either side at all times during internal piping erection. 
- 模組先前已利用墊片上之臨時填隙片於鍋爐長度方向完成固定。透過這些臨時型鋼（角鋼）之安裝，完整的模組管束於鍋爐寬度與長度方向均已鎖定，確保在內部配管安裝期間，兩側均能隨時符合自由間隙之要求。

- Tack welding of the temporary profile to the shoulder to be performed in such a way that the weld can be easily removed in a later stage. 
- 臨時型鋼至肩部之點銲作業，應確保後續階段能輕易移除該銲道。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制作業。

#### _Note:_ 【註】：

- Check correct erection temporary profile. 
- 檢查臨時型鋼之安裝是否正確。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 檢附未結項目清單（如有）進行釋放。

### 8.7.15. Erection internal piping 內部配管之安裝

Boiler internal piping (interconnecting piping) erection can start after acceptance of the locking of the modules. Erection of the boiler internal (interconnecting) piping shall be based on chapter “Piping”. The typical sequence for the erection of the internal piping is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
鍋爐內部配管（互連配管）之安裝，得於模組固定作業經檢驗合格後開始。鍋爐內部（互連）配管之安裝應依據「配管」章節之規定辦理。內部配管安裝之典型順序請參考文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 8.7.16. Harp suspension sealing 蛇形管吊桿密封

Once the modules have been verified to be suspended and installed correctly the harp suspension rods located on the outside of the boiler can be closed of gastight. This is done by installing the harp suspension sealing on the outside on top of the boiler. 
一旦確認模組懸吊與安裝正確，即可進行鍋爐外部蛇形管吊桿之氣密封閉作業。此作業係透過在鍋爐頂部外部安裝蛇形管吊桿密封件來完成。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須已備妥，並經權責單位（或相關單位）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業須已完成，並依適用規定於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。

   - Verification of the harp bundle alignment for modules with temporary transport frames. 
   - 針對帶有臨時運輸架之模組，確認管束 (Harp bundle) 之對齊校準。

#### Installation 安裝作業

- Install the harp suspension sealing for all modules with temporary transport frames. 
- 安裝所有帶有臨時運輸架模組之懸吊管束密封件。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Carefully check the drawing to identify which box needs to filled with insulation. In case of boxes with disc springs no internal insulation shall be installed. 
- 請仔細查閱圖面以確認哪些箱體需填充保溫隔熱棉。若箱體內設有碟形彈簧，則不得安裝內部保溫隔熱棉。

- Before installation of the “harp suspension sealing box” place insulation between the channels all the way to the bottom. Do this is for all locations requiring insulation. 
- 於安裝「懸吊管束密封箱」前，應將保溫隔熱棉放置於槽鋼之間並填充至底部。所有需進行保溫之處皆應比照辦理。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the harp suspension sealing. 
- 銲接懸吊管束密封件。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings. 
- 銲接作業應遵循圖面上之細節要求或典型銲接規範。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有任何待辦事項，應於放行時附上待辦事項清單。

### 8.7.17. Final inspection of the module erection 模組安裝之最終檢驗

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢驗。待辦事項應彙整為清單，並附於最終檢驗證明書中。

The Final inspection Certificate of the modules with temporary transport frames describes the systems or components inspected. 
帶有臨時運輸架之模組，其最終檢驗證明書應詳細說明所檢驗之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.
- 最終檢驗證明書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件群組，均須進行最終檢驗，以確認其安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.
- 現場步檢結束後，應立即建立待辦事項清單（如有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :
- 若適用待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)
   - 於水壓試驗前須解決之項目（A類項目）

   - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items)
   - 於熱機試運轉前須解決之項目（B類項目）

   - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)
   - 於暫時驗收 (PAC) 前須解決之項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認相關系統之適用施工品質計畫 已由所有相關方簽署。待辦事項須納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。待辦事項須納入待辦事項清單中。

## 8.8. Casing (remaining components) 爐牆外殼板（剩餘組件）

This paragraph describes the erection of the remaining components for the casing.
本章節說明爐牆外殼板剩餘組件之安裝作業。

### 8.8.1. General 一般事項

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the remaining casing components shall be prepared by the erection contractor.
安裝承商須準備爐牆外殼板剩餘組件之安裝施工說明書、風險評估及吊裝計畫。

The erection sequence for the remaining casing components is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
爐牆外殼板剩餘組件之安裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 8.8.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the remaining casing components .
安裝爐牆外殼板剩餘組件所需之文件與程序：

- Work method statement : Erection boiler casing panels
- 施工說明書：鍋爐爐牆外殼板安裝

- Work method statement : Erection elevated work platform (inside boiler)
- 施工說明書：高空作業平台安裝（鍋爐內部）

- FQP : HRSG boiler casing
- 施工品質計畫：HRSG 鍋爐爐牆外殼板

- Bolt torque procedure : Non pressure parts.
- 螺栓扭力施工程序：非受壓組件

- Work method statement : Scaffolding
- 施工說明書：施工架

- WPS / PQR / WPQ : Non-pressure parts
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序檢定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工檢定紀錄 (WPQ)：非受壓組件

- Weld typical / record : Non-pressure parts
- 銲接典型圖說 / 紀錄：非受壓組件

- Welding consumable handling procedure : Non-pressure parts
- 銲接材料管理程序：非受壓組件

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications : Non-pressure parts
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件

### 8.8.3. Erection of vertical top and bottom casing panels rows D & F and H & M 垂直頂部與底部爐牆外殼板（D&F 排與 H&M 排）安裝

These vertical top and bottom panels are located on boiler inlet side and outlet side, as well as in the SCR area. Before erection of the vertical top and bottom panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
上述垂直頂部與底部爐牆外殼板位於鍋爐入口側與出口側，以及選擇性觸媒還原 (SCR) 區域。在開始安裝垂直頂部與底部爐牆外殼板前，須先行準備若干前置作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須備妥，並由負責方（或各負責方）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成相關簽核（若適用）。

   - Locking of modules for the applicable box 
   - 對應箱體模組之鎖定作業

- Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
- 材料進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（開箱檢驗報告 OSD Report）

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Internal insulation and liner sheeting. 
- 隨著本段落各項活動順利完成，下列活動准予放行：- 內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板安裝。

   - Final erection pipe bumpers. 
   - 最終管路緩衝器安裝。

#### Erection 安裝工程

- Erect the vertical top and bottom panels with angle bar connections (where applicable). 
- 安裝垂直上下側之爐牆外殼板，並配合角鋼連接（適用處）。

- Fit and tack-weld the panels. 
- 對準面板並進行點銲固定。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Align the casing panels and in this stage only tack-weld. The panels need to be in line and parallel to each other. 
- 將爐牆外殼板對正，此階段僅執行點銲。面板需保持對齊且相互平行。

- Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force. 
- 安裝前，移除爐牆外殼板貫穿處之塑膠膜與保溫隔熱棉。應使用刀具適當切割塑膠膜與隔熱棉。切勿強行拉扯移除。

- Align the panels to the correct position. 
- 將面板對準至正確位置。

- Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the top panels. 
- 切除頂部面板內側的保溫保護塑膠膜。

- During tack welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection. 
- 點銲期間，須使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉，以進行火花防護。

- During erection of the vertical top and bottom casing panels do not forget to temporarily erect the pipe bumpers. Prior to erection, fill the pipe bumpers with insulation wool. For erection instructions for pipe bumpers, see paragraph 8.9.5. 
- 安裝垂直上下側爐牆外殼板時，切勿遺忘臨時安裝管路緩衝器。安裝前，須於管路緩衝器內填充保溫隔熱棉。管路緩衝器之安裝說明請參閱第 8.9.5 節。

#### Welding of the panels 面板銲接

- Weld the casing panels to the angle bar connections. 
- 將爐牆外殼板銲接至角鋼連接處。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 應遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之銲接細節或典型施工說明。

- All external welds shall be continuous, no stich welds on the outside allowed. 
- 所有外部銲道均須為連續銲，外側嚴禁採用斷續銲。

- Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see details. 
- 斷續銲僅允許施作於內部接合處，尺寸請參閱細部圖。

#### Field parts erection top / bottom panels 現場組件安裝—頂部/底部板材

- Erect the guide / stiffeners to the outside right / left side casing panels. 
- 於爐牆外殼板之左右外側安裝導板/補強條。

- Fit and tack-weld the guide plates / stiffeners. 
- 進行導板/補強條之組裝及點銲固定。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Guide and stiffener plate cross and connection points need to be erected with the correct weld preparation. 
- 導板與補強條之交叉及連接點，於安裝時須具備正確的銲接坡口準備。

- All gaps at corners and field splices shall be closed (seal welded) using filler plates. (6 mm thickness). 
- 所有轉角處及工地接合處之縫隙，應使用填充板（厚度 6 mm）進行封閉（密封銲）。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld all field parts. 
- 銲接所有工地安裝之組件。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 應遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之銲接細節或典型施工說明。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the fit-up and alignment of the panels before welding. 
- 銲接前須檢查板材之組裝密合度與對正狀況。

- 8.9. HRSG baffles and sealing plates 8.9. 熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 導流板與密封板

This paragraph describes the installation of HRSG baffles and sealing plates. 
本段落說明熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 導流板與密封板之安裝作業。

### 8.9.1. General Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for installation of the HRSG baffle and sealing plates shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 8.9.1. 一般規定：安裝廠商應針對熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 導流板與密封板之安裝作業，編製施工計畫書、風險評估及吊裝計畫。

The erection sequence for the HRSG baffle and sealing plate is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 導流板與密封板之安裝順序請參閱文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 8.9.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for installation of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates .
安裝熱回收蒸汽產生器 (HRSG) 導流板及密封板所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement :  Installation HRSG baffles and sealing plates
- 施工計畫書：HRSG 導流板及密封板安裝
- Work method statement :  Installation scaffolding boiler casing
- 施工計畫書：鍋爐爐牆外殼板施工架搭設
- FQP :  HRSG baffles and sealing plates
- 施工品質計畫：HRSG 導流板及密封板
- WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格紀錄 (WPQ)：非受壓組件
- Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts
- 銲接標準圖 / 銲接紀錄：非受壓組件
- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts
- 銲接材料管理程序：非受壓組件
- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格證明：非受壓組件

### 8.9.3. Bumper sealing plates 緩衝器密封板

Sealing plates are located on the top and bottom transverse bumpers and pipe bumpers and fulfill the same purpose as the floor plates. Keeping the flue gas path and HRSG attic and basement boxes separated.
密封板位於頂部及底部橫向緩衝器與管路緩衝器上，其功能與底板相同。主要用途為將煙氣流道與 HRSG 頂棚及底部箱體進行隔離。

Before installation of bumper sealing plates can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始安裝緩衝器密封板之前，需先行完成部分作業準備。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備作業與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須已備妥，並由權責單位（或相關方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/作業必須已完成，且若適用時，須於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Removal of the temporary filler plates.
   - 拆除臨時填隙片。

#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection bumper end plates.
- 本段落作業順利完成後，方可放行下列作業：- 緩衝器端板吊裝安裝。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the bumper sealing plates.
- 吊裝、組對並點銲緩衝器密封板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- The given free space on the drawings is required for thermal expansion, check the actual situation and adjust (if necessary). See the applicable drawings for the correct tolerances.
- 圖面上標示之預留空間係考量熱膨脹所需，請現場確認實際狀況並於必要時進行調整。相關公差請參閱適用之工程圖面。

- The sealing plate connection point is used as a sliding point. During installation properly verify where the sliding point is located and only weld the parts indicated on the drawing.
- 密封板連接點作為滑動節點使用。安裝期間應確實核對滑動節點位置，並僅針對圖面所示部位進行銲接。

- The slotted holes in the plates are required for thermal expansion of the plate. See drawings for the correct tolerances.
- 板材上之長圓孔係為滿足板材熱膨脹所需。正確公差請參閱圖面。

- At the slotted hole connections the bolt connection shall be installed finger tight and tack welded, ensuring proper free movement during hot conditions. Metal contact between the connected parts however should exist.
- 於長圓孔連接處，螺栓連接應以手鎖緊至貼合後點銲，以確保熱態運轉時能自由移動。然而，連接組件間仍須保持金屬表面接觸。

- At the fixed points, all nuts shall be fully fastened and the bolt connection tack welded
- 於固定點處，所有螺帽均應完全鎖緊，並將螺栓連接處點銲固定。

- Verify the piece mark numbers for correctness during installation. 
- 於安裝過程中，請核對零件編號是否正確。

- In case of any deviation regarding free space or free gaps, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若空間或間隙出現任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all sealing plates and cover end plates. 
- 銲接所有密封板及端部蓋板。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業請遵循設計圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節與典型規範。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Check the bolt connections at sliding and fix points. 
- 檢查滑動端與固定點之螺栓連接。

- Check the slotted holes for correct tolerances. 
- 檢查長孔之公差是否正確。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 於放行時附上待辦事項清單（如有）。

#### Erection bumper end plates 安裝緩衝器端板

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the bumper end plates. 
- 吊裝、裝配並點銲緩衝器端板。

#### _Note:_ 註記：

- Fit the profile correctly to the sidewall liner sheeting without gap. 
- 將型鋼正確安裝至爐牆不銹鋼內護板上，不得留有間隙。

- During installation of the profile it is important to keep the given free gap as mentioned on the drawings. 
- 安裝型鋼時，務必維持圖面上標示之預留間隙。

- Tack weld the cover plates only as stated on the drawing and ensure free movement at the sliding point. 
- 僅得依設計圖說規定進行蓋板點銲，並確保滑動點之自由位移。

- In case of any deviation regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若預留間隙出現任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all sealing plates and cover end plates. 
- 銲接所有密封板及封端板。

#### _註：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 依據銲接施工圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型詳圖進行銲接。

#### 品質管制 Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或作業程序執行品質管制活動。

- _Note:_ - Check all free gaps before welding. 
- _註：_ - 銲接前須檢查所有預留間隙。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有待辦事項，須檢附待辦事項清單後方可放行。

### 8.9.4. 頂棚與底層導流板 頂棚與底層導流板位於熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 之頂棚與底層箱體內，其功用為減少這些區隔空間內的氣流旁通。此為垂直設置之密封板，將頂棚與底層箱體分割為數個封閉空間。 Attic and basement baffles The attic and basement baffles are located in the HRSG attic and basement boxes and serve the purpose of reducing bypass flow in these compartments. They are vertical sealing plates dividing the attic and basement boxes in several closed of compartments.

Before erection of the attic and basement baffles, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在進行頂棚與底層導流板之安裝作業前，需預先準備相關工作。

#### 準備工作與先決條件 Preparations and preconditions

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述章節提及之文件與程序須到位，並經權責單位審核完成。

- • The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. - HRSG internal piping installed. - Internal insulation HRSG attic and basement boxes installed - Bumper sealing plates installed 
- • 下列準備工作/作業須完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核：- HRSG 內部管路已安裝。 - HRSG 頂棚與底層箱體內部保溫已安裝。 - 緩衝器密封板已安裝。

- • All large attic and basement baffle materials were already stored in previous erection steps and are positioned in the basement boxes for the basement baffles and in the attic boxes for the attic baffles. 
- • 所有大型頂棚與底層導流板材料皆已於前階段安裝步驟中存放，底層導流板材料已置於底層箱體內，頂棚導流板材料則置於頂棚箱體內。

- • Identification of the baffle components. _Note:_ - All field installed baffle components have individual piece mark numbers for identification. These shall be checked prior to installation. 
- • 導流板組件識別。 _註：_ - 所有現場安裝之導流板組件均有個別之零件編號以供識別。安裝前須進行核對。

- - In case of any deviation contact the manufacturer. 
- - 如有任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

- • Measurements of the “boxes” for verification of sizes. _Note:_ - Before start erection carefully measure the “boxes” for sizing. During this measurement verification, it is important to exactly determine the location of the piping penetrations. 
- • “箱體”尺寸測量以進行驗證。 _註：_ - 安裝作業開始前，須仔細測量“箱體”尺寸。在此測量驗證過程中，精確確認管路穿孔位置至關重要。

- - In case of any deviations contact the manufacturer. 
- - 如有任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

- Erection • Erect, fit and tack-weld the baffles. _Note:_ - The baffles can be adjusted in the vertical and horizontal direction, but keep the free gaps and spaces as mentioned on the drawings. Compare the actual dimensions with the drawings. In case of major deviations, contact the manufacturer. 
- 安裝 • 安裝、組裝及點銲導流板。 _註：_ - 導流板可在垂直與水平方向進行調整，但須保持圖說所述之預留間隙與空間。應將實際尺寸與設計圖說進行比對。若有重大偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

- - For erection of the attic baffles, start with the bottom part on the top bumpers, align the baffles plates and verify presence of the free gaps and spaces. Secondly, erect the top part. Also, align the plates here and verify the free gaps and spaces available. 
- - 頂棚導流板安裝時，先安裝位於頂部緩衝器上之底部組件，對齊導流板並確認預留間隙與空間。其次，安裝頂部組件。同樣地，在此處對齊板件並確認預留間隙與空間。

- - For erection of the basement baffles, start with the top part on the bottom bumpers, align the plates and check the free gaps and spaces. Secondly, erect the bottom part. Also, align the plates here and verify the free gaps and spaces available. 
- - 底層導流板安裝時，先安裝位於底部緩衝器上之頂部組件，對齊板件並確認預留間隙與空間。其次，安裝底部組件。同樣地，在此處對齊板件並確認預留間隙與空間。

- - Carefully verify the cut-outs made on the baffle profiles during the assembly. Adjust when necessary - Check all dimensions according the tolerances drawings. 
- - 組裝期間須仔細核對導流板型材之開孔切口。必要時進行調整。 - 依據容許誤差圖說檢查所有尺寸。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld all the baffles. 
- 銲接所有導流板。

#### _Note:_ 備註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業請遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型施工要求。

- Check the free gap between the attic and basement baffles and the internal liner sheeting before welding. 
- 銲接前，請檢查頂棚導流板、基層導流板與內部不銹鋼內護板之間的自由間隙。

- Carefully control heat input during welding works, assuring no deformation of the plate material. 
- 銲接作業期間應謹慎控制熱輸入，確保板材不會發生變形。

#### Field components erection attic and basement baffles 現場組件之頂棚與基層導流板安裝

- Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing plates at each baffle pipe penetration.
