- 吊裝、組對並點銲各導流板管件貫穿處之密封板。

#### _Note:_ 備註：

   - Pipe sealing plates shall be installed in such a way that the pipe can move freely during hot conditions. 
   - 管路密封板之安裝方式應確保管路在熱態運轉時能自由位移。

   - In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

- Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles and respective connection plates. 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲密封角鋼及相對應之連接板。

#### _Note:_ 備註：

- Sealing angles are located on the sidewall liner sheeting on the right and left side wall and fixate the attic and basement baffles and reduce flue gas bypass flow. 
- 密封角鋼設置於左、右側壁之爐牆外殼板內護板上，用於固定頂棚及基層導流板，並減少煙氣旁通流。

- Fit the sealing angles to the sidewall liner sheeting without gap and as per drawing. The sealing angle shall touch the attic baffle. 
- 密封角鋼應與側壁不銹鋼內護板緊密貼合且無縫隙，並符合圖面要求。密封角鋼應與頂棚導流板接觸。

- It is important during the installation to verify the actual position of the sealing angles and maintain the required free gap to the casing. 
- 安裝過程中，確認密封角鋼之實際位置並維持其與爐牆外殼板間所需的自由間隙至關重要。

- Carefully verify the cut-outs made on the sealing angles during the pre-assembly. Adjust when necessary 
- 詳實核對預組裝階段於密封角鋼上所製作之切口，必要時進行調整。

- The connection plates shall only be tack welded and used as a sliding point, as per drawing, 
- 連接板僅能進行點銲，並依圖面要求作為滑動點使用。

- In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
- 若自由間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

#### Welding of the field components 現場組件之銲接

- Weld all installed field components. 
- 銲接所有已安裝之現場組件。

#### _Note:_ 
- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 應遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中關於銲接之細節或典型工法。

#### Quality control 
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 
- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 釋出時應附上未結項目清單（如有）。 

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the attic and basement baffles with internal liner sheeting.to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
- 製造商應進行目視檢查，並審閱頂棚及底部導流板與內部不銹鋼內護板之實際測量報告，以確保其符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列。 

### 8.9.5. Module sidewall gas baffles 模組側牆氣流導流板 

This paragraph describes the erection of the module sidewall gas baffles. 
本節敘述模組側牆氣流導流板之吊裝作業。 

Module sidewall gas baffles are located on the inside of the boiler duct along the complete height of the sidewalls. The baffles are positioned on the front and rear side and left and right side of each box that contains modules. 
模組側牆氣流導流板位於鍋爐煙道內側，沿側牆全高配置。導流板安裝於各個模組箱體的前、後及左、右側。 

Different kinds of sidewall gas baffles exist. For the different types, see the applicable module sidewall gas baffle drawings and the paragraphs in this chapter. 
側牆氣流導流板種類各異。關於不同類型，請參閱適用之模組側牆氣流導流板圖面及本章節相關段落。 

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the module sidewall gas baffles shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
吊裝承攬商應針對模組側牆氣流導流板之吊裝作業，準備施工計畫書/風險評估報告及吊裝計畫。 

The erection sequence for the module sidewall gas baffles is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
模組側牆氣流導流板之吊裝順序詳如文件 60031-730-05-001。 

Before erection of the module side wall gas baffles, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
於吊裝模組側牆氣流導流板前，需先行準備相關作業。 

#### Preparations and preconditions 

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書需到位，並經相關責任單位審查。 

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動需已完成，且如適用，應於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。 

   - Removal of all temporary erected filler plates and profiles (at top / bottom headers, wraparounds, pipe bumpers and internal shoulders). 
   - 拆除所有臨時安裝之填隙板及型鋼（位於頂部/底部聯箱、包覆結構、管排緩衝器及內部肩部處）。 

   - Internal piping (per box) erected. 
   - 內部管路（各箱體內）已吊裝完成。 

   - Modules free from any obstacles. 
   - 模組應淨空且無任何障礙物。 

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢核（缺損報告 OSD）。

#### Erection of type one (1) baffles and cover plates 第一型導流板與蓋板之安裝

- Fit and tack weld the baffle profiles (with stiffeners) located on the sidewall liner sheeting and fit the profile on the module side. Also, fit the cover plates on respective baffle profiles. 
- 安裝並點銲位於爐牆不銹鋼內護板上的導流板型鋼（含加勁肋），並安裝管束模組側的型鋼。同時，將蓋板安裝於各對應的導流板型鋼上。

#### _Note:_  _註：_

- Follow the notes on the applicable drawings. 
- 請遵循相關施工圖說之註記。

- Fit the profiles correctly and without gap to the sidewall liner sheeting. The baffles once fitted, shall touch the modules as per drawing. 
- 確保型鋼與爐牆不銹鋼內護板緊密貼合且無間隙。導流板安裝完成後，應依圖說規定接觸管束模組。

- During erection it is important to keep the required free gap to the top headers, the intermediate bumpers and the bottom bumpers. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation. 
- 安裝期間，務必保留與頂部聯箱、中間緩衝器及底部緩衝器之間規定的預留間隙，以利運轉時的熱膨脹空間。

- The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions. Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings. 
- 蓋板作為滑動點，必須在熱態運轉時能自由移動。請嚴格遵循圖說中關於銲接的細節要求。

- In case of any deviation regarding free spaces or free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
- 若預留空間或間隙出現任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

#### Welding of type one (1) baffle profiles (with stiffener) and the cover plates 第一型導流板型鋼（含加勁肋）與蓋板之銲接

- Weld all erected profiles and cover plates. 
- 銲接所有已安裝之型鋼與蓋板。

#### _Note:_  _註：_

- U-profiles are stitch welded. 
- U型鋼採間斷銲（點銲）。

- The profiles with stiffeners are plug welded, stitch welded in between two plug welds and stich welded at the baffle ends. 
- 帶加勁肋之型鋼採用塞銲，於兩塞銲之間進行間斷銲，並於導流板端部進行間斷銲。

- During welding follow the drawings to determine which side to weld the cover plates. 
- 銲接時，請參照圖說確認蓋板需銲接之側別。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循施工圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中的細節說明或典型構造圖。

#### Erection of type two (2) baffles and cover plates 第二型導流板與蓋板之安裝

This type of side wall gas baffle construction consists of a U-profile located on the modules, a profile (with stiffeners) located on the sidewall liner sheeting and a profile “inside” the U-profile. 
此類爐牆氣流導流板結構由位於管束模組上的U型鋼、位於爐牆不銹鋼內護板上帶加勁肋的型鋼，以及位於U型鋼「內部」的型鋼所組成。

Gaps between baffles are closed using cover plates. Cover plates are used on both baffles 
導流板之間的間隙需使用蓋板封閉。兩種導流板皆須使用蓋板。

- Fit and tack-weld the U-profile baffles, located on the module side. 
- 安裝並點銲位於管束模組側的U型鋼導流板。

- Fit and tack-weld the cover plates, located on the U-profiles. 
- 安裝並點銲位於U型鋼上的蓋板。

#### _Note:_  _註：_

   - Follow the notes on the applicable drawings. 
   - 請遵循相關施工圖說之註記。

- During erection of the U-profiles it is important to monitor the free space to the sidewalls, the free gap to the top headers, the free gap to the intermediate bumpers and the free gap to the bottom bumpers. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation. 
- 於安裝 U 型鋼期間，務必監控與爐牆側壁、頂部聯箱、中間緩衝器以及底部緩衝器之間的預留間隙。此舉係為確保機組運轉時熱膨脹之需求。

- The free space from the U-profile to the liner sheeting needs to be maintained over the complete sidewall height. 
- U 型鋼與不銹鋼內護板之間的預留空間，必須在整個爐牆高度範圍內保持一致。

- The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions. Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings. 
- 蓋板係作為滑動點使用，於高溫運轉條件下需能自由移動。請嚴格遵照圖面所示之銲接細節執行。

- In case of any deviation regarding free spaces, gaps or dimensions contact manufacturer. 
- 若預留空間、間隙或尺寸出現任何偏差，請立即聯繫原廠。

- Fit and tack-weld the profiles with stiffeners, located on the side wall liner sheeting and the U-profile. 
- 將帶有加勁肋之型鋼安裝並定位銲接於爐牆側壁不銹鋼內護板與 U 型鋼上。

- Fit and tack-weld the cover plates, located on the profiles. 
- 將蓋板安裝並定位銲接於型鋼之上。

#### _Note:_  ## _注意事項：_

- 

- Fit the profiles correctly to the sidewall liner sheeting and without gap. 
- 務必將型鋼正確貼合於爐牆側壁不銹鋼內護板上，不得留有間隙。

- Do not fit the profiles too tight into the U-profile. 
- 將型鋼裝入 U 型鋼內時，切勿過度緊配。

- During erection of the profile keep the given free gap to the top headers, free gap to the intermediate bumpers and free gap to the bottom bumpers. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation. 
- 於安裝型鋼期間，請保持與頂部聯箱、中間緩衝器以及底部緩衝器之間規定的預留間隙。此舉係為確保機組運轉時熱膨脹之需求。

- The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions. Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings. 
- 蓋板係作為滑動點使用，於高溫運轉條件下需能自由移動。請嚴格遵照圖面所示之銲接細節執行。

- In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, tolerances or other dimensions, contact the manufacturer 
- 若預留間隙、公差或其他尺寸出現任何偏差，請立即聯繫原廠。

#### Welding of type two (2) baffle U-profiles (with stiffener) and the cover plates  ## 二型導流板 U 型鋼（含加勁肋）與蓋板之銲接作業

- Weld all erected profiles and cover plates. 
- 將所有已安裝之型鋼與蓋板進行銲接。

#### _Note:_  ## _注意事項：_

- The U-profile is stitch welded to the module. 
- U 型鋼與管束模組採用斷續銲（縫銲）連接。

- The profiles with stiffeners are plug welded, stitch welded in between 2 plug welds and stich welded at the baffle ends. 
- 帶有加勁肋之型鋼需進行塞銲，兩塞銲點之間應進行斷續銲，且於導流板末端進行斷續銲。

- Closely follow which side to weld for the cover plates in order to ensure free movement. 
- 請嚴格遵照圖面指示之蓋板銲接側，以確保其滑動自由度。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業請確實遵循圖面之細節或典型規範及銲接程序規範 (WPS)。

#### Erection of type three (3) baffles and cover plates  ## 三型導流板與蓋板之安裝作業

This type of side wall gas baffle construction consists of a pre-assembled “door” located on the modules and two profiles (angles). The first profile (sidewall angle) is located on the sidewall liner sheeting and the second profile (fixation angle) is located on the first profile. After erection, the two profiles lock the “pre-assembled door baffle” in position). 
此類側牆氣體導流板結構由安裝於模組上的預組裝「門板」及兩組型鋼（角鋼）組成。第一組型鋼（側牆角鋼）位於側牆不銹鋼內護板上，第二組型鋼（固定角鋼）則位於第一組型鋼上。安裝完成後，該兩組型鋼將「預組裝門板導流板」鎖定於定位。

- Positioning the “doors” on the modules. _Note:_ 
- 模組上「門板」的定位。_註：_

   - Position the “doors” to the correct position, 90 degrees with a tolerance of 0.5 degree. 
   - 將「門板」置於正確位置，須保持 90 度角，容許誤差為 0.5 度。

   - During erection check the free space to the liner sheeting to be as mentioned on the drawing. 
   - 安裝期間須確認與不銹鋼內護板之間的預留間隙符合圖說要求。

   - In case of any deviation regarding free space, contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若預留間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

- Fit and tack weld the sidewall angle located on the sidewall liner sheeting and fit and tack weld the coverplates. _Note:_ 
- 裝配並點銲位於側牆不銹鋼內護板上的側牆角鋼，並裝配及點銲蓋板。_註：_

   - Fit the side wall angle profiles correctly and without gap to the sidewall liner sheeting. 
   - 側牆角鋼型鋼須安裝正確，且與側牆不銹鋼內護板之間不得有間隙。

- During erection it is important to keep the given free gap distance to the top headers, the free gap to the intermediate bumpers, the free gap to the bottom bumpers and the free gap between the “doors”. 
- 安裝過程中，務必保持與頂部聯箱、中間緩衝器、底部緩衝器以及各「門板」之間的指定預留間隙。

   - The cover plates are sliding points and need to move freely during hot conditions. Closely follow the details for welding on the drawings. 
   - 蓋板為滑動節點，於高溫運轉條件下須能自由移動。銲接作業時請嚴格遵守圖說中的細節要求。

   - In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若預留間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

- Fit and tack weld the fixation angle profiles on the sidewall angle profiles. _Note:_ 
- 裝配並點銲位於側牆角鋼上的固定角鋼型鋼。_註：_

   - Fit the fixation angle profile correctly to the sidewall angle profile and without gap. 
   - 固定角鋼型鋼須與側牆角鋼準確密合，不得有間隙。

   - During erection of the fixation angle profile maintain the given free gap between the “doors”. 
   - 安裝固定角鋼型鋼時，須維持「門板」之間指定的預留間隙。

   - In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若預留間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding of type three (3) baffle profiles and cover plates 第三（3）型導流板型鋼與蓋板之銲接作業

- Weld all erected sidewall and fixation angle profiles. 
- 銲接所有已安裝之側牆角鋼及固定角鋼型鋼。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Sidewall angles profiles connected to the liner sheeting are plug and stich welded. 
- 連接於不銹鋼內護板的側牆角鋼型鋼採用塞銲與斷續銲銲接。

- Fixation angles are plug welded and stitch welded between 2 holes. 
- 固定角鋼採用塞銲，並於兩孔之間進行斷續銲。

- Closely follow which side to weld for the cover plates in order to ensure free movement. 
- 務必嚴格遵循蓋板的銲接位置要求，以確保其運轉時能自由移動。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業須遵循圖說及銲接程序規範（WPS）中的細節或典型規定。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Check all free gaps and tolerances before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查所有間隙與公差。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the module side wall gas baffles to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
- 製造廠應執行目視檢查，並審查模組側牆導流板之實測數據報告，以確保符合相關公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列之規定。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 釋放作業時應附上未完成事項清單（若有）。

### 8.9.6. Flow baffle 8.9.6. 導流板

This paragraph describes the erection of the flow baffles. 
本節敘述導流板之吊裝作業。

This baffle prevents flue gasses from entering the hot box area in front of box 1, by covering the opening between the inlet duct bottom insulation and the bottom bumper in axis E. 
此導流板藉由覆蓋入口煙道底部保溫隔熱棉與 E 軸底部緩衝器之間的開口，防止煙氣進入 1 號箱體前方之熱箱區域。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the flow baffle shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
導流板吊裝之施工計畫書/風險評估及吊裝計畫應由安裝承攬商編製。

The erection sequence for the flow baffle is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
導流板之吊裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

Before erection of the flow baffle, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
導流板吊裝前，需預先完成部分準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提到之文件與程序應準備就緒，並經權責單位完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 以下準備工作/活動必須完成，並在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認（若適用）。

   - Inlet duct erected, including vertical panel in front of axis E. 
   - 入口煙道已吊裝完成，包括 E 軸前方之垂直板面。

   - Inlet duct hot box piping erected. 
   - 入口煙道熱箱管路已吊裝完成。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已點收並完成數量與品質檢核（開箱檢驗報告 OSD）。

#### Erection of flow baffle 導流板之吊裝

- Fit the sliding supports over the pipe bumpers of the vertical casing panels and place the flow baffles on top of the sliding support and bottom bumper of axis E. 
- 將滑動支座安裝於爐牆外殼板之管狀緩衝器上，並將導流板置於滑動支座及 E 軸底部緩衝器上方。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Follow the notes on the applicable drawings. 
- 應遵循相關圖面之註記。

- Fit the profiles correctly and without gap to the transverse bumper. The baffles once fitted, shall touch the bumpers as per drawing. 
- 應將型鋼正確安裝於橫向緩衝器且不得有間隙。導流板安裝後應依圖面要求確實與緩衝器接觸。

- During erection it is important to keep the required free gap to the insulation sheeting of the vertical panel. This to allow for thermal expansion during operation. 
- 在安裝期間，務必維持垂直爐牆外殼板保溫隔熱棉所需的預留間隙，以利運轉時的熱膨脹需求。

- The sliding points need to move freely during hot conditions (no welding to the pipe bumpers!). 
- 滑動點在熱態條件下需能自由移動（禁止將其銲接於管排緩衝器上！）。

- In case of any deviation regarding free spaces or free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
- 若預留空間或間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding of the flow baffles 導流板銲接作業

- Weld all flow baffles. 
- 銲接所有導流板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循施工圖說與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中的細節及典型施作要求。

- Check all free gaps before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查所有預留間隙。

#### Sealing angles flow baffles 導流板密封角鋼

- Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles at vertical casing panel (in front of box 1). 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲位於垂直爐牆外殼板（Box 1 前方）的密封角鋼。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Sealing plates shall be erected in such a way that the flow baffle can move freely during hot conditions. 
- 密封板之安裝方式須確保導流板在熱態條件下能自由移動。

- In case of any deviations regarding free gaps, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若預留間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

- Erect, fit and tack weld the sealing angles and respective connection plates. 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲密封角鋼及各別的連接板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Sealing angles are located on the vertical casing panel liner sheeting in front of box 1, guiding gas flow from inlet duct bottom panel onto the flow baffle, to reduce flue gas bypass flow. 
- 密封角鋼位於 Box 1 前方的垂直爐牆外殼板不銹鋼內護板上，用於引導煙氣從入口煙道底板流向導流板，以減少煙氣旁通流。

- Fit the sealing angles to the liner sheeting without gap and as per drawing. The sealing angle shall touch the flow baffle. 
- 依據圖說將密封角鋼緊密安裝於不銹鋼內護板上，不得留有間隙。密封角鋼應與導流板接觸。

- It is important during the erection to verify the actual position of the sealing angles and the fixation clips and maintain the required free gaps. 
- 安裝過程中，務必確認密封角鋼與固定夾的實際位置，並維持必要的預留間隙。

- In case of any deviation regarding free gaps contact the manufacturer. 
- 若預留間隙有任何偏差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Welding of the sealing angles 密封角鋼銲接作業

- Weld all installed field components. 
- 銲接所有已安裝之現場組件。

#### _註記：_ _Note:_

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中所述之細節及典型銲接要求。

- Ensure free gap and expansion possibilities of the assembly. 
- 確保組件具有足夠的預留間隙與熱膨脹空間。

#### 品質管制 (Quality Control) Quality control

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _註記：_ _Note:_

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 交付時應隨附待辦事項清單（如有）。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the measurements from the attic and basement baffles with internal liner sheeting.to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
- 製造商應進行目視檢查，並審閱頂棚及底部導流板連同不銹鋼內護板之實測數據報告，確保符合適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列。

### 8.9.7. Final inspection of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates 8.9.7. HRSG 導流板與密封板之最終檢驗

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝作業完成後，應進行檢驗。待辦事項應彙整列入待辦事項清單，並附於最終檢驗證書中。

The Final inspection Certificate of the HRSG baffles and sealing plates describes the systems or components inspected. 
HRSG 導流板與密封板之最終檢驗證書應詳細說明所檢驗之系統或組件。

#### 檢驗 Inspection

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 最終檢驗證書中所述之所有系統或組件群，應進行安裝正確性、完整性及損壞情形之最終檢驗。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 於現場步檢完成後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（如有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若有適用之待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - 需於水壓試驗前解決之項目 (A類項目)

   - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) 
   - 需於熱態試車前解決之項目 (B類項目)

   - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
   - 需於暫時驗收 (PAC) 前解決之項目 (C類項目)

#### _註記：_ _Note:_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 核對相關系統之適用施工品質計畫 是否已由所有相關單位簽署確認。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 核對所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 是否皆已結案。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

||||the top|of the|bottom girder.|||||||||||

|||•|Use and apply plywood||on the bottom||casing panels.|||||||||
|||•|於底部爐牆外殼板上使用並舖設膠合板。|||||||||||||
||||_Note:_|||||||||||||
||||_註：_|||||||||||||
||||-<br>Prepare the plywood panels (for protection|||||||of the bottom panels) during the pre-assembly of the main steel||||||
||||columns for the boiler main steel.|||||||||||||
||||-<br>在鍋爐主鋼結構的柱體預組裝期間，應準備好用於保護底部面板的膠合板。|||||||||||||
||||-<br>To avoid damaging of the boiler casing panels liner sheeting use plywood panels. Erect the plywood panels|||||||||||||
||||-<br>為避免損壞鍋爐爐牆外殼板的不銹鋼內護板，請使用膠合板。並搭設膠合板。|||||||||||||

||||during erection of the bottom panels.|||||||||||||
- 在爐底板安裝期間。

- Open the plywood panels during the fit-up and weld activities, but keep the panels as far as closed to each other as possible.
- 在組裝與銲接作業期間開啟膠合板，但應儘量保持膠合板彼此間的閉合狀態。
- Plywood on the bottom panels needs to be in place (on the liner sheeting) until the end of the construction phase.
- 爐底板上的膠合板須維持定位（置於不銹鋼內護板上），直至施工階段結束。
- After finalizing the inside bottom casing, modify the plywood in such a way that the “floor is protected” during further erection.
- 在完成內部爐牆外殼板後，應調整膠合板，以確保在後續安裝作業期間「地面受到保護」。
- Cut holes in the plywood for piping activities and close the holes until the relevant piping is erected.
- 為管路作業於膠合板上開孔，並於相關管路安裝前將孔洞封閉。
• Elevated platform (after erection of the bottom casing and during or after the erection of the sidewall casing).
• 高架平台（於爐牆外殼板安裝後，以及側牆外殼板安裝期間或之後）。
_Note:_
_註：_
- An elevated working platform (man basket) on the inside of the boiler is useful for erection of internal insulation at the casing sidewall insulation field splices.
- 鍋爐內部的作業高架平台（人員吊籃）有助於側牆外殼板絕緣層現場接頭的內部保溫安裝。
- Erection of the elevated platforms can commence during sidewall casing panel erection.
- 高架平台可在側牆外殼板安裝期間開始架設。
- Elevated platforms to be erected on both sides (right / left side) of the boiler in such a way that proper access along the complete length and height of the boiler sidewalls can be provided.
- 高架平台應架設於鍋爐兩側（右側/左側），以確保能順利沿鍋爐側牆的全長與高度進行施工。

|||_Note:_|||||||||||
|||_註：_|||||||||||
||||-|Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing||||||penetrations. Properly cut the plastic|||
||||-|安裝前，移除外殼穿孔處的塑膠與保溫隔熱棉。應使用刀具妥善切割塑膠|||
|||||and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out|||using force.||||||
|||||與隔熱棉。切勿用力強行拉出。||||||
||||-|Align the panel to the correct position and bolt the U-channels to the main steel girders. In case of welded|||||||||
||||-|將板件對正至正確位置，並將 U 型鋼槽栓接至主鋼樑。若為銲接|||||||||
|||||connections tack-weld the panel to main|||steel structure after alignment.||||||
|||||接頭，對正後將板件點銲至主鋼結構上。||||||

||||-|裁除爐底板上的內部保溫保護塑膠。|||||||||
||||-|Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing.|||||||||
||||-|板件安裝與點銲時應無間隙。必要時依圖說使用填隙板。|||||||||
||||-|During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.|||||||||
||||-|點銲期間，使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉以進行火花防護。|||||||||
||||-|Erect the remaining bolts and nuts. When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made|||||||||
||||-|安裝剩餘螺栓與螺帽。當發現螺栓孔位不正時，僅可在諮詢原廠後進行調整。|||||||||
|||||only after consultation with the manufacturer.|||||||||
||||-|Use taper washers for the connection of the U-channels to the bottom girder.|||||||||
||||-|將 U 型鋼槽連接至底部鋼樑時，請使用斜面墊圈。|||||||||

||||-|For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous.|||||||||

#### Erection side wall casing panels 側牆爐牆外殼板吊裝

|•|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.|Erect, fit and tack-weld the side wall casing panels.||||||||
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
||_Note:_|||||||||||||
||-|Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations. Properly cut the plastic||||||||||||
||-|吊裝前，請移除爐牆外殼板貫穿處之塑膠膜及保溫隔熱棉。||||||||||||
|||and wool using|a knife and do not pull it out using force.|||||||||||
|||請使用美工刀適當切割塑膠膜與保溫棉，切勿強行拉扯。|||||||||||
||-|Position and align the side||||wall casing panels to||the correct position.||||||
||-|將側牆爐牆外殼板定位並對準至正確位置。||||||||||||
||-|Verify fit-up elevations and tolerances as|||||indicated on the drawings.|||||||
||-|依據設計圖說核對安裝標高及公差。||||||||||||
||-|Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the side wall casing|||||||||panels.|||
||-|割除側牆爐牆外殼板內側之保溫防護塑膠膜。||||||||||||
||-|Fit and tack-weld the panels to the aligned position.||||||||||||
||-|將板片合攏並點銲至定位。||||||||||||
||-|During tack welding, cover||||the insulation|wool using weld blankets for spark protection.|||||||
||-|點銲期間，應使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉，以防火花噴濺。||||||||||||
|Welding of||the side wall casing panels||||||||||||
|•|Weld the sidewall panels.|||||||||||||
|•|進行側牆板銲接作業。||||||||||||
||_Note:_|||||||||||||
||-|Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the sidewall panels.||||||||||||
||-|割除側牆板內側之保溫防護塑膠膜。||||||||||||
||-|All external welds shall be||||continuous, no stitch welding|||on the outside allowed.|||||
||-|所有外部銲道均應為連續銲，外部嚴禁斷續銲。||||||||||||
||-|Stitch welding is only allowed on the inside joints where|||||||indicated on|the drawings, for dimensions see the||||
||-|僅允許於設計圖說標註之內部接縫處使用斷續銲，尺寸請參閱圖說細節。||||||||||||
|||details on the drawings.||||||||||||
||-|Follow the details and or|||typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.|||||||||
||-|銲接作業應遵循圖說細節或典型銲接方式及銲接程序規範 (WPS)。||||||||||||
||-|During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection.||||||||||||
||-|銲接期間，應使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉，以防火花噴濺。||||||||||||
|Field parts||side wall casing panels||||||||||||
|•|Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary|||||field parts for|the side wall casing panels.|||||||
|•|吊裝、組裝並點銲側牆爐牆外殼板所有必要之現場組件。||||||||||||
||_Note:_|||||||||||||
||-|Field parts for the side wall casing panels can be filler, guide, stiffener plates and U-channels, identify all||||||||||||
||-|側牆爐牆外殼板之現場組件包含填隙板、導板、補強板及 U 型鋼，請確認圖說標註之所有現場組件。||||||||||||
|||required field parts as indicated on the drawings.||||||||||||
||-|Cross- and connection points of guide plates / stiffeners|||||||/ U-channels need to be erected using the correct|||||
||-|導板/補強板/U 型鋼之交叉與連接點，需依正確之銲接準備進行組裝。||||||||||||
|||weld preparation.||||||||||||
||-|All gaps at corners and||field splices have to be closed (seal welded)||||||using filler plates (6 mm thickness).||||
||-|角部及現場接合處之所有間隙，均須使用填隙板（厚度 6 mm）封閉（密封銲）。||||||||||||

- 9.3.4. Top casing panels for the SCR duct SCR煙道頂部爐牆外殼板
- Erect the horizontal top panels for the SCR duct. 吊裝SCR煙道之水平頂板。
- Top casing panels after • Documents and procedures: - Approved and reviewed 爐牆外殼板放行後 • 文件與程序：- 已核准與審查

- • Acceptance: - Scaffolding ready - Erection AIG and SCR systems (inside) completed • 驗收：- 施工架就緒 - AIG及SCR系統（爐內）安裝完成

- • Release: - Erection top panels Burner and SCR duct • 放行：- 燃燒器與SCR煙道頂板安裝

- Erection • Erect, fit and tack-weld the top casing panels. 安裝 • 吊裝、組對並點銲頂部爐牆外殼板。
- _Note:_ - Before erection, remove the plastic and insulation wool from the casing penetrations if applicable. Properly cut the plastic and wool using a knife. Do not pull it out using force. 註：- 安裝前，若適用，應移除爐牆貫穿孔處之塑膠與保溫隔熱棉。使用美工刀適當裁切塑膠與隔熱棉，切勿強行拉扯。

- - Align the panel to the correct position and tack-weld the panel to the main steel structure after alignment. - Cut away the internal insulation protection plastic from the top casing panels. - Fit and tack-weld the panels without gap. Use filler plates where required as per drawing. - During tack-welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection. - 將外殼板對正至正確位置，並於校準後將外殼板點銲至主鋼構件上。 - 切除頂部爐牆外殼板之內部保溫防護塑膠。 - 組對並點銲外殼板，確保無縫隙。依圖說需求使用填隙片。 - 點銲作業期間，使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉以防止火花噴濺。

- Welding • Weld the top casing panel field splices 銲接 • 銲接頂部爐牆外殼板之現場接合銲道
- _Note:_ - All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed. - Stitch welds are only allowed on the inside joints, for dimensions see the details on drawings. - For all channel ends the welds shall be continuous. - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. - During welding, cover the insulation wool using weld blankets for spark protection. 註：- 所有外部銲道均應為連續銲，外側不得進行斷續銲。 - 僅內部接合處允許斷續銲，尺寸詳見圖說細節。 - 所有槽鋼末端之銲道均應為連續銲。 - 遵循圖說與銲接程序規範（WPS）之銲接細節或典型圖。 - 銲接作業期間，使用銲接防火毯覆蓋保溫隔熱棉以防止火花噴濺。

- Field parts top casing panels • Erect, fit and tack-weld all necessary field parts. 頂部爐牆外殼板之現場組件 • 吊裝、組對並點銲所有必要之現場組件。
- _Note:_ - Field parts for the top casing panels can be filler, guide and stiffener plates. Identify all required field parts as indicated on the drawings. 註：- 頂部爐牆外殼板之現場組件可能包含填隙片、導板與加勁板。依據圖說標示辨識所有所需之現場組件。

- - Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the field part drawings. - All gaps at corners and field splices have to be closed (seal welded) using filler plates (6 mm thickness). - 遵循現場組件圖說上之銲接典型圖要求。 - 所有角落與現場接合處之縫隙均須使用填隙片（6 mm 厚）封閉（密封銲）。

- Welding field parts • Weld all fitted field parts. 現場組件銲接 • 銲接所有已組對之現場組件。
- _Note:_ - All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welding on the outside allowed. - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings. 註：- 所有外部銲道均應為連續銲，外側不得進行斷續銲。 - 遵循圖說之銲接細節或典型圖。

- Corner connections top panels 
- 頂板角落連接處

- • Erect, fit and tack-weld all corner connections using angle or flat bar connections. Verify the erection drawings to determine which type to use. _Note:_ - Align the angle / flat bar connections to the casing panels without gap. - Angle / flat bar cross sections and connection points need to be erected using the correct weld preparation, for details see the drawings. 
- • 使用角鋼或扁鐵連接件安裝、試組並點銲所有角落連接處。請查閱施工圖說以確認使用何種類型。_註：_ - 將角鋼/扁鐵連接件與爐牆外殼板對齊，不得有縫隙。 - 角鋼/扁鐵截面及連接點的安裝需採用正確的銲接坡口準備，詳細資訊請參閱施工圖說。

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

### 9.3.6. Mechanical completion AIG and SCR systems 機械竣工 AIG 與 SCR 系統
When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. 
當特定系統或一組特定元件的機械安裝完成後，應對其進行檢查。
Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. 
待辦事項應彙整於待辦事項清單中。
The outstanding items list can be attached to a Mechanical Completion Certificate. 
待辦事項清單可附加於機械竣工證書中。
Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities. 
此類證書作為安裝作業適當完成的紀錄。
The Mechanical Completion Certificate for the SCR / AIG system describes the systems or components inspected. 
SCR/AIG 系統的機械竣工證書描述了已檢驗的系統或元件。
By signing the Mechanical Completion Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of erection to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly. 
透過簽署機械竣工證書，相關各方確認所提及之系統或元件已達足夠進度的安裝階段，以便確認系統移交試運轉 (Commissioning) 前所需的剩餘項目，若無此類項目，則直接將系統移交給試運轉部門。
Walk-down 現場步檢
• All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
• 機械竣工證書上提及的所有系統或特定元件群組，均應進行最終檢查，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。
• A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
• 現場步檢結束後，將立即建立待辦事項清單紀錄 (若有)。
• In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized: 
• 若適用待辦事項清單，應進行分類：
- Items to be solved before hydro testing. 
- 於水壓試驗前需解決之項目。
- Items to be solved before commissioning. 
- 於試運轉前需解決之項目。
- Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. 
- 於初步驗收前需解決之項目。
_Note:_ 
_註：_ 
- Verify that the applicable site assembly travellers for the systems involved are signed off by all involved parties. 
- 確認相關系統的適用工地組裝作業紀錄 (Travellers) 已由所有相關方簽署。
- Check for any outstanding NCRs (if any). 
- 檢查有無未結案之不符合報告 (NCR) (若有)。
- Check for lists of outstanding items made in earlier stages. 
- 檢查先前階段所製作之待辦事項清單。
9.3.7. Installation of scr blocks 9.3.7. SCR 模組塊安裝

Install the SCR block according the relevant supplier documentation 24 hours after running on base load. 
依據供應商相關文件規定，於滿載運轉 24 小時後安裝 SCR 模組。

# 10. DRUMS AND VESSELS 汽鼓與容器設備

本章包含下列章節：

## 10.1. General 一般規定

Drum and vessel erection for the HRSG scope consists out of a IP and LP drum and a HP separator vessel. Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of drums shall be prepared by the erection contractor. The erection sequence for drums and vessels is shown in document 60031-730-05-001 
熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 範圍內之汽鼓與容器吊裝作業，包含中壓與低壓汽鼓及高壓分離容器。吊裝承攬商應編撰汽鼓吊裝之施工計畫書／風險評估報告及吊裝計畫。汽鼓與容器之吊裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

## 10.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for installation of the drums and Vessels . 
安裝汽鼓與容器所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement :  Erection drums and tanks 
- 施工計畫書：汽鼓與槽體吊裝

- - FQP :  HRSG drums and vessels 
- - 施工品質計畫：HRSG 汽鼓與容器

- FQP 
- 施工品質計畫

- WPS / PQR / WPQ 
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格紀錄 (WPQ)

   - :  Non-pressure parts. :  Non pressure parts. 
   - ：非承壓組件。：非承壓組件。

- Bolt torque procedure 
- 螺栓扭力鎖緊程序

- Weld typical / record 
- 銲接典型 / 紀錄

   - :  Non-pressure parts. 
   - ：非受壓組件。

- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲接材料管理程序：非受壓組件。

- - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts. - Documents according Chapter “piping” :  Pressure parts. 
- - 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格認證：非受壓組件。 - 相關文件依據「管路」章節：受壓組件。

## 10.3. Drum erection 汽鼓吊裝作業

Before erection of the drums can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始汽鼓吊裝作業前，必須先行準備相關工項。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落所提及之文件與程序必須到位，並經由權責單位（或相關方）審查核可。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/工項必須完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Temporary storage of IP and LP down comers 
   - 中壓與低壓下降管的臨時存放。

   - Drum support beams erected 
   - 汽鼓支撐樑之吊裝。

   - Grouting of main steel columns and torqueing of the anchors. 
   - 主鋼結構柱之無收縮水泥灌漿及錨栓扭力鎖緊。

   - Elevation correct 
   - 高程校正。

- Install the sliding supports on the drum suspension beams. 
- 於汽鼓懸吊樑上安裝滑動支座。

- Install the counter sliding plates with shims on the drum saddles. 
- 於汽鼓鞍座上安裝帶有填隙片之對應滑動板。

- Install shim plates on the fixation lug of the drum. 
- 於汽鼓固定耳板上安裝填隙板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Perform a survey to determine the location and dimensions of the drum fixation lug support and the drum centre fixation fork. (See also main steel structure) 
- 執行測量以確認汽鼓固定耳板支座與汽鼓中心固定叉之位置及尺寸。（參見主鋼結構圖說）

   - Once the drum is positioned the free space between the centre fixation fork and the fixation lug support shall be equally divided to each side and be as given on the drum drawings. Based on the dimensions from the survey report the correct shim thickness can be installed and welded. 
   - 汽鼓定位後，中心固定叉與固定耳板支座間之餘隙，應均分於兩側，並符合汽鼓圖說之規範。依據測量報告所得之尺寸，安裝並銲接正確厚度之填隙片。

- Perform a survey to determine the dimensions from the centreline of the drum to the lowest points of the drum saddles. Elevation of the drum support beams shall be known and available as well. Based on the available dimensions and elevations the required shim thickness for installation between 
- 執行測量以確認從汽鼓中心線至汽鼓鞍座最低點之尺寸。汽鼓支撐樑之高程資訊亦須確認並備妥。根據既有尺寸與高程，可判定安裝於

the counter sliding plates and the drum saddles can be determined and installed. Use the tolerance drawings from the manufacturer. 
對應滑動板與汽鼓鞍座間所需之填隙片厚度並進行安裝。請使用製造商提供之公差圖說。

- Keep the location clean during erection and prevent pollution of surfaces. 
- 吊裝期間應保持現場清潔，並防止表面受到污染。

- Install the slide support plates on the drum support beams at the correct location, NO TACK WELDING. 
- 請將滑動支承板安裝於汽鼓支承樑的正確位置，嚴禁實施點銲 (NO TACK WELDING)。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行
#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Alignment of the drums 
- 本章節各項作業順利完成後，放行下列活動：- 汽鼓對心。

#### erection 安裝作業
#### erection 安裝作業

- Lift / transport the drums as per the applicable Work Method Statement. 
- 依照適用的施工計畫書 (Work Method Statement) 進行汽鼓的吊裝與運輸。

#### _Note:_ 註：

   - Check all connections before lifting / transport of the drums 
   - 汽鼓吊裝與運輸前，務必檢查所有連接處。

   - During loading and lifting, frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape. 
   - 在裝載與吊裝過程中，須頻繁檢查設備狀態以確保其處於良好狀況。

   - Transport / Lifting to take place according the instructions for lifting and the Work Method Statement. 
   - 運輸與吊裝作業須遵循吊裝說明書及施工計畫書之規範。

   - In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若發生任何偏差或失效情形，請立即聯繫製造商。

- Erect the drums on the correct elevation. 
- 將汽鼓吊裝安裝至正確標高位置。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Frequently check the cup shaped sliding support base with PTFE pad is not damaged during erection. (On the drum support beams) 
- 於安裝期間，須頻繁檢查位於汽鼓支承樑上，配有 PTFE 墊片的杯狀滑動支座是否受損。

- Verify the elevation to be in accordance with the drum tolerance drawings. In case adjustment of the drum elevation is required, do not forget to incorporate the actual dimensions of the top of the steel goalpost rows in the evaluation. Discuss this with manufacturer. 
- 驗證標高是否符合汽鼓公差圖說。若需調整汽鼓標高，請務必將鋼結構門型架 (Steel goalpost) 頂部的實際尺寸納入評估，並與製造商研商。

- Make a survey report for the final elevation of the drums. 
- 製作汽鼓最終標高的測量報告。

#### Quality control 品質管制
#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依照適用的施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Verify the elevation of the drum and placement on sliding plates for correctness. 
- 驗證汽鼓標高及其於滑動板上的放置位置是否正確。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the drum measurement to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
- 製造商應進行目視檢查，並審查汽鼓實測測量報告，以確保其符合適用之 60031-730-06 系列公差圖說。

## 10.4. Drum alignment 10.4. 汽鼓對心作業
## 10.4. Drum alignment 10.4. 汽鼓對心作業

Before alignment of the drums can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在進行汽鼓對心作業前，需預先完成下列準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與前提條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
上述段落所提及之文件與程序書需備妥，並經權責單位（或人員）審閱。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
下列準備工作／活動需已完成，並在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認（如適用）。

   - Drums installed 
   - 汽鼓安裝完成

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
本段落所述作業若已順利完成，即可放行下列作業：

   - Installation drum centre fixation fork and guide plates 
   - 安裝汽鼓中心固定叉及導板

#### Alignment 對心作業

- Install several riser pipes from the harp header nozzles to the drum nozzles. Install two riser pipes on the left and right sides and two riser pipes divided over the harp headers. 
安裝數支由集管箱 (harp header) 接管至汽鼓接管的上升管。於左右兩側各安裝兩支上升管，並將兩支上升管分配在集管箱上。

During fit-up of the riser piping use pipe clamps on the harp header side. Keep the riser piping free from any clamping on the drum nozzles side. 
進行上升管組裝時，在集管箱側使用管夾固定。汽鼓接管側的上升管則不得施加任何夾具。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- In case (out of tolerance) offset is showing at the connection between the riser piping and the drum nozzles, the drum placement needs adjustment. 
若上升管與汽鼓接管之連接處出現偏差（超過容許公差），則需調整汽鼓安裝位置。

- Use the harp header side as the “fixed point” and starting point for the drum alignment. 
以集管箱側作為「固定點」，並以此為基準進行汽鼓對心。

- During erection of the riser piping DO NOT FORGET TO INSTALL THE METAL EXPANSION BELLOWS. 
在上升管安裝期間，切勿遺忘安裝金屬波紋伸縮接頭。

- When the offset is more than the allowable tolerances, contact the manufacturer. 
若偏差超過容許公差，請聯繫製造商。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
依照適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制工作。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Tack-welding can only commence when all documents for the pressure parts (piping) are approved and reviewed by the client. 
僅在所有壓力組件（管路）相關文件皆經業主核准與審閱後，始可進行點銲作業。

- Verify the fit-up of the piping to be stress-free.
- 確認管路之組裝為無應力狀態。

- Verify the metal expansion bellow is installed (if applicable).
- 確認金屬波紋伸縮接頭已安裝（如適用）。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the drum measurements to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series.
- 製造商應進行目視檢查，並審查汽鼓尺寸之實際測量報告，以確保符合相關公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列之要求。

#### Tack-welding of the riser piping 上升管管路之點銲作業

- Tack-weld the riser piping between the harp header nozzles and the drum nozzles.
- 將上升管管路於排管聯箱接管與汽鼓接管之間進行點銲固定。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 銲接作業應遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中之細節說明或典型構造。

## 10.5. Drum centre fixation fork and guide plates 汽鼓中心固定叉與導板

Before erection of the drum centre fixation fork and guide plates can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始安裝汽鼓中心固定叉與導板之前，須預先準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述章節提及之文件與程序須備妥，並經由權責單位（或相關方）審查確認。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動須完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成相關簽認（如適用）。

   - Drums aligned
   - 汽鼓對正完成

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - erection external piping
- 本章節之各項活動順利完成後，放行進行後續活動：- 外接管路安裝

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect the drum center fixation fork in the correct position by tack-welding.
- 將汽鼓中心固定叉定位於正確位置並進行點銲。

- Fit and tack weld the guide plates.
- 組裝導板並進行點銲。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the gap between the guide plates and the drum centre guide. Verify the tolerances mentioned on the drum drawings before welding.
- 檢查導板與汽鼓中心導件之間之間隙。在進行銲接前，務必確認汽鼓圖面上所列之公差要求。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld the drum sliding supports and the guide plates.
- 銲接汽鼓滑動支座及導向板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 銲接作業請依據圖面細節及典型銲接規範 (WPS) 執行。

#### Bolting 螺栓鎖固

- Erect the bolted drum center fixation fork (where applicable)
- 吊裝汽鼓中心固定叉（若適用處）。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Tightening to take place according the work method statement.
- 螺栓緊固作業應依據施工計畫書執行。

- Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening (see 60031-730-01-008)
- 螺栓緊固時請採用正確的扭力值（詳參 60031-730-01-008）。

- Splices in bolted connections are not permitted.
- 螺栓連接處嚴禁進行接續（拼接）。

- Use the correct bolt material and length, according the applicable bolt list.
- 請依據適用之螺栓清單，選用正確的螺栓材質及長度。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the tolerances before welding.
- 銲接前應先進行公差檢驗。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有任何遺留項目，須附帶清單進行放行。

## 10.6. Drum internals and equipment 10.6. 汽鼓內件與設備

### 10.6.1. Drum internals 10.6.1. 汽鼓內件

- Only the connection materials for the LP drum demisters (angles bars, bolts/nuts, and locking washers) are already installed upon delivery. The demister elements themselves are delivered loose.
- 低壓汽鼓除霧器之連接材料（角鋼、螺栓/螺帽及止退墊圈）於交貨時已先行安裝；除霧器本體元件則為散裝運抵現場。

- Between drum erection and hydrostatic testing, perform an inspection of the inside of the drum in order to assure the LP drum demister elements are not present and to assure the connection materials for these s are present and complete.
- 於汽鼓吊裝作業完成後至水壓試驗前，應進行汽鼓內部檢查，以確保低壓汽鼓除霧器元件尚未安裝，並確認相關之連接材料齊全且完整。

- During the inspection remove all Silica Gel bags from the drum.
- 檢查過程中，須將汽鼓內所有的矽膠乾燥包清除。

- Assure all loosed delivered Drum Secondary Separator elements are present on site (storage). 
- 確保所有散裝運抵現場（儲存區）的汽鼓二次分離器組件均已到齊。

#### Quality control 品質管制
#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the tolerances before welding. 
- 銲接前應先檢查公差。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有待辦事項（缺點項目），應列出清單後再行放行。

### 10.6.2. Drum equipment 汽鼓內部組件
### 10.6.2. Drum equipment 汽鼓內部組件

Examples of drum equipment: 
汽鼓內部組件範例：

- Level gauge elements 
- 水位計組件

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- For erection use the relevant supplier erection instructions. 
- 安裝作業請參閱供應商提供的安裝說明書。

- Follow the erection steps and requirements stipulated in chapter 15 “ _Piping”._ 
- 遵循第 15 章「管路」中所規定的安裝步驟與要求。

## 10.7. HP separator vessel erection 高壓分離器容器安裝
## 10.7. HP separator vessel erection 高壓分離器容器安裝

Before erection of the HP separator vessel can commence, some activities needs to be prepared in advance. 
在高壓分離器容器安裝開始前，需先行準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及的文件與程序書均須備妥，並經權責單位審核。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作與活動必須完成，並在施工品質計畫 中完成適用之簽認。

   - HP separator vessel supporting structure erected 
   - 高壓分離器容器支撐結構已完成安裝

   - Elevation correct 
   - 高程正確無誤

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已接收並完成數量與品質檢核（OSD 開箱檢驗報告）

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- Perform a survey to determine the centreline and location and dimensions of the HP separator supporting dummies. 
- 進行測量以確認高壓分離器支撐墊板的中心線、位置及尺寸。

- Perform a survey to determine the elevation and location of the HP nozzles. 
- 執行測量作業以確認高壓 (HP) 接管之標高與位置。

- Keep the location clean during erection and prevent pollution of surfaces. 
- 施工期間應保持作業現場清潔，並防止表面遭受污染。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業之執行釋放
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 本章節所述各項作業順利完成後，即釋放後續作業之執行權限：

   - piping connections 
   - 管路連接

#### Erection 施工安裝
- Lift / transport the HP separator vessel as per the applicable Work Method Statement. 
- 依據適用之施工方法說明書 (Work Method Statement) 進行高壓分離桶之吊裝與運輸。

#### _Note:_ 註：
   - Check all connections before lifting / transport of the HP separator vessel. 
   - 於吊裝或運輸高壓分離桶前，應檢查所有連接部位。

   - During loading and lifting, frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape. 
   - 於裝載與吊裝期間，應頻繁檢查設備狀態，以確保其保持良好完好狀況。

   - Transport / Lifting to take place according the instructions for lifting and the Work Method Statement. 
   - 運輸與吊裝作業應遵循吊裝指示及施工方法說明書之規定進行。

   - In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若發生任何偏差或異常，請聯繫製造商。

- Erect the HP separator vessel on the correct location and elevation. 
- 將高壓分離桶安裝於正確之位置與標高。

#### _Note:_ 註：
- Verify the elevation to be in accordance with the tolerance drawings. In case of adjustment of the HP separator vessel elevation is required; do not forget to incorporate the actual dimensions of the top of supporting steel. 
- 驗證標高是否符合公差圖說之規範。若需調整高壓分離桶之標高，請務必納入支撐鋼結構頂部之實際尺寸進行考量。

- If needed use shim plates to erect the HP separator vessel to the correct location. 
- 必要時，使用墊片 (shim plates) 將高壓分離桶安裝至正確位置。

- Make a survey report for the final elevation of the HP separator vessel. 
- 製作高壓分離桶之最終標高測量報告。

#### Quality control 品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or Procedures 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
- Verify the elevation of the HP separator vessel and placement on shim plates for correctness. 
- 確認高壓分離桶之標高及放置於墊片上之正確性。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for the HP separator vessel measurement to be in accordance with the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
- 製造廠商應目視檢查並審閱高壓分離槽之實際測量報告，以確保符合相關公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列之規定。

## 10.8. Final inspection drums and vessels 鍋爐汽鼓與壓力容器之最終檢驗

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. 
當特定系統或特定組件群組之機械安裝作業完成後，應進行檢驗。

Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
待辦事項應彙整列入待辦事項清單，並附於最終檢驗證書中。

Final inspection for the boiler part is mainly covered by the boiler casing, because all other boiler parts have a separate final inspection round. 
鍋爐部件之最終檢驗主要涵蓋爐牆外殼板，因為其他所有鍋爐部件皆有各自獨立的最終檢驗階段。

The Final inspection Certificate of the drums describes the systems or components inspected. 
汽鼓之最終檢驗證書應載明所檢驗之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 最終檢驗證書中所述之所有系統或特定組件群組，均應進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢結束後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若有適用之待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前須解決之項目（A類項目）

   - - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) 
   - - 熱機試運轉前須解決之項目（B類項目）

   - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
   - 暫時驗收 (PAC) 前須解決之項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 核對相關系統之施工品質計畫 是否已由所有相關單位簽署。待辦事項應列入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 核對所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 是否皆已結案。待辦事項應列入待辦事項清單中。

# 11. TANKS / SKIDS 儲槽 / 撬裝設備

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列段落：

# 1. General 1. 一般規定

# 2. Documents and procedures 2. 文件與程序

# 3. Tank / skid erection 3. 儲槽 / 撬裝設備安裝

# 4. Grouting 4. 無收縮水泥灌漿

# 5. Final inspection tanks / skids 最終檢查：儲槽 / 滑軌基座模組

- :  paragraph 11.1 :  paragraph 11.2 :  paragraph 11.3 :  paragraph 11.4 :  paragraph 11.5 
- :  第 11.1 節 :  第 11.2 節 :  第 11.3 節 :  第 11.4 節 :  第 11.5 節

## 11.1. General 概述

Tank erection for the HRSG scope consists out of a blowdown tank. 
HRSG 範圍內的儲槽安裝工程包含一座排污槽 (blowdown tank)。
Skid erection for the HRSG scope normally consists out of a AIG skid. 
HRSG 範圍內的滑軌基座模組 (skid) 安裝工程通常包含一座氨注入系統 (AIG) 滑軌基座。
Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of tanks / skids shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
儲槽與滑軌基座安裝工程之施工計畫書 / 風險評估報告及吊裝計畫，應由安裝承攬商負責編製。
The erection sequence for blowdown tank and AIG skid is shown in document 60031-730-05-001 
排污槽與 AIG 滑軌基座之安裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

- 11.2. Documents and procedures 11.2. 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the tanks / skids . 
儲槽 / 滑軌基座安裝所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement 
- 施工計畫書

- Work method statement 
- 施工計畫書

- FQP 
- 施工品質計畫

- FQP

- 螺栓扭力鎖固程序

- WPS / PQR / WPQ 
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格紀錄 (WPQ)

- Weld typical / record 
- 典型銲道圖 / 銲接紀錄

- Welding consumable handling procedure 
- 銲接材料管理程序

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications 
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格認證

- Documents according Chapter “piping” 
- 依據「配管」章節之相關文件

- :  Erection drums and tanks

- :  Erection SCR system 
- :  選擇性觸媒還原 (SCR) 系統安裝

## 11.3. Tank / skid erection 桶槽 / 橇裝模組安裝

Before erection of the blowdown tank or AIG skid can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝排污桶槽或氨注入系統 (AIG) 橇裝模組之前，需預先準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 前置準備與前提條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並由權責單位完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並視情況於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。

   - Tank / skid foundation 
   - 桶槽 / 橇裝模組基礎

- Lift and transport the tank / skid as per the applicable Work Method Statement. 
- 依據適用的施工計畫書進行桶槽/橇裝模組之吊裝與運輸。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check all connections before lifting and transporting the tank / skid. 
- 桶槽/橇裝模組於吊裝及運輸前，應檢查所有連接處。

- During loading and lifting, frequently check the status of the equipment to be in good shape. 
- 於裝載及吊裝過程中，須持續檢查設備狀態以確保其處於良好狀況。

- Transport and lifting to take place according the instructions for lifting and the Work Method Statement. 
- 運輸與吊裝作業須遵循吊裝說明及施工計畫書辦理。

- In case of skids verify the supplier handling and installation instructions. 
- 若為橇裝模組，須核對供應商之搬運與安裝說明書。

- In case of any deviation or failure, contact the manufacturer. 
- 若發生任何偏差或故障，請聯繫製造廠商。

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 本節各項作業順利完成後，准予進行下列作業：

   - Grouting of tanks / skids 
   - 桶槽 / 橇裝模組之無收縮水泥灌漿

   - Piping connections 
   - 配管連接

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Position the tank / skid onto its steel structure supports. 
- 將桶槽 / 橇裝模組定位於其鋼構支撐架上。

- Adjust for elevation and alignment using steel shims. 
- 使用鋼墊片進行高程與對準調整。

- Connect the tank/skid to the steel structure as indicated on the drawings. 
- 依照圖面所示，將槽體/撬塊連接至鋼結構。

#### _Note:_ _注意事項：_ 

- Closely monitor tank/skid coordinates during positioning. 
- 定位過程中需密切監控槽體/撬塊之座標。

- Perform a survey for correct position, alignment and elevation of the tank/skid when in position. 
- 當槽體/撬塊定位後，執行測量以確認其位置、對準度及高程是否正確。

- Any shims placed shall be welded to the steel structure. 
- 所放置之任何墊片均應銲接於鋼結構上。

- Welding of shims only after confirmation of correct position. 
- 墊片銲接應於確認位置正確後方可進行。

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業應遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型規範。

#### Quality control 品質控制 

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質控制作業。

- _Note:_ _注意事項：_ 

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 釋出時應檢附待辦事項清單 (如有)。

- Inspect the inside of a tank for cleanliness and remove any silica gel bags from the inside of the vessel. 
- 檢查槽體內部清潔度，並移除容器內之所有矽膠乾燥劑包。

## 11.4. Grouting 無收縮水泥灌漿 

Grouting of the tanks / skids is based on the Chapter “Grouting” in this manual. Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution. 
槽體/撬塊之無收縮水泥灌漿係依據本手冊「灌漿」章節辦理。執行期間應遵循該章節所述之安裝與品質步驟。

## 11.5. Final inspection tanks / skids 槽體/撬塊最終檢查 

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成時，應進行檢查。待辦事項應彙整為待辦事項清單，並附於最終檢查合格證書上。

The Final inspection Certificate of the tanks / skids describes the systems or components inspected. 
槽體/撬塊之最終檢查合格證書應載明已檢查之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢查 

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 最終檢查合格證書所提及之所有系統或特定組件群，均應進行安裝正確性、完整性及損壞情形之最終檢查。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢結束後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄 (如有)。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若有待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - 需於水壓試驗前完成之項目 (A類項目)

- - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
- 待熱試運轉前需解決項目（B類項目）- 待工程暫時驗收（PAC）前需解決項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_  _註記：_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 查驗相關系統之施工品質計畫 是否已由各相關單位簽署核准。遺留項目應納入待辦清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 查驗所有不符合報告 (NCR) 是否皆已結案。遺留項目應納入待辦清單中。

# 12. STACK AND OUTLET DUCT 煙囪與出口煙道

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章節包含下列段落：

1. Stack erection :  paragraph  12.1 
1. 煙囪吊裝：第 12.1 節

# 2. Outlet duct erection 出口煙道吊裝

:  paragraph  12.2 
：第 12.2 節

## 12.1. Stack erection 煙囪吊裝

This paragraph describes the erection of the main stack. 
本段落說明主煙囪之吊裝作業。

### 12.1.1. General 一般規定

The stack is to be erected in several (pre-assembled) sections, except for the stack base ring, which is directly placed on the anchor bolts. 
煙囪應分段（預組裝）進行吊裝，唯煙囪底座環除外，該底座環直接安裝於地腳螺栓上。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the stack shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
煙囪吊裝之施工計畫書／風險評估及吊裝計畫應由安裝承攬商負責編撰。

The erection sequence for the stack is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
煙囪之吊裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

### 12.1.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the stack . 
煙囪吊裝所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement 
- 施工計畫書

- Work method statement 
- 施工計畫書

- FQP 
- 施工品質計畫

- Bolt torque procedure 
- 螺栓扭力施工程序

- WPS / PQR / WPQ 
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序檢定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格檢定紀錄 (WPQ)

- Weld typical / record 
- 銲接典型細節 / 銲接紀錄

- Welding consumable handling procedure 
- 銲接材料管理作業程序

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications 
- 非破壞檢測作業程序 / 人員資格認證

- :  Erection stack / outlet duct. 
- :  煙囪 / 出口煙道吊裝。

- :  Erection scaffolding stack / outlet duct. 
- :  煙囪 / 出口煙道施工架搭設。

- :  HRSG stack. 
- :  熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 煙囪。

- :  Non pressure parts. 
- :  非受壓組件。

- :  Non-pressure parts. 
- :  非受壓組件。

- :  Non-pressure parts. 
- :  非受壓組件。

- :  Non-pressure parts. 
- :  非受壓組件。

- :  Non-pressure parts. 
- :  非受壓組件。

### 12.1.3. Stack base ring 煙囪底座環

Before Erection of the segments of stack base ring, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在吊裝煙囪底座環分段之前，需預先完成各項準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與作業程序應備妥，並經權責單位（或人員）審核。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/作業需已完成，且適用時應於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。

   - Foundation ready 
   - 基礎已就緒

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗 (OSD 報告)

- Placement of the base plate shims for stack base ring. 
- 安裝煙囪底座環之底板填隙片。

- Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for erection of the stack 
- 準備煙囪吊裝所需之施工架或吊籠 (Sky climbers)。

- Prepare the tools required for erection of the stack 
- 準備煙囪吊裝所需之工具。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Scaffolding and sky climbers based on applicable work method statements. 
- 施工架與吊籠應依據適用之施工計畫書執行。

- Parallel to the erection of the stack other activities can be carried out. 
- 其他作業可與煙囪吊裝同步進行。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業釋放

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 隨著本章節所述作業之順利完成，後續作業已獲准進行：

   - External insulation (if any) 
   - 外部保溫（若有）

   - Erection subsequent stack sections. 
   - 後續煙囪區段之吊裝。

   - Grouting of stack base ring. 
   - 煙囪基座環之無收縮水泥灌漿。

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the segments for stack base ring 
- 吊裝、組裝並點銲煙囪基座環之分段。

- Before erection of stack base ring segments can commence, it is important to place shims with the correct elevation and on the correct location on the foundation. Shimming can be required to obtain an equally leveled and correctly elevated foundation for the stack segments. 
- 在開始煙囪基座環分段吊裝前，務必於基礎上正確標高及位置處放置墊片。為使煙囪分段基礎達到水平並符合設計標高，可能需要進行墊片調整。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Any shims placed (for levelling of stack base ring) shall be installed under the flanges and shall not protrude. 
- 任何放置之墊片（用於煙囪基座環水平調整）均須安裝於法蘭下方，且不得外露。

- Before erection of the segments, clearly mark the 0, 90, 180 and 270 degrees references. 
- 於分段吊裝前，應清楚標示 0、90、180 及 270 度之基準線。

- During erection check the position of the segments longitudinal seams. 
- 吊裝期間應檢查分段縱向銲道之位置。

- During assembly frequently verify the elevation, dimensions and roundness of the stack part. 
- 組裝期間應頻繁核對煙囪構件之標高、尺寸及圓度。

- Stack segments stability shall be ensured by having guy wires secured at several points. 
- 應透過多點固定之拉線確保煙囪分段之穩定性。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the longitudinal seams of the stack base ring sections. 
- 銲接煙囪基座環區段之縱向銲道。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接作業請遵循工程圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型標準。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序執行品質管制作業。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check fit-up of segments and position of longitudinal seams before welding 
- 於銲接前，檢查節段的組裝間隙及縱向銲縫位置。

- Check elevation and roundness of the stack section 1 before welding. 
- 於銲接前，檢查第一節煙囪段的高程與真圓度。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 放行時須檢附遺留項目清單（如有）。

#### Erect field parts 現場安裝組件

Field parts for the stack can be stiffener plates, U-channels, secondary steel supporting and platforms. Identify all required field parts indicated on the drawings. 
煙囪的現場安裝組件可能包含加勁板、U型槽鋼、二次鋼結構支撐及平台。請確認圖面上標示的所有必要現場組件。

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the field parts 
- 安裝、組配並點銲現場組件。

_Note:_ 註：

- Follow the typical for the field parts on the drawings. 
- 現場組件安裝請遵循圖面上的典型細部說明。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld the field parts. 
- 執行現場組件之銲接。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面及銲接程序書 (WPS) 之細部說明或典型範例進行銲接。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的施工品質計畫 及/或作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 放行時須檢附遺留項目清單（如有）。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for measurements of the stack base ring to be in accordance with the tolerances mentioned on the applicable tolerance drawings (60031-730-06-series). 
- 製造商應進行目視檢查，並審閱煙囪底座環的實際測量報告，以確保其符合適用公差圖（60031-730-06 系列）中所述之公差要求。

### 12.1.4. Subsequent stack sections (field installed) 後續煙囪段（現場安裝）

The stack sections between stack base ring and the stack damper will be erected in location. 
位於煙囪底座環與煙囪擋板之間的煙囪節段將於現場進行安裝。

Before Erection of the segments of the subsequent stack sections, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在安裝後續煙囪節段之前，需預先準備部分作業項目。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須到位，並由相關權責單位完成審核。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用規定於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Stack base ring ready
   - 煙囪基座環已準備就緒

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)
   - 材料已到場，並完成數量與品質檢驗（OSD 報告）

- Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for installation of the stack
- 準備用於煙囪安裝之施工架或吊籠。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - External insulation (if any)
- 待本段落活動順利完成後，放行下列活動：- 外層保溫（若有）。

   - Erection stack damper.
   - 煙囪擋板安裝。

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the subsequent stack sections onto the stack base ring and previously erected sections. _Note:_
- 將後續煙囪分節吊裝、組對並進行點銲固定於煙囪基座環及先前已完成吊裝的分節上。_註：_

   - During erection check position, elevation and alignment of stack sections.
   - 吊裝期間須檢查煙囪分節之位置、標高及中心對齊度。

   - Perform “0-measurements” on wall thickness, as per client requirements.
   - 依業主要求執行壁厚「零點量測」。

   - Erected stack part to be secured by use of guy wires at several locations.
   - 已吊裝之煙囪部位須於多處使用拉桿鋼索進行固定。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

- _Note:_
- _註：_

   - Check the fit-up between subsequent stack sections
   - 檢查後續煙囪分節間之組對情形。

   - Regularly check dimension, elevation and roundness for erected stack sections.
   - 定期檢查已吊裝煙囪分節之尺寸、標高及圓度。

#### Welding 銲接作業

• Weld subsequent stack sections onto the stack base ring and previously erected sections. _Note:_ 
• 將後續的煙囪分節銲接至煙囪基座環以及先前已吊裝完成的分節上。註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 所示之銲接細節或典型工法。

#### Quality control 品質管制
#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用的施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check elevation and roundness of erected stack section 
- 檢查已吊裝煙囪分節之標高與圓度。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 檢附待辦事項清單（如有）進行釋放。

- Manufacturer shall visually check and review the actual survey report for measurements of the stack base ring to be in accordance with the tolerances mentioned on the applicable tolerance drawings (60031-730-06-series). 
- 製造商應執行目視檢查，並審閱煙囪基座環之實際測量報告，以確保符合相關容許誤差圖面 (60031-730-06 系列) 所述之公差規範。

### 12.1.5. Stack reinforcement structure 煙囪補強結構
### 12.1.5. Stack reinforcement structure 煙囪補強結構

The stack reinforcement structure gives rigidness to the stack at the stack location where the outlet duct is connected. 
煙囪補強結構旨在於出口煙道連接處之煙囪位置提供結構剛性。

Before Erection of the reinforcement structure, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在吊裝補強結構前，須預先完成部分作業準備。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須到位，並經相關責任單位審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用規定於施工品質計畫 中簽核完成。

   - Field erected stack sections ready 
   - 現場煙囪分節已就緒

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已點收並進行數量與品質檢查 (OSD 報告)

- Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for erection of the stack reinforcement structure 
- 準備用於吊裝煙囪補強結構之施工架及/或懸吊式工作台。

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業
#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 本段落作業順利完成後，得釋放進行下列活動：

   - Erection bottom of the stack 
   - 煙囪底部吊裝作業

- Erection stack damper
- 煙囪擋板安裝

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect, fit and weld the steel structure.
- 鋼結構吊裝、組裝及銲接。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Do not forget to erect the support and closing plates during erection of the rear side wireframe.
- 於安裝後側線架時，切勿遺漏支撐板與封閉板之安裝。

- During erection check the correct position of the steel structure.
- 安裝期間需檢查鋼結構之定位是否正確。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the structure.
- 結構體銲接。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS.
- 請遵循施工圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中關於銲接之細部要求或典型規範。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the inside wireframe for completeness.
- 檢查內部線架之完整性。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 若有缺失項目，須列出清單後方可放行。

- 12.1.7. Stack damper 煙囪擋板

The stack damper has already been pre-assembled. See chapter: HRSG Pre-assembly. 
煙囪擋板已完成預組裝。請參閱「HRSG 預組裝」章節。

Before Erection of the pre-assembled stack damper, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在進行預組裝煙囪擋板之吊裝作業前，需預先準備若干作業事項。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書需備妥，並由權責單位完成審核。

- • The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.

- - Field erected stack sections ready 
- - 現場安裝之煙囪分段已就緒
- - Inside wireframe ready 
- - 內部線架已就緒
- - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)

- Release subsequent activities 
- 後續作業之放行

- • 隨著本段落各項作業順利完成，核准進行下列活動：
- - Erection remaining (pre-assembled) stack sections. 
- - 吊裝剩餘的（預組裝）煙囪分段。
- - Stack drain line 
- - 煙囪排放管線

- Erection 
- 吊裝
- • Erect the pre-assembled stack damper onto the field installed stack sections including the drain piping system. 
- • 將預組裝之煙囪擋板吊裝至現場已安裝之煙囪分段上，包含排放管路系統。
- • Fit and tack-weld the stack damper 
- • 進行煙囪擋板之組裝與定位銲
- _Note:_ 
- _註：_
- - Lifting and erection to take place according the relevant drawing and handling instructions. The supplier documentation can be found using document 60031-730-01-006 “Supplier conservation storage, handling and installation procedures”. 
- - 起吊與安裝作業須依據相關圖說與搬運說明書執行。供應商文件可參閱文件編號 60031-730-01-006 “供應商保存儲放、搬運與安裝程序”。

- - Keep the crane connected during the fit-up, as per work method statement. 
- - 依據施工計畫書，組裝期間吊車應保持掛鉤狀態。
- - During erection check position and alignment of the stack damper 
- - 吊裝期間應檢查煙囪擋板之位置與對準情形。
- - After tack-welding remove the temporary transport bracings 
- - 定位銲完成後，拆除臨時運輸支撐架。

- Welding 
- 銲接
- • Weld the stack damper to the field installed stack sections 
- • 將煙囪擋板銲接至現場安裝之煙囪分段。
- _Note:_ 
- _註：_
- - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- - 遵循圖說與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之銲接細節或標準圖示。

- Quality control 
- 品質管制

- _註：_

-    - Stack damper drain line to be installed based on Chapter “Piping” 
-    - 煙囪擋板排放管線應依據「管路」章節進行安裝。

-    - After acceptance of the damper install the driver, driver connection and protection. 
-    - 擋板驗收合格後，安裝驅動器、驅動連結裝置與保護罩。

-    - After removal of the internal scaffolding stack perform a trial run (by hand) to verify free movement of the damper blades. 
-    - 拆除內部施工架後，進行試運轉（手動），以確認擋板葉片作動順暢。

### 12.1.8. Remaining -pre-assembled- stack sections 剩餘（預組裝）煙囪分段
For the pre-assembled stack sections, follow steps as indicated in the previous paragraph “Subsequent stack sections” for the erection/welding and quality control of the remaining pre-assembled stack sections. 
針對預組裝之煙囪分段，其吊裝/銲接與品質管制應遵循前述「後續煙囪分段」章節所指引之步驟執行。

### 12.1.9. Grouting stack 煙囪灌漿
Grouting of the base ring of the stack is based on Chapter “ _Grouting_ ”. Follow the execution and quality steps mentioned in this chapter. 
煙囪底座環之灌漿作業依據「灌漿」章節辦理。遵循該章節中所述之施工與品質步驟。

### 12.1.10. Final inspection of the boiler stack 鍋爐煙囪最終檢驗
When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成時，應進行檢驗。遺留缺失事項應彙整至待辦事項清單中，並附於最終檢驗合格證書。

The Final inspection Certificate of the stack describes the systems or components inspected. 
煙囪最終檢驗合格證書應記載已完成檢驗之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages.
- 最終檢驗證明書中所提及之所有系統或特定組件群組，均應進行最終檢驗，以確認其安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down.
- 現場步檢後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in :
- 若適用待辦事項清單，應將其分類為：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items)
   - 於水壓試驗前需解決之項目（A類項目）

   - - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items)
   - - 於熱試運轉前需解決之項目（B類項目） - 於暫時驗收（PAC）前需解決之項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認相關系統之施工品質計畫 已由所有相關方簽署。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list
- 確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

## 12.2. Outlet duct erection 12.2. 出口煙道安裝

This paragraph describes the erection of the outlet duct.
本章節說明出口煙道的安裝作業。

### 12.2.1. General 12.2.1. 概述

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the outlet duct shall be prepared by the erection contractor.
出口煙道安裝工程之施工方法說明書/風險評估及吊裝計畫，應由安裝承攬商編製。

The erection sequence for the outlet duct is shown in document 60031-730-05-001.
出口煙道的安裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

- 12.2.2. Documents and procedures 12.2.2. 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the outlet duct .
出口煙道安裝所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement :  Erection stack / outlet duct.
- 施工方法說明書：排氣煙囪/出口煙道安裝。

- - Work method statement :  Erection scaffolding stack / outlet duct. - FQP :  HRSG outlet duct. - Bolt torque procedure :  Non pressure parts. - WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts. - Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts. - Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts. - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts.
- - 施工方法說明書：排氣煙囪/出口煙道施工架搭設。 - 施工品質計畫：HRSG出口煙道。 - 螺栓扭力程序：非受壓組件。 - 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序檢定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工檢定紀錄 (WPQ)：非受壓組件。 - 銲接典型圖/紀錄：非受壓組件。 - 銲材處理程序：非受壓組件。 - 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序/人員資格：非受壓組件。

### 12.2.3. erection of outlet duct bottom panel 12.2.3. 出口煙道底板安裝

Before erection of the outlet duct can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在進行出口煙道安裝之前，需先行完成部分準備作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與前提條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須已到位，並經相關負責方審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. - Stack
- 下列準備工作/活動需已完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽署。- 排氣煙囪

- Flange connection boiler 
- 鍋爐法蘭連接 

- Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
- 材料進場及數量與品質檢驗 (OSD 報告) 

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業釋放 

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - erection right / left side ducting panels after scaffolding. 
- 本章節作業順利完成後，准予執行下列後續作業：- 施工架搭設後之左右側煙道板吊裝。 

#### Erection 安裝工程 

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom ducting panel from the boiler side to the stack side. 
- 由鍋爐側至煙囪側，進行底部煙道板的吊裝、定位及點銲固定。 

#### _Note:_ 註： 

- Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the bottom duct (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such a way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other. 
- 於鍋爐爐牆外殼板法蘭與底部煙道之間放置間距定位塊（定位塊厚度應與波紋伸縮接頭寬度一致）。調整法蘭位置，確保法蘭螺栓孔對正且相互吻合。 

After correct alignment, connect the supports to the stack base ring. 
- 完成正確對位後，將支撐連接至煙囪基座環。 

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔對位偏差，必須經與原廠諮詢確認後方可進行調整。 

- Align the bottom panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side. 
- 將各底部煙道板相互對齊並與煙囪側對正，必要時調整連接處，並將煙道板彼此點銲固定及銲接於煙囪側。 

- Where necessary place temporary supporting for stability of the bottom panels. 
- 必要時，設置臨時支撐以確保底部煙道板的穩定性。 

#### Welding 銲接作業 

- Weld the bottom ducting (splices) and stack side connection. 
- 銲接底部煙道（接合處）及煙囪側連接部。 

#### _Note:_ 註： 

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接應遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型做法。 

#### Quality control 品質管制 

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。 

#### _Note:_ 註： 

- Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查組裝間隙、高程及尺寸。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 發布並附上待辦事項清單（如有）。

### 12.2.4. Scaffolding outlet duct (right or left) “outside” 12.2.4. 出口煙道（右側或左側）「外側」施工架架設

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for erection of scaffolding, shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
施工架架設之施工計畫書／風險評估及吊裝計畫，應由安裝承包商準備。

Before erection of the outlet duct scaffolding can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始架設出口煙道施工架之前，需預先準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備作業與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須到位，並由相關責任方進行審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作／活動必須完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中簽核。

   - Bottom outlet duct panel installed 
   - 出口煙道底部面板已安裝完成

#### Release subsequent activities 釋放後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection right / left side ducting panels. 
- 本段落作業順利完成後，即釋放進行下列作業：- 吊裝右側／左側煙道面板。

#### Erection 吊裝／組裝

- Scaffolding to be erected along the “outside” of the outlet duct right or left side. 
- 施工架應沿出口煙道右側或左側之「外側」架設。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Erect the scaffolding in such way that all components to be erected can be easily reached. 
- 架設施工架時，須確保所有待安裝之組件皆可輕易觸及。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依照適用之施工品質計畫 及／或程序書執行品質管制工作。

#### _Note:_ 註：

   - Verify scaffolding for proper access and assembly. 
   - 確認施工架之作業動線及組裝狀況是否妥適。

- 12.2.5. Outlet duct right or left panel 12.2.5. 出口煙道右側或左側面板

Erect the outlet duct sidewall on the side where the scaffolding is erected during the previous step. 
於前一步驟已架設施工架之一側，進行出口煙道側牆面板之吊裝。

Before erection of the outlet duct side panel can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在出口煙道側板開始吊裝作業前，需預先完成下列準備活動。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並由權責單位（或相關方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Bottom outlet duct panel erected 
   - 出口煙道底部板件已吊裝完成

   - Scaffolding outlet duct right or left side erected 
   - 出口煙道左側或右側施工架已搭設完成

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動釋放

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 隨著本段落活動順利完成，可執行下列後續活動：

   - Erection outlet duct opposite side wall panels 
   - 出口煙道對側牆板之吊裝

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the right or left outlet side wall panels between the boiler and stack 
- 於鍋爐與煙囪之間吊裝、組裝並定位銲接出口煙道左側或右側牆板。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the sidewall ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other. 
- 於鍋爐爐牆外殼板法蘭與煙道側牆板之間放置間隙填隙片（填隙片厚度應代表波紋伸縮接頭之寬度）。調整法蘭位置，使法蘭螺栓孔對正且相互吻合。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，須於諮詢製造商後方可進行調整。

- Align the sidewall panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side. 
- 對齊各側牆板及煙囪側，必要時調整連接處，並將各板件間以及與煙囪側進行定位銲接。

- Where necessary place temporary supporting. 
- 必要時設置臨時支撐。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the sidewall ducting (splices) and stack side connections. 
- 銲接煙道側牆板（接合處）及煙囪側之連接點。

- Weld the sidewall ducting to the bottom ducting. 
- 將煙道側牆板銲接至底部煙道板件。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding.
- 銲接前須檢查組裝間隙、標高及尺寸。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any).
- 釋出時須附上待辦事項清單（若有）。

### 12.2.6. Scaffolding outlet duct opposite side 出口煙道對側施工架架設

Erect the outlet duct scaffolding on the opposite side of the previously erected outlet duct sidewall scaffolding. For requirements see also chapter 11.2.4.
於先前已架設之出口煙道側牆施工架對側，進行出口煙道施工架架設。相關要求請參閱第 11.2.4 章。

### 12.2.7. Outlet duct opposite sidewall casing 出口煙道對側側牆爐牆外殼板

在剩餘側牆煙道板件開始吊裝前，需預先完成部分準備工作。

   - Outlet duct baffles (silencers) installed
   - 已安裝出口煙道導流板（消音器）
