- 本段落各項作業順利完成後，准予進行下列作業：

   - Installation outlet duct top panels.
   - 安裝出口煙道頂板。

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the opposite outlet side wall panels between the boiler and stack and the bracing frame between the right and left outlet duct side walls
- 吊裝、組對並點銲鍋爐與煙囪間之出口側牆板件，以及左右出口煙道側牆間之支撐框架。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the sidewall ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other.
- 於鍋爐爐牆外殼板法蘭與側牆煙道之間放置間隔墊塊（間隔墊塊寬度應對應伸縮接頭之寬度）。對齊法蘭，確保法蘭螺栓孔吻合並相互正對。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.
- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，僅能於諮詢原廠後方可進行調整。

- Align the sidewall panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side. 
- 將側牆板彼此對齊並與煙囪側對齊，必要時調整連接部位，並將板件與煙囪側進行點銲固定。

- Where necessary place temporary supporting. 
- 必要時設置臨時支撐。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the sidewall ducting (splices) and stack side connections. 
- 銲接側牆風道（接合處）及煙囪側連接處。

- Weld the sidewall ducting to the bottom ducting. 
- 將側牆風道銲接至底部風道。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 請遵循圖面及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 所示之銲接細節或典型做法。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查組裝間隙、高程及尺寸。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有任何遺留項目，應列出清單後再行釋放後續作業。

### 12.2.8. Outlet duct baffles (silencers) 出口風道導流板（消音器）

在開始安裝出口風道導流板之前，需先行準備相關作業。

   - Bottom outlet duct panel installed

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- 支撐組裝後，應進行尺寸檢查。

#### Erection lower outlet baffles (silencers) 下部出口導流板（消音器）之吊裝

- Install the lower outlet baffles. Start the erection from the side where the outlet duct casing is already installed. 
- 安裝下部出口導流板。請從已安裝出口煙道爐牆外殼板之側開始吊裝作業。

- Follow the supplier erection instructions and drawing details for lifting and erection. 
- 吊裝與安裝作業應遵循供應商之安裝說明書及施工圖細節。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

   - Follow the supplier erection instructions and drawing details for lifting and erection. -  During erection check position and elevation of the baffles -  Verify the baffles are mounted in the support system without damaging the baffles. -  Install the connection strips during erection and apply the correct torque for bolting. -  Remove the lifting eye-bolts after erection. 
   - 吊裝與安裝作業應遵循供應商之安裝說明書及施工圖細節。 - 吊裝期間應檢查導流板之位置與標高。 - 確認導流板安裝於支撐系統時，未對導流板造成損壞。 - 於安裝期間裝設連接條，並依規定之扭矩進行螺栓鎖固。 - 吊裝完成後，拆除吊裝用吊環螺栓。

- Erection of scaffolding for the outlet sections _Note:_ 
- 出口段施工架之架設 _註：_

   - Scaffolding to be placed up and downstream of the outlet baffles. 
   - 施工架應設置於出口導流板之上游與下游處。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld the lower baffle support system. _Note:_ -  Follow the details and typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接下部導流板支撐系統。_註：_ - 銲接作業應遵循施工圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節及典型工法。

- Erection upper outlet baffles (silencers) 上部出口導流板（消音器）之吊裝

- • Install the upper outlet baffles on top of the lower outlet baffles. Start the erection from the side where the outlet duct casing is already installed. 
- • 將上部出口導流板安裝於下部出口導流板上方。請從已安裝出口煙道爐牆外殼板之側開始吊裝作業。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Follow the supplier erection instructions and drawing details for lifting and erection. 
- 吊裝與安裝作業應遵循供應商之安裝說明書及施工圖細節。

- During erection check position and elevation of the baffles 
- 吊裝期間應檢查導流板之位置與標高。

- Install the connection strips during erection and apply the correct torque for bolting. 
- 於安裝期間裝設連接板，並針對螺栓施加正確之鎖固扭力。

- Remove the lifting eye-bolts after erection. 
- 安裝作業完成後，拆除吊裝用吊環螺栓。

#### Quality control 品質管制
品質管制

Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依照適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
_Note:_ 註：

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
   - 應連同待辦事項清單（若有）一併釋出/放行。

   - The upper baffle support system is installed after acceptance of the outlet duct top casing. 
   - 上部導流板支撐系統須於出口煙道爐牆外殼板驗收合格後，方可進行安裝。

- 12.2.9. Outlet duct top panel 12.2.9. 出口煙道頂板
- 12.2.9. Outlet duct top panel 12.2.9. 出口煙道頂板

Before erection of the outlet top panels panels can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
- 在進行出口煙道頂板安裝作業前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並經權責單位（或相關方）審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須完成，且若適用時，須於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Outlet duct left and right sidewall panels erected 
   - 出口煙道左、右側牆板已安裝完成。

#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續作業
#### Release subsequent activities 放行後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection expansion joint between outlet duct and boiler. 
- 待本段落之活動順利完成後，放行下列作業：- 鍋爐與出口煙道間之波紋伸縮接頭安裝。

   - Upper stack baffle support system. 
   - 上部煙囪導流板支撐系統。

#### Erection 安裝作業
#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the outlet top panels from the boiler side to the stack side. 
- 由鍋爐側向煙囪側方向，吊裝、組裝並執行出口頂板之定位銲。

#### _Note:_ 註：
#### _Note:_ 註：

- Place distance holders between the boiler casing flange and the top ducting (distance holder shall represent the width of the expansion joint). Align the flanges in such way that the flange bolt holes match and are opposite to each other. 
- 於爐牆外殼板法蘭與頂部風道之間放置間距定位塊（間距定位塊之厚度應等同於波紋伸縮接頭之寬度）。對正法蘭使法蘭螺栓孔相互吻合且相對。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 當發現螺栓孔不對正時，僅能在諮詢原製造廠後方可進行調整。

- Align the top panels to each other and to the stack side, adjust the connections where necessary and tack-weld the panels together and to the stack side. 
- 將頂部板件相互對齊並與煙囪側對齊，必要時調整連接處，並將板件之間及與煙囪側進行點銲固定。

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld the top ducting (splices) and the stack side connections. 
- 銲接頂部風道（接合處）及煙囪側連接處。

- Weld the top ducting to the sidewall ducting. 
- 銲接頂部風道與側牆風道。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接細節或典型構造請遵循設計圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS)。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check fit-up, elevation and dimensions before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查組裝間隙、標高及尺寸。

- Erection of outlet duct upper baffle support system as per paragraph “outlet duct baffles”, located in this chapter. 
- 依據本章「出口風道導流板」段落進行出口風道上方導流板支撐系統之安裝。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有未結項目，應連同未結項目清單一併發布。

### 12.2.10. Final inspection of the outlet duct 出口風道最終檢查

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。未結項目應彙整於未結項目清單中，並附於最終檢查證明書後。

The Final inspection Certificate of the outlet duct describes the systems or components inspected. 
出口風道最終檢查證明書應載明所檢查之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢查

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 所有列於最終檢查證明書上之系統或特定組件群，均須進行最終檢查，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢後應立即建立未結項目清單（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若有未結項目清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前須解決之項目（A類項目）

- - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
- - 熱試車前須解決之項目（B類項目）- 暫定驗收（PAC）前須解決之項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_  註：

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list 
- 確認相關系統之施工品質計畫 已由各參與單位簽署。未結項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。未結項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

# 13. INLET DUCT 入口煙道

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列段落：

# 1. Inlet duct main steel structure 1. 入口煙道主鋼結構

# 2. Inlet Duct erection 2. 入口煙道吊裝

# 3. Final inspection of the inlet duct 3. 入口煙道最終檢驗

- :  paragraph 13.1 
- ：第 13.1 段

- :  paragraph 13.2 
- ：第 13.2 段

- :  paragraph 13.3 
- ：第 13.3 段

## 13.1. Inlet duct main steel structure 13.1. 入口煙道主鋼結構

This paragraph describes the erection of the inlet duct main steel structure. 
本段說明入口煙道主鋼結構之吊裝作業。

### 13.1.1. General 13.1.1. 概述

The inlet duct consists out of a main steel structure containing the bottom, side and top ducting. The inlet duct is connected directly to the HRSG duct. In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerance the flange connection for the compensator to the GT duct contains an adjustable flange connection. 
入口煙道由包含底部、側面及頂部導管之主鋼結構所組成。入口煙道直接與熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 煙道連接。為補償吊裝及製造公差，連接至氣渦輪機 (GT) 煙道之補償器法蘭連接處設有可調式法蘭連接設計。

Erection of the inlet duct takes place from the HRSG duct towards to inlet duct. 
入口煙道之吊裝作業順序係由 HRSG 煙道向入口煙道方向進行。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the inlet duct main steel structure shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
入口煙道主鋼結構吊裝之施工計畫書／風險評估及吊裝計畫應由安裝承攬商編製。

The erection sequence for the inlet duct main steel structure is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
入口煙道主鋼結構之吊裝順序詳見 60031-730-05-001 號文件。

### 13.1.2. Documents and procedures 13.1.2. 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the inlet duct main steel structure . 
入口煙道主鋼結構吊裝所需之文件與程序。

   - Work method statement :  Erection inlet duct. 
   - 施工計畫書：入口煙道吊裝。

   - - FQP :  HRSG inlet duct. 
   - - 施工品質計畫：HRSG 入口煙道。

- Bolt torque procedure :  Non pressure parts.
- 螺栓扭力作業程序：非受壓組件。

- WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts.
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格紀錄 (WPQ)：非受壓組件。

- Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts.
- 銲接典型圖 / 紀錄：非受壓組件。

- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts.
- 銲接耗材管理程序：非受壓組件。

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts.
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格：非受壓組件。

- 13.1.3. Steel structure 13.1.3. 鋼結構

Before erection of the steel structure rows can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在開始鋼結構排架吊裝作業前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序必須準備就緒，並由相關負責單位審查完成。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，且適用時需於施工品質計畫 中簽署核可。

   - Foundation ready
   - 基礎已就緒

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗 (OSD 報告)

- Erect the shims underneath the base plates before placement of the goalpost and level to the correct elevation.
- 在門型構架安裝就位前，先於底板下方安裝墊片並調校至正確高程。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- It is important that the shims (for levelling of the inlet duct steel structure portals) are underneath the base plates and do not protrude.
- 重要提示：用於調校入口煙道鋼結構門型構架的墊片，必須放置於底板下方，且不得外露凸出。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動釋放

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Erection Inlet duct bottom panels.
- 隨著本段落活動之順利完成，核准進行下列後續活動：入口煙道底部鋼板吊裝。

#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect the main steel goalpost rows for the inlet duct.
- 吊裝入口煙道之主鋼構門型構架排架。

- Erect the goalpost with the bearing plate and the 2 mm PTFE sliding plate, where applicable. Verify cleanliness of the bearing plate before installation onto the PFTE sliding plate.
- 吊裝門型構架時，應一併安裝支承板及 2 mm PTFE 滑動板（如適用）。在安裝至 PTFE 滑動板上之前，務必確認支承板之潔淨度。

- During erection check for position, alignment and elevation of the inlet duct main steel structure. Adjust position using the guy-wires and/or leveling nuts where required.
- 吊裝期間應檢查入口煙道主鋼結構之位置、軸線校準與高程。必要時，使用拉索 (guy-wires) 及/或調平螺帽進行位置調整。

- Tighten the anchors bolts to their final torque value, once the steel structure is adjusted. 
- 於鋼結構調整完成後，將地錨螺栓鎖緊至最終扭力值。

#### _Note:_  _註：_

- Closely monitor the steel structure coordinates during installation. 
- 於安裝期間需密切監控鋼結構之座標。

- Perform a survey for correct position, alignment and elevation of the steel structure when in position. 
- 待鋼結構定位後，應進行測量以確保其位置、軸線對正及高程正確。

- - Use the applicable torque value for tightening of the anchor bolts. 
- - 地錨螺栓鎖緊作業應使用適用之扭力值。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔對位不準，須經與製造廠諮詢確認後方可進行調整。

#### Quality control 品質控制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序書執行品質控制作業。

#### _Note:_  _註：_

- Compare the dimensional reports of the survey with the manufacturer tolerance drawings. 
- 將測量報告之尺寸數據與製造廠之容許差圖說進行比對。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 經確認無誤後予以放行，若有缺失項目應列出待辦清單 (若有)。

## 13.2. Inlet Duct erection 13.2. 入口煙道吊裝作業

This paragraph describes the erection of the ducting panels for the inlet duct. 
本節描述入口煙道板片之吊裝作業。

### 13.2.1. General 13.2.1. 一般規定

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the erection of the inlet duct panels shall be prepared by the erection contractor. 
入口煙道板片吊裝作業之施工計畫書／風險評估及吊裝計畫應由承攬商編撰。

The erection sequence for the inlet duct is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
入口煙道之吊裝順序詳見文件編號 60031-730-05-001。

- 13.2.2. Documents and procedures 13.2.2. 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for installation of the inlet duct panels . 
入口煙道板片安裝所需之文件與程序。

- Work method statement :  Erection inlet duct. 
- 施工計畫書：入口煙道吊裝。
- Work method statement :  Erection scaffolding inlet duct. 
- 施工計畫書：入口煙道施工架搭設。
- FQP :  HRSG inlet duct. 
- 施工品質計畫：HRSG 入口煙道。
- Bolt torque procedure :  Non pressure parts. 
- 螺栓扭力程序書：非壓力組件。
- WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲工資格紀錄 (WPQ)：非壓力組件。
- Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 典型銲道 / 紀錄：非壓力組件。
- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 銲接材料管理程序書：非壓力組件。
- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts. 
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序書 / 人員資格：非壓力組件。

### 13.2.3. Inlet duct bottom panels 13.2.3. 入口煙道底部板片

Before Erection of the inlet duct bottom panels can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
於開始進行入口煙道底部板片吊裝前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落中提及之文件及程序需備妥並由權責單位（或相關單位）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並視適用情況於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。

   - Steel structure inlet duct 
   - 進氣風道鋼結構

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料收貨及數量與品質檢驗（OSD 開箱短溢報告）

- Prepare the scaffolding and or sky climbers for installation of the inlet duct casing panels. 
- 準備進氣風道爐牆外殼板安裝所需之施工架或懸吊式工作台。

- Prepare the tools required for erection of the inlet duct. 
- 準備進氣風道吊裝所需之工具。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行
#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Sidewall panels inlet duct. 
- 本段落所述活動順利完成後，准予進行下列活動：- 進氣風道側牆板。

   - Internal insulation of bottom splices. 
   - 底部接縫處之內部保溫隔熱棉安裝。

#### Erection 吊裝作業
#### Erection 吊裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the bottom duct panels to the inlet duct steel structure and the boiler casing. 
- 將風道底板吊裝、組對並點銲固定於進氣風道鋼結構及爐牆外殼板上。

#### _Note:_ 注意事項： _Note:_

- The inlet duct bottom panel erection is done from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine. 
- 進氣風道底板吊裝作業應由鍋爐側向燃氣渦輪機側方向進行，因可調式法蘭接頭（用於補償吊裝與製造公差）位於與燃氣渦輪機之連接處。

- During erection of the bottom duct, erect the supports on the steel structure bottom girders and tack weld. 
- 風道底部吊裝期間，應將支撐件安裝於鋼結構底部大樑上並進行點銲。

- Align the bottom duct panels to the correct position and elevation. 
- 將風道底板對正至正確位置與標高。

- Fit all bottom duct panels without gaps. 
- 安裝所有風道底板並確保無縫隙。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，須經與製造商諮詢後方可進行調整。

#### Welding 銲接作業
#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all bottom splices and all supports. 
- 銲接所有底部接縫及所有支撐件。

#### _Note:_ 注意事項： _Note:_

- Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding. Weld outside and/or inside as per drawings. 
- 進氣風道爐牆外殼板銲接應為連續銲道，不得採斷續銲。依據圖說進行外側及/或內側銲接。

- Channel ends need to be seal welded. Before erecting the head plates prepare (grind smooth) the surface for erection of the head plates. 
- 槽鋼末端需進行密封銲接。在吊裝封板前，應預先處理（磨平）表面，以利封板之安裝。

- Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS. 
- 需遵循施工圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中典型銲接的要求。

#### Quality control 品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ _註：_
- Check fit-up, elevations and centerline of the bottom ducting supports and connection plate before welding. 
- 銲接前，應檢查底部風道支撐及連接板之組裝配合度、標高及中心線。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 於釋放作業時，應附上未完成項目清單（如有）。

### 13.2.4. Inlet duct sidewall panels 進氣風道側牆板安裝
Before erection of the side wall panels can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始側牆板吊裝作業前，需預先準備相關工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與前提條件
- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述章節提及之文件與程序必須準備就緒，並經相關權責單位審核。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須已完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核（如適用）。

   - Bottom panels inlet duct erected 
   - 進氣風道底部板件已吊裝完成

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（短缺或損壞報告 OSD）

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業釋放
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 待本章節各項作業順利完成後，方可釋放下列後續作業：

   - Top wall panels inlet duct. 
   - 進氣風道頂部牆板。

   - Internal insulation of field splices. 
   - 現場銲接接頭之內部保溫隔熱工程。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld side wall duct panels. During erection make the support connections to the inlet duct main steel structure where applicable. 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲側牆風道板。在吊裝過程中，適用時應完成與入口風道主鋼結構之支撐連接。

#### _Note:_  ## _註：_

- Side wall ducting to be erected from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine. 
- 側牆風道應由鍋爐側向氣渦輪機側進行吊裝，因可調整式法蘭連接處（旨在補償吊裝與製造誤差）位於與氣渦輪機之連接處。

- During erection of the side duct, install the supports to the steel structure columns for each row. 
- 側風道吊裝期間，應針對每一排架設安裝支撐至鋼結構柱。

- Fit the duct sidewalls to the bottom panels without gaps. 
- 應組對風道側牆與底部板，確保無間隙。

- Ducting has to be gastight, all gaps in corners and at field splices shall be closed (seal welded) with plate (6 mm thickness). 
- 風道必須氣密，所有轉角處及現場接合處之縫隙皆應使用鋼板（厚度 6 mm）封閉（密封銲）。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，必須在諮詢製造商後方可進行調整。

#### Welding side ducting ## 側風道銲接作業

- Weld all side wall panel splices. 
- 銲接所有側牆板接合處。

- Weld the corner connections between the sidewall panels and the bottom panels. 
- 銲接側牆板與底板間之轉角連接處。

- Weld the inlet duct side wall to the boiler side. 
- 銲接入口風道側牆與鍋爐側之連接。

- Weld all supports. 
- 銲接所有支撐。

#### _Note:_ ## _註：_

- Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding. Welding outside and/or inside as per drawings. 
- 入口風道爐牆外殼板銲接應為連續銲，不得點銲。應依據圖說進行外部及/或內部銲接。

- Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接應遵循圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之銲道標準要求。

#### Quality control ## 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ ## _註：_

   - Check fit-up, elevations and side wall connection to the bottom ducting before welding 
   - 銲接前應檢查組對狀況、標高，以及側牆與底部風道之連接。

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
   - 經檢查放行時應附上未完成事項清單（若有）。

- 13.2.5. Inlet duct top panels - 13.2.5. 入口風道頂板

Before Erection of the top wall panels can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
- 在開始吊裝頂板前，需預先準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions ## 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落所提及之文件與程序須備妥，並經負責方（或各負責方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽核。

   - Sidewall panels inlet duct erected 
   - 側牆板入口風道已吊裝完成

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（OSD 報告）

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行
- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 隨著本段落活動之圓滿完成，下列活動可准予放行：

   - Internal insulation field splices. 
   - 內部保溫現場接縫作業。

   - Erection field parts. 
   - 現場零組件安裝。

   - Grouting steel structure rows. 
   - 鋼結構排架無收縮水泥灌漿作業。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the top duct, incl. supports to the steel structure. 
- 吊裝、對位並點銲頂部風道，包含安裝至鋼結構之支撐件。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Top duct to be erected from the boiler side to the gas turbine side, as the adjustable flange connection (In order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances) is located at the connection with the gas turbine. 
- 頂部風道安裝方向須由鍋爐側向氣渦輪機側進行，因可調整式法蘭接頭（用以補償安裝與製造誤差）位於與氣渦輪機之連接處。

- During erection of the top duct, erect the supports to the steel structure for each row 
- 於頂部風道安裝期間，須同時將各排架之支撐件安裝至鋼結構。

- Fit the top duct to the sidewall casing without gaps. 
- 頂部風道與爐牆外殼板之對接須緊密無縫隙。

- Ducting has to be gastight, all gaps in corners and at field splices have to be closed (seal welded) with plate (6 mm thickness). 
- 風道須具備氣密性，所有角落與現場接縫處之縫隙皆須以鋼板（厚度 6 mm）封閉（銲接密封）。

- When a misalignment of the bolt holes is detected, adjustments can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，須經與製造商諮詢後始可進行調整。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all top duct panel splices. 
- 銲接所有頂部風道板塊之接縫。

- Weld the corner connections between the sidewall panels and the top panels. 
- 銲接側牆板與頂板之間的角隅接頭。 

- Weld the inlet duct top to the boiler casing. 
- 銲接入口煙道頂部與爐牆外殼板。 

- Weld all supports. 
- 銲接所有支撐件。 

#### _Note:_ 註： 

- Inlet duct casing welding is continuous, no stitch welding. Weld outside and/or inside as per drawings. 
- 入口煙道爐牆外殼板之銲接須為連續銲，不得跳銲。依據圖說進行內側及/或外側銲接。 

- Channel ends need to be seal welded. Before installing the head plates prepare (grind smooth) the surface for installation of the head plates. 
- 槽鋼端部須施作密封銲。安裝封頭板前，須先處理（研磨平整）表面，以利封頭板安裝。 

- Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS. 
- 遵循圖說及銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中之典型銲接要求。 

#### Quality control 品質管制 

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。 

#### _Note:_ 註： 

   - Check fit-up, elevations and top wall connection to the side ducting before welding 
   - 銲接前檢查組裝間隙、標高及頂牆與側向煙道之連接處。 

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 於釋出時檢附待辦事項清單（若有）。 

- 13.2.6. Grouting of the steel structure 13.2.6. 鋼結構之無收縮水泥灌漿 

Grouting of the inlet duct steel structure is based on the Chapter “ _Grouting_ ” in this manual. Follow the erection and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution. 
入口煙道鋼結構之無收縮水泥灌漿係依據本手冊「無收縮水泥灌漿」章節辦理。執行時請遵循該章節所述之吊裝及品質作業步驟。 

- 13.2.7. Field parts 13.2.7. 現場安裝件 

Before erection of the field parts can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝現場組件前，須先行準備若干作業。 

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與前提條件 

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落所提之文件與程序書須備妥，並由權責單位（或人員）審核完成。 

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並於施工品質計畫 中簽核（如適用）。 

   - Top wall panels inlet duct erected 
   - 入口煙道頂牆板已吊裝完成。 

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量及品質檢驗（OSD 報告）。 

#### Release subsequent activities 釋出後續作業

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 本章節活動順利完成後，准予進行下列活動：

   - Inlet duct adjustable flange connection. 
   - 入口風道可調式法蘭連接。

#### Erection 現場安裝作業

- Erect, fit and tack-weld the head plates, connection plates for connection to the side wall casing. 
- 吊裝、組對並點銲封頭板及與側牆爐牆外殼板連接用之連接板。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- During erection of the head plates verify the weld on the channel ends is in place and grind smooth. 
- 封頭板安裝期間，須確認槽鋼端部之銲道完整並研磨平整。

- Erect all field parts according the typical on the applicable drawings. 
- 依照適用圖面之典型細節，進行所有工地安裝組件之安裝。

#### Welding 銲接作業

- Weld all field parts. 
- 執行所有工地安裝組件之銲接。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings and WPS. 
- 銲接時須遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細節或典型規範。

- All external welds shall be continuous, no stitch welds on the outside allowed. 
- 所有外部銲道均須為連續銲，外部嚴禁使用斷續銲。

- Install all field parts according the typical on the applicable drawings. 
- 依照適用圖面之典型細節，安裝所有工地安裝組件。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書，執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Check the fit-up of field parts before welding. 
- 銲接前應檢查工地組件之組對狀況。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 放行時須檢附待辦事項清單（如有）。

### 13.2.8. Adjustable flange connection 可調式法蘭連接

The HRSG inlet duct is connected to the gas turbine duct using a compensator. The flange connection for this compensator on the HRSG side is made adjustable in order to compensate for erection and fabrication tolerances. 
HRSG 入口風道係透過補償器與氣渦輪機風道連接。為補償安裝與製造誤差，該補償器位於 HRSG 側之法蘭連接處設計為可調式。

Before erection of the adjustable flange connection can start, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝可調式法蘭連接之前，需預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
前述章節提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並由責任單位（或相關單位）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用規定在施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Inlet duct panels and field parts erected. 
   - 入口風道板與工地組件已吊裝完成。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢核（短缺損毀報告 OSD Report）。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
本章節所述工作順利完成後，即放行下列作業：

   - Internal insulation. 
   - 內部保溫隔熱棉施工。

#### General 一般規定

- The flange connection is designed for correction/adjustment in the longitudinal and vertical direction. 
法蘭連接之設計係為了能在縱向與垂直方向進行修正與調整。

- The flange is built-up from : 
法蘭由以下組件構成：

   - An “In head plate” connected to the bottom, side and top ducting. 
   - 連接至底部、側邊與頂部風道的「內部封頭板」。

   - An outside shell plate 
   - 外殼板。

   - A ring for the outside 
   - 外環。

- For an overview of the adjustable flange connection, see the applicable drawings. 
關於可調式法蘭連接之概覽，請參閱相關施工圖說。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect the head plate (vertical ducting plate). 
- 吊裝封頭板（垂直風道板）。

- Erect the outside ring on the head plate and outside shell. 
- 將外環安裝於封頭板與外殼板上。

- Fit and tack-weld the installed flange. 
- 組裝已安裝之法蘭並進行定位銲。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Use distance holders between the adjustable flange of the gas turbine and connection flange on the HRSG side. (Distance holder to represent the width of the expansion joint). 
- 於氣渦輪機可調式法蘭與熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 側連接法蘭之間使用間隙保持器。（間隙保持器係用以呈現波紋伸縮接頭之寬度）。 

- During erection of the distance holders keep the bolt holes for the “flange” on the connection and adjustable flange equal to each other. 
- 於安裝間隙保持器期間，應確保連接法蘭與可調式法蘭之「法蘭」螺栓孔保持對正。 

#### Welding 銲接

- Weld the adjustable flange connection. 
- 銲接可調式法蘭連接處。 

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- DO NOT REMOVE the distance holders. 
- 請勿移除間隙保持器。 

   - These will be removed during installation of the expansion joint connection. 
   - 該組件將於安裝波紋伸縮接頭連接處時移除。 

- Follow the requirements of the weld typical on the drawings and WPS. 
- 應遵循圖面與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之銲道典型要求。 

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或程序書執行品質管制活動。 

#### _Note:_ _註：_

   - Check the fit-up and dimensions before welding. 
   - 銲接前應檢查組裝間隙與尺寸。 

   - Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
   - 釋出時應附上未完成項目清單（若有）。 

   - Manufacturer shall review the actual survey report of the flange connection for, location and elevations according the applicable tolerance drawings 60031-730-06-series. 
   - 製造商應依據適用之公差圖面 60031-730-06 系列，審查法蘭連接處之位置與標高實際測量報告。 

- 13.2.9. Internal Insulation 13.2.9. 內部保溫

Erection for the internal insulation and liner sheeting is based on the Chapter “ _Internal insulation_ ”. Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution. 
內部保溫與不銹鋼內護板之安裝作業係基於「內部保溫」章節。執行過程中應遵循該章節所提及之安裝與品質步驟。 

## 13.3. Final inspection of the inlet duct 13.3. 入口煙道最終檢查

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成後，應進行檢查。 

Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
未完成項目應彙整至未完成項目清單中，並附於最終檢查合格證書內。 

Final inspection for the boiler part is mainly covered by the boiler casing, because all other boiler parts have a separate final inspection round. 
鍋爐本體之最終檢查主要包含爐牆外殼板，因其餘鍋爐組件均有各自獨立的最終檢查程序。 

The Final inspection Certificate of the inlet duct describes the systems or components inspected. 
入口煙道之最終檢查合格證書應載明受檢之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 所有最終檢驗證書中所提及之系統或特定組件群組，均須進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若存在待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前須解決之項目（A類項目）

   - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) 
   - 熱機試運轉前須解決之項目（B類項目）

   - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) 
   - 臨時驗收（PAC）前須解決之項目（C類項目）

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認相關系統之適用施工品質計畫已由各相關方簽署完成。待辦事項須納入待辦清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認所有不符合事項報告（NCR）皆已結案。待辦事項須納入待辦清單中。

# 14. SECONDARY STEEL 二次鋼構

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列段落：

1. General :  paragraph 14.1 
1. 一般規定：第14.1節

2. Documents and procedures :  paragraph 14.2 
2. 文件與程序：第14.2節

3. Secondary steel (and hoisting beam erection) :  paragraph 14.3 
3. 二次鋼構（及起吊樑安裝）：第14.3節

4. Grouting secondary steel :  paragraph 14.4 
4. 二次鋼構灌漿：第14.4節

5. Final inspection of secondary steel and hoisting beams :  paragraph 14.5 
5. 二次鋼構與起吊樑之最終檢驗：第14.5節

## 14.1. General 一般規定

The described erection for secondary steel components is set-up generally and applies for all secondary steel erection works. 
上述之二次鋼構組件安裝方式為通則，適用於所有二次鋼構安裝工程。

Specific requirements as a part of the erection for secondary steel are mentioned in the relevant chapter or paragraph (if any). 
二次鋼構安裝工程之特殊要求，將於相關章節或段落中載明（若有）。

During erection of the HRSG it is important to combine the installation of secondary steel with the piping (supports) systems and scaffolding erection. 
在熱回收鍋爐（HRSG）安裝期間，務必將二次鋼構之安裝與管線（支撐）系統及施工架（鷹架）搭設作業進行整合。

Discuss and coordinate the erection of secondary steel, piping and scaffolding with the relevant parties on site in order to form and achieve a good plan for erection, in an early stage of the project. 
應於專案初期與現場相關單位討論並協調二次鋼構、管線及施工架之安裝事宜，以規劃並達成完善的安裝計畫。

Manufactures advice is to erect the piping (supports) systems before erection of the secondary steel, where possible. In some cases piping supports are part of the secondary steel. 
製造商建議在可行情況下，優先安裝管線（支撐）系統，再進行二次鋼構安裝。部分案例中，管線支撐屬於二次鋼構之一部分。

The erection sequence for secondary steel is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
二次鋼構之安裝順序請參照文件 60031-730-05-001。

## 14.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序

- Documents and procedures required for installation of the secondary steel (and hoisting beams .) 
- 二次鋼構（及起吊樑）安裝所需之文件與程序：

- Work method statement :  Erection secondary steel 
- 工作說明書：二次鋼構安裝

- Work method statement :  Scaffolding secondary steel 
- 工作說明書：二次鋼構施工架搭設

- FQP :  HRSG secondary steel 
- 施工品質計畫：HRSG二次鋼構

- Bolt torque procedure :  Non-pressure parts 
- 螺栓扭力程序：非受壓組件

- WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts 
- 銲接程序規範（WPS）/ 銲接程序評定紀錄（PQR）/ 銲工資格紀錄（WPQ）：非受壓組件

- Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts 
- 典型銲道 / 紀錄：非受壓組件

- Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts 
- 銲材管理程序：非受壓組件

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts 
- 非破壞檢測（NDE）程序 / 人員資格：非受壓組件

## 14.3. Secondary steel (and hoisting beam) erection 二次鋼構（及起吊樑）安裝

Erection of secondary steel and hoisting beams as pre-assembled or loose components. 
二次鋼構及起吊樑之安裝方式，採預組裝件或散裝組件進行。

Before erection of the secondary steel can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在次要鋼結構開始吊裝作業前，須先行完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書須備妥，並經負責單位（或相關方）審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作與活動須已完成，並依適用規定於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 已完成材料點收與品質檢驗（OSD 開箱檢驗報告）。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續活動放行 

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: 
- 本段落作業順利完成後，方可放行進行下列活動：

   - Grouting (where applicable) 
   - 無收縮水泥灌漿作業（若適用）。

#### Erection 吊裝作業 

- Erect the pre-assembled components or loose parts. 
- 進行預組裝構件或散件之吊裝。

- Erect loose parts like, columns, beams, bracings, stairs, handrail and grating according the piece mark drawings. _Note:_ 
- 依據構件標示圖吊裝散件，如：鋼柱、鋼樑、斜撐、樓梯、扶手及格柵板。_註：_

   - Erect the shims (under the base plates) before placement of the vertical steel structure at ground level and level to the correct elevation. 
   - 於地面放置垂直鋼結構前，須先安裝底板下之填隙片，並校正至正確高程。

   - Before lifting verify that hand railing and grating is not loose, but all tightened. 
   - 起吊前須確認扶手與格柵板均已緊固，無鬆脫情形。

   - Shims used for levelling of the columns shall be under the base plate and not protrude. 
   - 用於鋼柱水平調整之填隙片須置於底板下方，且不得外露。

   - - Tightening of secondary steel parts to take place according the work method statement. 
   - - 次要鋼結構構件之緊固作業須依據施工計畫書進行。

   - During pre-assembly check the piece marks on the secondary steel for correctness. 
   - 預組裝期間須核對次要鋼構之構件標示，以確保正確性。

   - - During pre-assembly check position and alignment of the columns and beams. - Erection to be executed in manageable components which are still easily manipulated during erection. Where required and possible, include stairs, platforms, hand railing and gratings. 
   - - 預組裝期間須檢查鋼柱與鋼樑之位置與直線度。- 吊裝作業應以易於操控之構件尺寸進行。於必要且可行情況下，應包含樓梯、平台、扶手及格柵板。

   - - Apply the correct torque value for bolt tightening. - Splices in bolted connections are not permitted, except as shown on drawing. - Use the correct bolt material and length, according the applicable bolt list. - When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
   - - 螺栓緊固須使用正確扭矩值。- 螺栓接合處不得擅自變更接頭形式，除非圖面另有標示。- 應依照適用之螺栓清單，選用正確之螺栓材質與長度。- 若發現螺栓孔位偏移，須經諮詢原製造廠後方可進行調整。

   - - Verify span direction of bearing bars when installing grating into the platform frames. - Touch up painting according applicable painting procedure. - Strictly follow the general notes and welding details on the drawings (if any). - Adjustment of holes with cutting torches is prohibited. 
   - - 安裝格柵板至平台框時，須確認承重扁鐵之跨距方向。- 依據適用之油漆作業程序書進行補漆。- 嚴格遵守圖面上之一般註解與銲接細節（如有）。- 禁止使用氣銲切割方式調整螺栓孔。

- Welding of temporary devices is prohibited. 
- 禁止銲接任何臨時性設備。

- • Deviations on branch points (if any) _Note:_ 
- • 分支點之偏差（若有）_備註：_

- Connection beam to short: Maximum deviations up to - 5mm and must be compensated with shims. Only one shim fitting the actual gap is permitted. If a deviation is over 5 mm, shims must be used on both sides. 
- 連接樑過短：最大偏差值達 -5mm 以內時，必須使用填隙片進行補償。僅允許使用單一片填隙片以符合實際間隙。若偏差大於 5mm，則必須於兩側同時使用填隙片。

- Connection beam too long: In case the connection beam is too long the flange plate must be cut off, after removal the length of the beam can be corrected to the required length and the flange plate welded on again. 
- 連接樑過長：若連接樑過長，則必須切除法蘭板；拆除後，將樑長度修正至所需尺寸，並將法蘭板重新銲接。

- Flange plate is distorted: 
- 法蘭板變形：

If the flange is distorted, the flange plate must be cut off, corrected and welded on again. 
若法蘭變形，則必須切除法蘭板，進行校正後再重新銲接。

- Gap and flatness of the flange plates: 
- 法蘭板間隙與平整度：

If respective gap is bigger than 5 mm or the angle of the flange is incorrect, the flange must be cut off, corrected and welded on again. 
若相關間隙大於 5mm 或法蘭角度不正確，則必須切除法蘭，進行校正後再重新銲接。

- Welding of secondary steel components. 
- 二次鋼構件之銲接。

   - _Note:_ 
   - _備註：_

      - For welding follow the details and typical on the drawings and WPS. 
      - 有關銲接作業，請遵循圖說與銲接程序規範 (WPS) 之細部說明及典型圖。

#### Quality control 工地品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ _備註：_

- Check fit-up before welding (if any). 
- 銲接前檢查組裝狀況（若有）。

- Check torque of bolted connections 
- 檢查螺栓接頭之鎖緊扭力。

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 釋出時須附上待辦事項清單（若有）。

## 14.4. Grouting secondary steel 二次鋼構之無收縮水泥灌漿

Grouting for secondary steel parts is based on the Chapter 7.2 “ _Grouting_ ” in this manual. Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution. 
二次鋼構件之無收縮水泥灌漿作業係依據本手冊第 7.2 章「灌漿」之規定。執行時請遵循該章節中所述之安裝與品質步驟。

## 14.5. Final inspection of secondary steel (and hoisting beams) 二次鋼構（及起吊樑）之最終檢驗

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Final Inspection Certificate. Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the erection activities. 
當特定系統或一組特定組件之機械安裝作業完成後，應進行檢驗。待辦事項應彙整列入待辦事項清單中。待辦事項清單可附於最終檢驗證明書之後。該證明書係作為安裝活動圓滿完成之紀錄。

The Final Inspection Certificate for secondary steel describes the systems or components inspected. 
二次鋼構之最終檢驗證明書應載明受檢之系統或組件。

By signing the Final Inspection Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to either identify the points remaining before the system can be handed over to Commissioning, or in absence of any of such points hand over the system to Commissioning directly. 
相關各方透過簽署最終檢驗證明書，確認所指之系統或組件安裝進度已達足夠程度，足以辨識在系統移交試運轉前所需完成之剩餘項目；若無任何剩餘項目，則可直接將系統移交予試運轉單位。

#### Inspection 檢驗

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages. 
- 所有於最終檢查證書中所列之系統或特定組件群組，均應進行最終檢查，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢結束後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（如有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in: 
- 若適用待辦事項清單，應將其分類如下：

   - Items to be solved before hydro testing. (A-items) 
   - 水壓試驗前須解決之事項。（A類事項）

   - - Items to be solved before commissioning. (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance. (C-items) 
   - - 試運轉前須解決之事項。（B類事項）- 暫定驗收前須解決之事項。（C類事項）

#### _Note:_  註：

- Verify that the applicable FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認相關系統之施工品質計畫 已由各參與單位簽署。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports (NCR’s) are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認所有不符合報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。待辦事項應納入待辦事項清單中。

# 15. PIPING 15. 管路工程

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列段落：

# 1. General 1. 一般規定

2. General :  paragraph 15.1 2. Documents and procedure :  paragraph 15.2 3. Large bore piping :  paragraph 15.3 4. Small bore piping :  paragraph 15.4 5. Grouting pipe supports :  paragraph 15.5 6. Final inspection of piping per system :  paragraph 15.6 
2. 一般規定：第15.1節 2. 文件與程序：第15.2節 3. 大口徑管路：第15.3節 4. 小口徑管路：第15.4節 5. 管支撐無收縮水泥灌漿：第15.5節 6. 各系統管路之最終檢查：第15.6節

## 15.1. General 15.1. 一般規定

Piping (spools) erection is based on the requirements by the applicable construction code and project specifications for the pressure parts erection of the HRSG. 
管路（管件模組）之安裝係依據適用之施工規範及餘熱鍋爐 (HRSG) 受壓組件安裝之工程規範要求進行。

All work executed on site shall be of first class and good workmanship. The erection contractor shall adhere to all requirements and regulations applicable and ensure that work execution complies with local law and regulations. 
所有現場施作工程應具備一流且優良之施工品質。安裝承包商應恪遵所有適用之要求與法規，並確保施工過程符合當地法令規章。

Welding of grade 91/92 is a quality sensitive activity. The following Manufacturer specification for welding of grade 91/92 materials has to be followed: “ _IKZ09-909-14 Instruction for fabrication and supply of grade 91 materials_ ”, as attached in document 60031-409-10. Not following the right procedures and requirements might lead to quality issues. 
Grade 91/92 材質之銲接作業為品質敏感活動。必須遵循下列製造商對於 Grade 91/92 材質之銲接規範：「_IKZ09-909-14 Grade 91 材質之製造與供應說明_」（如文件 60031-409-10 所附）。未遵守正確程序與要求可能導致品質問題。

For the piping erection it is important to follow the requirements as mentioned in the standard specification site installation. Some topics of this specification are emphasized in the notes for installation or the paragraphs. 
進行管路安裝時，務必遵循標準施工規範中所述之要求。該規範中部分要點已於安裝注意事項或相關章節中強調。

It is a strong recommendation to erect the large bore piping and small bore piping per box (top and bottom) and per hydro testing system for the external piping. 
強烈建議大口徑與小口徑管路之安裝應按區塊（頂部與底部）進行，外接管路則應按水壓試驗系統劃分進行安裝。

In order to enable initiation of the remaining erection activities for a box, like baffles, sealing plates and mechanical completion walk downs, it is important to finish the erection of the piping per box. 
為利於後續各區塊安裝作業（如導流板、密封板及機械完工現場步檢）之啟動，完成各區塊之管路安裝至關重要。

#### _Note: Important for the erection of the pressure parts:_  註：受壓組件安裝之重要事項：

- Control of incoming materials to be recorded according the MRR with OSD (if any). 
- 進場材料之管制應依據材料驗收報告 (MRR) 並紀錄貨損報告 (OSD)（如有）。

- Use the HTT isometric legend standard as information for piping erection. 
- 應使用 HTT 等角圖圖例標準作為管路安裝之資訊參考。

- Execute NDE works as per applicable code and project specific requirements. 
- 應依據適用法規及專案特定要求執行非破壞檢測 (NDE) 作業。

- For local heat treatment of piping butt joints, branch and nozzle connections with recording thermocouples, follow the figures as given in the applicable construction code and project specifications. 
- 針對管路對接銲道、支管及噴嘴連接處之局部熱處理，應使用記錄型熱電偶，並遵循適用施工規範及專案規格書中之圖示進行。

Work method statements / risk assessments with lifting plans for the installation of tanks / skids shall be prepared by the erection contractor. The erection sequence for piping is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
- 儲槽與撬裝模組 (Skids) 安裝之施工計畫書/風險評估及吊裝計畫應由安裝承攬商負責編撰。管路安裝順序請參閱文件 60031-730-05-001。

## 15.2. Documents and procedures 文件與程序書

Documents and procedures required for installation of piping . 
- 管路安裝所需之文件與程序書。

- Work method statement :  Erection piping 
- - 施工計畫書：管路安裝

- - FQP :  HRSG Piping - Bolt torque procedure :  Pressure parts - WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Pressure parts - LISL’s :  Pressure parts - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Pressure parts - PWHT procedure :  Pressure parts - Hardness testing procedure :  Pressure parts - Welding consumable handling procedure :  Pressure parts - Welder qualification procedure :  Pressure parts - Re-stamping materials procedure :  Pressure parts - Material cleanness procedure :  Pressure parts - WPS / PQR / WPQ :  Non-pressure parts - Weld typical / record :  Non-pressure parts - Welding consumable handling procedure :  Non-pressure parts - NDE procedures / personnel qualifications :  Non-pressure parts 
- - 施工品質計畫：熱回收鍋爐 (HRSG) 管路 - 螺栓扭力程序：受壓組件 - 銲接程序規範/銲接程序檢定紀錄/銲工檢定紀錄 (WPS/PQR/WPQ)：受壓組件 - 檢驗清單 (LISL’s)：受壓組件 - 非破壞檢測程序/人員資格：受壓組件 - 銲後熱處理 (PWHT) 程序：受壓組件 - 硬度試驗程序：受壓組件 - 銲材管理程序：受壓組件 - 銲工檢定程序：受壓組件 - 材料鋼印重刻程序：受壓組件 - 材料清潔程序：受壓組件 - 銲接程序規範/銲接程序檢定紀錄/銲工檢定紀錄 (WPS/PQR/WPQ)：非受壓組件 - 銲接典型圖/紀錄：非受壓組件 - 銲材管理程序：非受壓組件 - 非破壞檢測程序/人員資格：非受壓組件

## 15.3. Large bore piping 大口徑管路 

Large bore piping describes all HRSG piping, which is over 2” in size and contains a lot of piping accessories. Some examples of large bore piping accessories are: 
- 大口徑管路係指所有管徑大於 2 英吋且包含眾多管件配件之熱回收鍋爐管路。大口徑管路配件範例如下：

- Pipe supports 
- - 管支撐

- Valves 
- - 閥門

- Measurement devices 
- - 量測裝置

- Steam Silencers 
- - 蒸汽消音器

- etc. 
- - 其他

### 15.3.1. Erection large bore piping 大口徑管路安裝 

Before erection of the piping can commence some preparations need to be made in advance. 
- 管路安裝開始前，需先行進行各項準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備與前置條件 

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序書必須已備妥，並經負責單位 (或人員) 審查核可。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並依適用狀況於施工品質計畫 中簽核。

      - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
      - - 材料已收受並完成數量與品質檢核 (OSD 報告)

      - Harps / drums installed 
      - - 管排 (Harps) / 汽鼓 (Drums) 已完成安裝

- Prepare piping, accessories, appendages and pipe supports according the isometrics for the erection. 
- 依據施工用等長圖 (Isometric drawings) 準備管路、配件、附屬元件及管支撐進行安裝。

- Prepare metal expansion bellows for the erection (during temporary erection of piping). 
- 準備金屬波紋伸縮接頭以進行安裝 (於管路臨時安裝期間)。

- _Note:_ 
   - _註：_

      - Fabric expansion bellow erection after Final inspection of piping. 
      - 織布式波紋伸縮接頭應於管路最終檢驗後進行安裝。

- Installation of skids and rotating equipment (if any). 
- 安裝橇塊及旋轉設備（若有）。

- Prepare secondary steel or scaffolding for the erection. 
- 準備安裝所需之二次鋼構或施工架。

- Prepare temporary supporting. 
- 準備臨時支撐。

- Prepare correct tools and equipment. 
- 準備正確之工具與設備。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Prepare all necessary equipment and tools for the erection. 
- 準備安裝所需之所有必要設備與工具。

- Verify piping (spools), accessories, appendages and pipe supports for correct numbering, labelling (nameplates), flow direction and dimensions. 
- 確認管路（預製管段）、配件、附屬件及管架之編號、標籤（銘牌）、流向及尺寸是否正確。

- In order to protect the weld area from weather influences, cover the area in case required. 
- 為保護銲道區域免受氣候影響，必要時請將該區域遮蔽。

- Do not forget to erect the expansion joints during erection together with the piping (only applicable in case of metallic bellows, or prefabricated fabric bellows). 
- 於管路安裝期間，切勿遺漏安裝伸縮接頭（僅適用於金屬波紋管或預製織布式波紋管之情況）。

- Similarly, do not forget to erect the insulation donuts and penetration covers, before piping installation, as these are delivered as 1 piece. 
- 同樣地，由於保溫環及穿牆保護罩係以一體式交付，務必於管路安裝前先行裝設。

- In case of any deviation regarding piping (spools) contact the manufacturer. 
- 若管路（預製管段）有任何偏差，請聯繫製造廠。

#### Release subsequent activities 後續作業放行

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - Hydrotesting. 
- 本段落作業順利完成後，即放行下列作業：- 水壓試驗。

   - Erection fabric expansion bellows. 
   - 織布式波紋伸縮接頭安裝。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- Erect and fit piping with accessories per system. 
- 依據系統安裝並組裝管路及其配件。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Starting points for erection of external large bore piping are system “fixed points”, like already installed main headers, harps or tanks and vessels. 
- 外部大口徑管路之安裝起點應為系統之「固定點」，例如已安裝完成之主聯箱、管束模組或槽桶與容器。

- All piping accessories to be installed as per the relevant supplier installation instructions. 
- 所有管路配件均須依據相關供應商之安裝說明書進行安裝。

- Piping and piping accessories shall be kept clean and free from dirt or debris during pre-assembly. In case possible keep components capped. 
- 管路及管路配件於預組裝期間應保持清潔，不得有髒污或雜物。在可行情況下，請將組件開口加蓋密封。

- During erection (welding and PWHT) of piping accessories follow the relevant supplier installation instructions. Especially focus on the required open/close position of valves during installation. 
- 於管線配件安裝期間（銲接及焊後熱處理 PWHT），應遵循相關供應商之安裝說明書。安裝過程中，請特別留意閥門所需之開/關狀態。

   - Align flanges free of stress at all time. Use the correct gasket and apply the appropriate bolt tightening values. 
   - 法蘭對接時應確保全程無應力狀態。使用正確之密封墊片，並依規定之螺栓鎖固扭矩值進行施工。

   - Use the appropriate lubricant for bolted connections and apply torque values as mentioned in the bolt tightening specification “60031-400-20 “Bolt torque procedure flanged connections”. 
   - 螺栓連接處應使用適當之潤滑劑，並依照「60031-400-20 法蘭連接螺栓鎖固程序」規範之扭矩值進行施工。

   - Verify piping slope during erection. 
   - 施工期間應確實檢核管線坡度。

   - In case of tolerances deviating more than the allowable tolerances specified, contact the manufacturer. 
   - 若施工誤差超出規範容許範圍，應聯繫原製造廠商。

   - Fit the final supports to the correct position and location. 
   - 將最終支撐件安裝至正確之位置與點位。

   - Drawings of completed lines shall be made as-built, where required. 
   - 若有要求，已完工之管線圖說應繪製成竣工圖 (As-built drawings)。

- Quality control on tack-welded fit-ups: 
- 點銲組裝之品質管制：

#### _Note:_ 備註：

   - Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings / WPS. 
   - 應遵循圖說或銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中關於銲接之細節或典型做法。

   - Temporary welded attachments shall be of a compatible chemical composition as the permanent material. 
   - 臨時銲接之附屬構件，其化學成分必須與永久母材相容。

   - Fit-ups to be checked, before welding. 
   - 銲接前應確實檢查組裝 (Fit-up) 狀況。

- Welding: 
- 銲接作業：

#### _Note:_ 備註：

- Follow the details and or typical for welding on the drawings / WPS. 
- 應遵循圖說或銲接程序規範 (WPS) 中關於銲接之細節或典型做法。

- During welding and PWHT of piping accessories follow the relevant supplier installation instructions. Especially focus on the required open/close position of valves during installation. 
- 於管線配件銲接及焊後熱處理 (PWHT) 期間，應遵循相關供應商之安裝說明書。安裝過程中，請特別留意閥門所需之開/關狀態。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依照適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關程序書執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 備註：

- Release with a list of outstanding items (if any). 
- 若有任何未結項目，應列出清單並辦理放行。

- Erection contractor to draw-up as-built P&ID’s and isometrics upon piping completion per system. 
- 安裝承攬商應於各系統管線安裝完成後，繪製竣工管線儀表流程圖 (P&ID) 及管線單線圖 (Isometrics)。

## 15.4. Small bore piping 小口徑管線 

Piping 2 inch and smaller is covered by the categories small bore. Small bore piping is supplied as loose items. 
- 管徑 2 英吋及以下之管線歸類為小口徑管線。小口徑管線係以散裝件方式供應。

Routing of small bore piping is subject to final dimension check at site. However, overall geometry as shown on the isometric shall be maintained due to expansion requirements. Actual routing at site to be verified against the routing on the small bore isometrics; 10% deviation in each direction is allowed (unless otherwise specified on the isometric). 
小口徑管路的佈設須於現場進行最終尺寸確認。惟受限於熱膨脹要求，等長管線圖 (isometric) 上所示之整體幾何形狀必須維持。現場實際佈設需與小口徑等長管線圖進行校對；在各方向允許 10% 的偏差值 (除非等長管線圖另有特別說明)。

Possibilities for pre-assembly of small bore piping depend on the situation at the construction site, like space for pre-assembly, availability of cranes, potential rework and access at the installation location. As mentioned before, properly coordinate which parts will be preassembled with all involved parties. 
小口徑管路預組裝的可行性取決於工地現場狀況，例如預組裝空間、吊車可用性、潛在的重工需求以及安裝位置的進入性。如前所述，應與所有相關單位妥善協調預組裝的工項內容。

Small bore pipe supports are show as typicals on the isometrics and related to typical small bore pipe support documents unless otherwise noted. 
除非另有註明，小口徑管支撐在等長管線圖上顯示為典型細節，並對應相關之典型小口徑管支撐文件。

### 15.4.1. Small bore piping erection 小口徑管路安裝工程

Small bore piping installation steps and requirements are equal to and based on the paragraph  “Large bore piping” . Follow the installation and quality steps mentioned in that paragraph  for installation of small bore piping. 
小口徑管路的安裝步驟與要求與「大口徑管路」章節所述相同且以此為基礎。執行小口徑管路安裝時，請遵循該章節所提及之安裝與品質步驟。

In addition the following small bore piping specific requirements are to be taken into account. 
此外，必須考量以下小口徑管路之特別要求。

#### Installation 安裝作業

- Erect and fit piping (spools) with accessories per system. 
- 依據系統進行管路 (管件) 及其附屬組件的吊裝與安裝。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Routing of field run piping is to be actually verified on site in order to ensure sufficient space for insulation, expansion and convenient operation of small-bore appendages and sufficient space for maintenance. Handles and hand wheels shall be orientated for operator convenience. 
- 現場佈設管路之路線須於現場實際驗證，以確保有足夠的空間進行保溫、膨脹預留，並利於小口徑附屬裝置的操作及維護作業。閥柄與手輪之朝向應考量操作便利性。

- Socket connections shall have a gap of 2mm between the pipe end and the bottom of the socket. 
- 插焊式管接頭之管端與承口底部間應保留 2mm 間隙。

## 15.5. Grouting pipe supports 管支撐無收縮水泥灌漿

Grouting of pipe supports is based on the Chapter 7.2 “ _Grouting_ ” in this manual. Follow the erection and quality steps mentioned in this chapter during execution. 
管支撐之無收縮水泥灌漿係依據本手冊第 7.2 章「無收縮水泥灌漿」辦理。執行時，請遵循該章節所提及之安裝與品質步驟。

## 15.6. Final inspection of piping per system 各系統管路最終檢驗

When the mechanical installation of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list. The outstanding items list can be attached to a Mechanical Completion Certificate. Such certificate serves as a record for proper completion of the installation activities. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝完成時，應進行檢驗。遺留事項應彙整於遺留事項清單中。該遺留事項清單可附於機械完工證明書。此證明書作為安裝作業妥善完成之紀錄。

The Mechanical Completion Certificate for piping per system describes the systems or components inspected. 
各系統管路之機械完工證明書應詳述受檢之系統或組件。

By signing the Mechanical Completion Certificate the parties involved confirm that the system or components referred to are in a sufficiently advanced stage of installation to hand-over to Commissioning. 
簽署機械完工證明書即代表各相關方確認上述系統或組件已安裝至足夠程度，可移交至試運轉階段。

- a. Walk-down 現場步檢

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Mechanical Completion Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct installation, completeness and damages. 
- 所有機械完工證明書上所列之系統或特定組件群，均須進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) will be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢結束後，將立即建立遺留事項紀錄 (若有)。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in: 
- 若適用遺留事項清單，應分類如下：

|-|Items to be solved before hydro testing.|(A-items)|
|---|---|---|
|-|水壓試驗前須解決之項目。|(A類項目)|

|-|Items to be solved before commissioning.|(B-items)|
|-|於試運轉前須解決之項目。|(B-items)|
|-|Items to be solved before provisional acceptance.|(C-items)|
|-|於暫時驗收前須解決之項目。|(C-items)|

#### _Note:_  _註：_

- Verify that the applicable FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認相關系統之施工品質計畫 已由所有相關方簽署核准。未完成項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports (NCR’s) are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認所有不符合事項報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。未完成項目應納入待辦事項清單中。

- Check for lists of outstanding items made in earlier stages. 
- 檢查前期階段所列之待辦事項清單。

# 16. EXPANSION JOINTS 伸縮接頭

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列各節：

# 1. General 1. 一般規定

# 2. Documents and procedures 2. 文件與程序

# 3. Fabric expansion bellow inlet duct 3. 進風道纖維伸縮接頭

# 4. Fabric expansion bellow outlet duct 4. 出風道纖維伸縮接頭

- : paragraph 16.1 : paragraph 16.2 : paragraph 16.3 : paragraph 16.4 : paragraph 16.5 : paragraph 16.6 
- ：第 16.1 節 ：第 16.2 節 ：第 16.3 節 ：第 16.4 節 ：第 16.5 節 ：第 16.6 節 

## 16.1. General 16.1. 一般規定

Work method statements / risk assessments for erection of expansion joints shall be prepared by the erection contractor. The erection sequence for expansion joints is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
伸縮接頭安裝作業之施工計畫書 / 風險評估應由安裝承攬商編製。伸縮接頭之安裝順序詳見文件編號 60031-730-05-001。

## 16.2. Documents and procedures 16.2. 文件與程序

Documents and procedures required for erection of the expansion joints . 
伸縮接頭安裝所需之文件與程序。

- Supplier erection manual 
- 供應商安裝手冊

- FQP 
- 施工品質計畫

- WPS / PQR / WPQ 
- 銲接程序規範 (WPS) / 銲接程序評定紀錄 (PQR) / 銲接人員資格檢定紀錄 (WPQ)

- Weld typical / record 
- 典型銲道 / 銲接紀錄

- Welding consumable handling procedure 
- 銲接材料管理程序

- NDE procedures / personnel qualifications 
- 非破壞檢測 (NDE) 程序 / 人員資格認證

- :  Expansion joints 
- :  波紋伸縮接頭

## 16.3. Fabric expansion bellow inlet duct 入口煙道織布式波紋伸縮接頭

Before erection of the inlet duct expansion bellow can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始安裝入口煙道波紋伸縮接頭之前，必須預先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備作業與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序必須備妥，並經責任方（或各方）審查完畢。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認（若適用）。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（OSD 開箱檢驗報告）。

   - erection bellow flanges completed 
   - 已完成波紋伸縮接頭法蘭安裝。

   - Verification for absence of sharp edges at bellow connecting surfaces 
   - 確認波紋伸縮接頭連接面無銳利邊緣。

#### Erection 安裝作業

- The erection for the expansion joint is described in the relevant supplier installation manual. 
- 波紋伸縮接頭之安裝說明請參照相關供應商安裝手冊。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- It is highly recommended to order a specialist of the supplier for the supervision of the erection of the expansion joints as this is complex work, with minimum room for error and with reference to possible warranty issues later on. 
- 強烈建議聘請供應商專業技術人員至現場督導波紋伸縮接頭之安裝，因該項作業複雜、容錯率低，且涉及後續保固責任問題。

   - Pre-order such specialist in time in order not to delay works. 
   - 應提前預訂此類專業人員，以免延誤施工進度。

- Have a specific crew trained in the erection and do not rotate personnel as knowledge gained about the erection will be lost. 
- 指定專責安裝團隊進行培訓，且切勿隨意更換人員，以免施工經驗與技術傳承流失。

- Follow the instructions of the supplier for erection of the expansion joints. 
- 安裝波紋伸縮接頭時，務必遵循供應商之指示。

- Use the correct gasket and apply the appropriate bolt tightening values. 
- 請使用正確的密封墊片，並施加合適的螺栓鎖緊扭力值。

- When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer. 
- 當檢測到螺栓孔錯位時，僅能在諮詢原廠後方可進行調整。

- TAKE CARE TO USE SUFFICIENT INSULATION MATERIAL AS FAILING TO DO SO WILL LEAD TO HOT SPOTS AND BURNING OF THE BELLOW, ONCE IN OPERATION. 
- 請務必使用充足的保溫隔熱棉，若未落實將導致運轉時產生熱點並燒毀波紋伸縮接頭。

#### Quality control 品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 應依照適用的施工品質計畫 及/或作業程序執行品質管制工作。

#### _Note:_ 註：
   - Release without a list of outstanding items. 
   - 須在無任何未決事項清單之情況下進行放行。

   - After erection completion cover the top side of the expansion joint with weld blankets or other spark/dirt protection. This to avoid any damage by welding or other work activities. Keep the protection in place till the end of the construction works. 
   - 安裝完成後，請使用銲接防火毯或其他防火花/防污覆蓋物遮蓋波紋伸縮接頭頂部。此舉旨在避免銲接或其他施工作業造成損傷。在工程結束前，應保持該防護措施原狀。

- 16.4. Fabric expansion bellow outlet duct 16.4. 出口煙道織布式波紋伸縮接頭
Before erection of the outlet duct expansion bellow can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在開始出口煙道波紋伸縮接頭的安裝作業前，需預先準備部分工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties). 
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序必須準備就緒，並由權責單位（或多方權責單位）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP. 
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認（如適用）。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report) 
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（開箱檢驗報告 OSD Report）。

   - erection bellow flanges completed (casing and outlet duct side) 
   - 已完成波紋伸縮接頭法蘭安裝（含爐牆外殼板側與出口煙道側）。

   - Verification for absence of sharp edges at bellow connecting surfaces 
   - 確認波紋伸縮接頭連接表面無銳利邊緣。

#### Erection 安裝
- The erection for the expansion joint is described in the relevant supplier erection manual. 
- 波紋伸縮接頭之安裝方式詳述於相關供應商安裝手冊中。

#### _Note:_ 註：
- It is highly recommended to order a specialist of the supplier for the supervision of the erection of the expansion joints as this is complex work, with minimum room for error and with reference to possible warranty issues later on. 
- 強烈建議聘請供應商之專業技術人員現場督導波紋伸縮接頭之安裝作業，因該項作業複雜、容錯率極低，且涉及後續保固責任問題。

Pre-order such specialist in time in order not to delay works. 
請務必提前預約該技術人員，以免延誤施工進度。

- Have a specific crew trained in the erection and do not rotate personnel as knowledge gained about the erection will be lost.
- 應指派經過安裝訓練的專屬施工班組，切勿隨意調換人員，以免安裝過程中積累的技術經驗流失。

- Follow the instructions of the supplier for erection of the expansion joints.
- 關於波紋伸縮接頭的安裝，請遵循供應商之安裝說明書辦理。

- Use the correct gasket and apply the appropriate bolt tightening values.
- 務必使用正確的密封墊片，並依照規範的螺栓扭力值進行鎖緊作業。

- When a misalignment of bolt holes is detected, adjustment can be made only after consultation with the manufacturer.
- 當發現螺栓孔位偏移時，必須在與原廠諮詢確認後，方可進行調整。

- TAKE CARE TO USE SUFFICIENT INSULATION MATERIAL AS FAILING TO DO SO WILL LEAD TO HOT SPOTS AND BURNING OF THE BELLOW, ONCE IN OPERATION.
- 請務必確保使用足夠的保溫隔熱棉，若保溫不足，運轉時將導致局部過熱點並燒毀波紋管。

#### Quality control 品質管制
- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s).
- 應依據適用的施工品質計畫 及相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：
- Release without a list of outstanding items.
- 在無遺留缺失清單的狀態下放行。

- After erection completion cover the top side of the expansion joint with weld blankets or other spark/dirt protection. This to avoid any damage by welding or other work activities. Keep the protection in place till the end of the construction works
- 安裝完成後，請使用銲接防火毯或其他防護措施覆蓋波紋伸縮接頭頂部，以避免銲接或其他施工作業造成損壞。相關防護措施應持續保留至施工工程結束為止。

## 16.5. Expansion bellows pipe casing penetrations 16.5. 爐牆外殼板管道貫穿處之波紋伸縮接頭
The expansion bellows for the pipe casing penetrations consist of two (2) types:
爐牆外殼板管道貫穿處所使用的波紋伸縮接頭分為兩 (2) 種類型：

- Metal expansion bellows for top casing penetrations.
- 用於頂部爐牆外殼板貫穿處的金屬波紋伸縮接頭。

- Fabric expansion joints for bottom casing penetrations.
- 用於底部爐牆外殼板貫穿處的織物型伸縮接頭。

Before erection of the expansion bellows for pipe casing penetrations can commence, some activities need to be prepared in advance.
在進行爐牆外殼板管道貫穿處波紋伸縮接頭的安裝作業前，需先完成相關準備工作。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件
- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與作業程序應備齊，並由權責單位（或人員）完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動必須完成，並在適用時需於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Materials received and surveyed for quantity and quality (OSD report)
   - 材料已進場並完成數量與品質檢驗（含開箱檢驗報告 OSD Report）。

   - Pipe penetration locations accepted
   - 管道貫穿處位置已檢驗合格。

- Prior to start the erection of the expansion bellows for the pipe penetrations, some items need to be verified in advance:
- 在開始管道貫穿處波紋伸縮接頭的安裝前，需預先確認下列事項：

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Verify each pipe to penetrate the casing at the location as indicated on the drawings. This is very important as not having the pipe located in the right position might lead to damages and/or hotspots during hot conditions. 
- 確認每一根貫穿爐牆外殼板之管路位置，皆須符合施工圖說。此點至關重要，若管路位置偏差，可能導致運轉時產生損壞及/或局部過熱點。

In case of unacceptable dislocation of a pipe penetration adjust the casing cut out using “half-moons”. 
若管路貫穿處之位移超出容許範圍，須使用「半月板」補件調整爐牆外殼板之開孔。

- Erect the bellow connection flanges as per the drawing tolerances. Correctly sizing the distance between the flanges and aligning the flange bolt hole patterns is of utmost importance. 
- 依照圖說公差安裝波紋伸縮接頭之連接法蘭。正確量測法蘭間距並對正法蘭螺栓孔位至關重要。

#### Installation 安裝作業

- For erection follow the expansion bellow supplier erection instructions. Note: 
- 有關安裝作業，請遵循波紋伸縮接頭供應商之安裝說明書。注意：

   - It is highly recommended to order a specialist of the supplier for the supervision of the erection of the expansion joints as this is complex work, with minimum room for error and with reference to possible warranty issues later on. 
   - 強烈建議聘請供應商之技術專家至現場督導波紋伸縮接頭之安裝，此作業複雜度高、容許誤差極小，且涉及後續保固相關事宜。

Pre-order such specialist in time in order not to delay works. 
請提早預訂該技術專家，以免延誤施工進度。

- Have a specific crew trained in the erection and do not rotate personnel as knowledge gained about the erection will be lost. 
- 指派經受訓之專門施工班組負責安裝，並避免人員頻繁更動，以免安裝經驗與技術傳承中斷。

- Follow the instructions of the supplier (supervisor) for erection of the expansion joints. 
- 執行波紋伸縮接頭安裝時，應遵從供應商（督導人員）之指示。

- Use the correct gasket and apply the appropriate bolt tightening values. 
- 使用正確規格之密封墊片，並依照規定之扭力值鎖緊螺栓。

- TAKE CARE TO USE SUFFICIENT INSULATION MATERIAL AS FAILING TO DO SO WILL LEAD TO HOT SPOTS AND BURNING OF THE BELLOW, ONCE IN OPERATION. 
- 請務必使用足量之保溫隔熱棉，若保溫不足，將導致機組運轉時產生局部過熱點並燒毀波紋管。

#### Quality control 品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per applicable FQP and/or procedure(s). 
- 依據適用之施工品質計畫 及/或相關作業程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Release without a list of outstanding items. 
- 發布時應確保無遺留待辦事項。

## 16.6. Final inspection expansion joints 波紋伸縮接頭最終檢驗

When the mechanical erection of a certain system, or group of specific components is finalized these shall be inspected. 
當特定系統或特定組件群之機械安裝作業完成後，應進行檢驗。

Outstanding items shall be collected in an outstanding items list and attached to the Final inspection Certificate. 
所有遺留待辦事項應彙整列入待辦事項清單，並附於最終檢驗證書後。

Final inspection for the boiler part is mainly covered by the boiler casing, because all other boiler parts have a separate final inspection round. 
鍋爐部分之最終檢驗主要涵蓋爐牆外殼板，因其他鍋爐組件皆有獨立之最終檢驗程序。

The Final inspection Certificate of the expansion joints describes the systems or components inspected. 
波紋伸縮接頭之最終檢驗證書應載明所檢驗之系統或組件。

#### Inspection 檢驗作業

- All systems or group of specific components referred to on the Final inspection Certificate shall have a final inspection for correct erection, completeness and damages. 
- 所有最終檢驗證明書中所提及之系統或特定組件群組，應進行最終檢驗，以確認安裝正確性、完整性及有無損壞。

- A record of outstanding items (if any) shall be set-up directly after the walk-down. 
- 現場步檢完成後，應立即建立待辦事項紀錄（若有）。

- In case a list of outstanding items is applicable it shall be categorized in : 
- 若適用待辦事項清單，應分類如下：

- Items to be solved before hydro testing (A-items) - Items to be solved before hot-commissioning (B-items) - Items to be solved before provisional acceptance (PAC) (C-items) _Note:_ 
- 水壓試驗前須解決之項目（A類項目） - 熱機試運轉前須解決之項目（B類項目） - 暫定驗收（PAC）前須解決之項目（C類項目） _註：_

- Verify that the applicable site FQPs for the systems involved are signed off by all parties involved. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認相關系統之施工品質計畫 已由所有參與方簽署。待辦事項須納入待辦事項清單中。

- Verify that all Non-Conformity Reports are closed. Outstanding items are to be included in the outstanding points list. 
- 確認所有不符合報告 (NCR) 皆已結案。待辦事項須納入待辦事項清單中。

# 17. HYDROTESTING 水壓試驗
This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列段落：

# 1. General 1. 一般規定

# 2. Documents and procedures 2. 文件與程序

# 3. Pressure testing 3. 壓力測試

- :  paragraph 17.1 :  paragraph 17.2 :  paragraph 17.3 
- ： 17.1 節 ： 17.2 節 ： 17.3 節

## 17.1. General 17.1. 一般規定
HRSG hydrostatic and pneumatic pressure testing is divided into several systems. Testing is based on testing procedure 60031-735-01 “ _Hydro testing_ ”. 
HRSG 水壓及氣壓測試分為數個系統進行。測試依據測試程序 60031-735-01 「水壓試驗」執行。

For each system a separate test shall be performed. The pressure test scope is indicated on the hydro test schedules. 
每一系統均應進行個別測試。壓力測試範圍標示於水壓試驗進度表中。

The erection sequence for hydro testing is shown in document 60031-730-05-001. 
水壓試驗之安裝順序詳見文件 60031-730-05-001。

- 17.2. Documents and procedures - 17.2. 文件與程序

   - Documents and procedures required for hydrotesting . - Work method statement - Work method statement 
   - 水壓試驗所需文件與程序。 - 施工方法說明書 - 施工方法說明書

   - :  Hydro testing procedure 
   - ： 水壓試驗程序

   - :  Pneumatic testing procedure (if applicable) 
   - ： 氣壓測試程序（若適用）

- System test package :  Completed QC documentation for system 
- 系統測試包 ： 系統已完成之品質管制文件

- - System test package :  Affected component list 
- - 系統測試包 ： 受影響組件清單

## 17.3. Pressure testing 17.3. 壓力測試
Before pressure testing (hydrostatic or pneumatic) can commence some activities need to be prepared in advance. 
在壓力測試（水壓或氣壓）開始前，須預先準備相關作業。

#### Preparations and preconditions 準備工作與先決條件

- The documents and procedures mentioned in previous paragraph need to be in place and reviewed by the responsible party (or parties).
- 前述段落提及之文件與程序須到位，並由權責單位完成審查。

- The following preparations/activities need to have been completed and if applicable signed-off in the FQP.
- 下列準備工作/活動須已完成，並依適用情形於施工品質計畫 中完成簽認。

   - Release Authorized Inspector for hydrostatic testing applicable system 
   - 釋出適用系統之水壓試驗授權檢驗員。

- The erection contractor shall prepare a test package for the hydrostatic testing per system, in advance.
- 安裝承攬商應針對各系統提前準備水壓試驗包 (Test package)。

- Prepare the systems for hydrostatic testing.
- 完成水壓試驗之系統準備作業。

#### _Note:_ _註：_

   - Test package should contain as minimum a cover page, table of contents, record of hydrostatic test, test procedure, ITPs, mechanical completion certificate with list of outstanding items (if any), hydro test schedules, isometric with supports (as built drawings), drawing of arrangement for the equipment, LISL’s, line list, valve list and all relevant NDE reports.
   - 水壓試驗包內容至少應包含：封面、目錄、水壓試驗紀錄、試驗程序書、檢驗計畫 (ITPs)、機械竣工證明書（含缺失項目清單，若有）、水壓試驗時程表、附支撐之管路立體圖（竣工圖）、設備配置圖、管線隔離單 (LISL)、管線清單、閥件清單，以及所有相關之非破壞檢測報告。

   - Test package shall comply with the requirements as per the applicable code and project specific requirements.
   - 水壓試驗包須符合適用法規及本專案之特定要求。

   - During the preparations carefully read the general notes on the hydro test schedules.
   - 於準備期間，須詳閱水壓試驗時程表上之一般註記。

   - Follow the requirements of the hydrostatic test procedure.
   - 遵循水壓試驗程序書之各項要求。

   - Check and prepare hydro test tools and equipment in advance.
   - 提前檢查並準備水壓試驗所需之工具與設備。

   - Submit the hydrostatic test packages in advance for document control and final walk-downs of the systems.
   - 提前提交水壓試驗包，以利文件管制與進行系統之最終現場步檢 (Walk-down)。

- Quality control 品質管制

#### _Note:_ _註：_

- Visually check the complete system and all required documentation as per code and project specific requirements.
- 依據法規及專案特定要求，對完整系統及所有規定文件進行目視檢查。

- The applicable mechanical completion certificates with a list of outstanding items (if any) shall be signed off and accepted.
- 相關之機械竣工證明書（含缺失項目清單，若有）應經簽認並驗收。

#### Release subsequent activities 釋出後續活動

- With the successful completion of the activities in this paragraph, release for the following activity (activities) is given: - External insulation.
- 本段落作業圓滿完成後，即釋出下列後續活動：- 外部保溫工程。

#### Testing 測試作業

- Perform the hydrostatic and or pneumatic testing. 
- 執行水壓及/或氣壓試驗。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Testing to be executed as per code and project specific requirements. 
- 試驗應依照規範及計畫特定要求執行。

#### Quality control client 客戶品質管制

- Perform quality control activities as per pressure testing procedure 
- 依照壓力試驗程序執行品質管制活動。

#### _Note:_ 註：

- Verify the system which is hydrostatically or pneumatically tested. 
- 確認進行水壓或氣壓試驗之系統。

- Sign-off the record for hydrostatic testing of the relevant system with all involved parties. 
- 與所有相關單位共同簽署相關系統之水壓試驗紀錄。

- TAKE CARE TO REMOVE ALL HYDROTEST PLUGS FROM THE WELDED SAFETY VALVES AFTER HYDROTESTING. TO BE EXECUTED BY A VALVE SUPPLIER SPECIALIST. 
- 務必於水壓試驗後移除銲接安全閥上之所有試驗塞。此作業須由閥門供應商專業人員執行。

# 18. ELECTRICAL AND INSTRUMENTATION 18. 電氣與儀控系統

This chapter contains the following paragraphs: 
本章包含下列各節：

1. General :  paragraph 18.1 
1. 一般事項：第 18.1 節

## 18.1. General 18.1. 一般事項

The Instrumentation of the boiler and its auxiliary parts will be erected according to the consecutive supplier installation manuals and the HTT E&I Installation manual (60028-607-08). 
鍋爐及其輔助設備之儀控系統安裝作業，應依循各設備供應商之安裝手冊及 HTT 電儀安裝手冊 (60028-607-08) 執行。

I&C cables, relevant tubing and cable tray’s must be erected between field equipment (actuators, transmitters, positioners, limit switches. E.g.) and junction boxes according to the consecutive supplier installation manuals. The junction boxes must be erected by the contractor. 
儀控電纜、相關管路及電纜橋架應依照各設備供應商之安裝手冊，安裝於現場設備（如：致動器、傳送器、定位器、極限開關等）與接線箱之間。接線箱須由承包商負責安裝。

# 19. SHROUD 19. 爐牆外殼板

Erection of the shroud is based on relevant supplier drawings, documents and installation instructions. 
爐牆外殼板之安裝作業應依據相關供應商圖說、文件及安裝說明書進行。
